jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvaliḥ
|| namo gurubhyaḥ śāstrakṛdbhyaśca ||
1. nibandhakartṛparicayaḥ
bhāratīyadārśanikeṣu jñānaśrīnāmnā prasiddhau dvāvācāryāvāstām | tayoḥ kāśmīrā-
bhijanaḥ pramāṇaviniścayavyākhyātā bhūyasāṃ bauddhaśāstragranthānāṃ bhoṭabhāṣānuvāda vidhāyako
jñānaśrībhadro'nyataraḥ, itaraśca gauḍadeśodbhavo vikramaśīlācārya: suvikhyātakītirjñāna-
śrīmitraḥ | anayodvitīyo'trādhikṛtaḥ | kutracidasya jñānaśrīnāmnā nirdeśaḥ, kutracicca
jñānaśrīmitranāmnā | svagranthapuṣkiāsu tu mahāpaṇḍitācāryajñānaśrīmitrapāda ityupādhi -
maṇḍitaṃ tasya nāmadheyamāyāti | vaṅgamagadhamaṇḍaleśvareṇa dharmapālena pratiṣṭhite tadanvavāya-
saṃbhavairupalālite ca vikramaśīlāmahāvihāre bhāratetaradeśebhyo'pi vidyārthino vividhavidyā-
•vāptaye samājagmuḥ, śāstrāṇi tu sarvāṇi bauddhapramukhānyadhigamya bahuśrutebhya ācāryebhyaste
bhāratavarṣasyādhyātmikasampadā svaṃ svaṃ deśamalaṃcakruḥ | śrūyate ekādaśe sṛṣṭaśatake vidyā-
vihāre'tra catvāro dvārapaṇḍitāḥ dvau ca mahāstambhau babhūbuburiti | jñānaśrīmitraśca teṣu
dvitīya mahāstambhapadaṃ bhūṣayāmāsa |
ādāvayaṃ jñānaśrīmitraḥ saindhavasampradāyabhuktaḥ śrāvaka āsīt tadanu ca tantra-
yānamāśritavāniti śrūyate | āsīdatra mahāvihāre saindhavānāmatiprābalyam | kadācit
tantragranthā herukapratimā ca kācit tairvahāvāhutīkṛtāḥ | rājñā ca te na daṇḍitāḥ |
eteṣu saindhaveṣu śrīmitranāmadhāriṇo janā dṛśyante | vaṅgadeśodbhavaistantrayānānusāribhire-
teṣāṃ vivāda itivṛttaviśruta eva |
bhoṭadeśīya granthebhyo jñānaśrī mitramadhikṛtyaitadanyacca vivaraṇaṃ samupalabhyate | svadeśe
viśuddhabauddhadharmapracāraṇāparāyaṇena bhoṭamahīpena hra. lā. ye. śe. od ityākhyena vikrama-
śīlācāryaṃ dīpaṅkaramatīśamāmantrayituṃ svajanāḥ preṣitāḥ | parijñāya teṣāṃ vikramaśīlā-
gamanakāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca rājopāyanādikaṃ rājasammānalābhāya vā dhanasañcayanārthaṃ vā bhoṭadeśa-
gamanaṃ na tadā svīkṛtavānācārya : | anantarametadarthaṃ punarāgatebhyo bhoṭadeśīyebhyo rājñastasya
dharmārthaṃ dhanasaṃgrahaparasya śatrubhirbaṃndhanaṃ kārāgāre jīvanāvasānaṃ ca viditvā karuṇāparavaśo
dīpaṅkaraḥ saddharmapracārāya duḥkhasaṅkalāṃ bhoṭadeśayātrāmaṅgīcakāra | ime ca bhoṭadeśīyā
nāropāntasya saṃvardhanāṃ vikramaśīlāyāṃ pratyakṣīcakruḥ | ativṛddho'yamācāryo'tīśasya dakṣiṇaṃprastāvanāṃ
jñānaśrī mitrasya ca vāmaṃ bāhumāśritya śivikāto'vatatāra | bhoṭadeśāya prasthānāt
pūrvaṃ dīpaṅkaro jñānaśrīmitrād guhyamupadeśamadhigamya tadanuṣṭhitavānityapi śrūyate |
etebhyo jñānaśrīmitrasya vikramaśīlāyāṃ maryādātirekaḥ parijñāyate |
dīpaṅkarastūnaṣaṣṭivarṣadeśīya ekacatvāriṃśadadhikaikasahasrata me khuṣṭa saṃvatsare
vasantata bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tatyāja | tatkāle jñānaśromitro'pi svīyapāṇḍityena granthanirmāṇana
ca parāṃ prakhyātimadhijagāmeti śakyānumānam |
upalabhyamānānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ pariśīlanāj jñāyate vācaspatipramukhānāṃ
naiyāyikānāṃ sandarbhāstena nāmagrāhamuddhṛtāḥ khaṇḍitāśceti | vācaspatestu nyāyasūcī-
nibandhanirmāṇakālastasyaiva svavacasā vasvaṅkavasuvatsara iti vijñāyate | paraṃ tu vatsa ro'yaṃ
vikramābdaṃ vā nirdiśati śakābdaṃ veti vipratipattisthānaṃ paṇḍitānāmāsīt | adhunā
śakasaṃvatsara eva vācaspatinollikhita iti nipuṇagaveṣaṇayā nirdhāritam |
nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāyāṃ [ 1. 1. 6. ] jarannaiyāyikasya jayantabhaṭṭasya mataṃ
vācaspatinā parāmṛṣṭamiti tātparyapariśuddhāvudayanācāryokti: | jayantaśca kāśmīrādhipasya
śaṅkaravarmaṇo'mātyapadamalaṃ cakāreti jayantakṛtādāgamaḍambaranāṭakāt parijñāyate | ayaṃ
śaṅkaravarmā sṛṣṭīyapañcāśītyadhikāṣṭaśatatamāndād prabhṛti dvayadhikanavaśatatamābdaṃ yāvat
kāśmīramahīṃ bhunakti smetītivṛttavidāṃ matam | nyāyavārtikatātparyaṭīkāpariśiṣṭabhūto
nyāyasūcīnibandhastu tadanusāraṃ na vasvaṅkavasumite vikramānde [ 8841-2 khuṣṭadhabde ]
janimarhati, paraṃ tu tatsaṃkhyakaśakasaṃvatsare [ 8976-7 vṛḥ ] iti draṣṭavyam | vācaspatinā
svagranthānāmanukramo bhāmatyāṃ pradarśitaḥ | tadanusāraṃ nyāyagranthadvitayānantaramapi tena .
tattvakaumudī tattvavaiśāradī bhāmatī ca vinirmitā iti parijñāyate | ato jñānaśrīmitreṇa
prathame vayasi ācāryasya vācaspate vidyāvibhūtiḥ pratyakṣīkṛteti vāḍhaṃ saṃbhāvyate |
jñānaśrīmitraśca svaśiṣyeṇa ratnakīrtinā sahodayanācāryakṛtiṣu khaṇḍita ityagre
pradarśanīyamasmābhiḥ | ratnakīrtiḥ svagurorgranthānāṃ sārasaṅkalanaṃ kṛtavāniti tannibandha-
bhūmikāyāṃ pradarśitam | ataevodayano'nayoḥ kanīyān samakālikaśceti saṃbhavet |
suvikhyātayornyāyācāryayorvācaspatyudayanayoścāntarā jñānaśrīmitra: setubandhanaṃ cakāreti
mahattvātiśayastasya tadgranthānāṃ ca | tasya granthanirmāṇakālastu sṛṣṭīyaikādaśaśatakasyādi-
me'rdhe saṃbhavet |
prastāvanā
āstikaśāstreṣu bauddhagrantheṣu ca sutarāṃ niṣṇāta āsīdayaṃ jñānaśrīmitra iti
tannibandhapāṭhād vijñāyate | tasya prākpradiṣṭaṃ tantrayānānugatvaṃ tu na granthaparyālocanātaḥ
spaṣṭībhavati | pramāṇavārtikasthailokaviśeṣa [1.16] vyākhyāvasare svagurortamapi pradarśita
metena | suvarṇadvīpavāsino dharmapālācāryasya śiṣyatvasvīkāropya'sya śrūyate | svasampradāya -
paricāyakastatkṛtaślokastu tadīyasākārasiddhī,
āryāsaṅgamanaṅgajinnayavaho yadbhūpatīśo'nvaśād
ācāryo vasubandhurudhuramatistasyājñayādidyutat |
dignāgo'tha kumāranāthavihitāsāmānyasāhāyaka-
stasmin vārtikabhāṣyakārakṛtinoradyānavadyā sthitiḥ ||
iti | atra svavacasānena maitreyanāthopajñayogācāravijñānavādasampradāye prajñākarapravartite ca
dharmaprasthāne'sthāntarbhāva iti sphuṭīkṛtam | prācāryeṇa sthiravratakena [Stcherbatsky]
prajñākarānuyāyināṃ tredhā vibhāga: pradarśitaḥ | teṣu vibhāgeṣu jino ravigupto yamāriśca
pravaktāraḥ saṃjātāḥ | prajñākara śiṣyo ravigupto jñānaśrīsamakālaṃ kāśmīreṣūvāsa | yamāriśca
kāśmīrakasya jñānaśriyaḥ śiṣyaḥ, kāryakṣetraṃ cāsya vaṅgeṣviti tena pratipāditam | atha
raviguptakṛtijinena svagranthe khaṇḍitā jinakṛtiśca yamāriṇā iti tata eva śrūyate |
jñānaśrīmitrastu kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasyāntime bhāge kañcanācārya ravināmānaṃ dvedhā
nāmagrāhaṃ sasammānaṃ collikhati | etaṃ viṣayaṃ manasi nidhāya raviguptajñānaśrīyamāriṇāṃ
parasparasaṃbandhaḥ punarvivecanamarhati | sarvaṃ ime vaṅgamagadhapracalite prajñākarīye prasthāne'nta-
rbhūtā na veti, raviguptayamāryorantarā ca jñānaśrīmitrasya sthānamuta jñānaśrībhadrasyeti ca
punaravekṣaṇīyam | atra nirṇayastu jñānaśrīmitranibandhaiḥ saha bhoṭabhāṣānuvādanibaddhābhyāṃ
raviguptasya yamāreśca kṛtibhyāṃ sādhyena tulaneneva saṃbhāvyate ||
2. upalabdhanibandhaparicayaḥ
upalabdhānāṃ jñānaśrīmitranibandhānāṃ kaścit paricayo'trāpekṣita iti kṛtvā
svalpaparisareṇaiva sa prastūyate |prastāvanā
(1) kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyākhyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vastūnāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaparo mukhyatamo jñāna-
śrīmitranibandhaḥ | eṣa ca granthāntarasyādhyāyaviśeṣa iti na mantavyam | etasyaiva catvāraḥ
paricchedāḥ santi | atra nyāyavedistambhabhūtānāṃ śaṅkarabhāsarvajñatrilocanavācaspatīnāṃ
matāni samunmūlya svamataṃ sthāpitamiti granthakṛtā kaṇṭhata evāpāditam | dṛśyate cātra
tattanmatāni proddhṛtya bāhulyena khaṇḍitānīti |
yat sat tat kṣaṇikaṃ yathā jaladhara : santastu bhāvā ime
sattā śaktirihārthaṃkarmaṇi miteḥ siddheṣu siddhā na sā |
nāpyekaiva vidhānyadāpi parikṛnnaiva kriyā vā bhaved
dvedhāpi kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃgatirataḥ sādhye ca viśrāmyati ||
ityādimaśloke śāstrārtha: saṃgṛhītaḥ | tataścaturṣu paricchedeṣu pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekā
hetukavināśādhikārākhyeṣu sthiravādaṃ dīrghaviśleṣaṇena khaṇḍayitvā svamataṃ pratiṣṭhāpitam |
vicāraścātra pūrṇāṅgo mārmikaśca ||
(2) vyāpticarcā tu bauddhopajñavyāptisvarūpa pradarśanaparo nibandha: | vyāptiśca
bhāratīyadarśanaprasthāneṣu cārvākān prahāya sarvaiḥ svīkriyate | kiṃ tu tasyā mūlaṃ svarūpaṃ
cādhikṛtya teṣu matabhedo vartatetarām | naiyāyikā vyabhicārājñānaṃ sahacārajñānaṃ ca
vyāptiniścayopāya iti kathayanti, bauddhāśca tādātmyatadutpattibhyāmabhāvena ca vyāptimupa
pādayanti | atra tu prāsaṅgike vicāre trilocanavācaspatiprabhṛtīnāṃ matānyuddhṛtya
khaṇḍitāni | ante ca pratyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavaiva hetuphalabhāvasvabhāvavyāptisiddhiriti
niṣkarṣaḥ pradattaḥ ||
(3) jñānaśriyo nibandhāvalau bhedābhedaparīkṣā hastratamā | jñānajñeyayoḥ saṃbandha-
vicāro'syā viṣaya iti bhāti | tayorbhedameke āmananti, aikyaṃ cāpare | pakṣayorubhayorapi
doṣāḥ pradiṣṭā itītare bhedābhedapakṣamurarīkurvanti | bhedasvīkāreṇābhedapakṣasya, abhedāva-
lambanena ca bhedapakṣasya doṣā apayantīti teṣāmāśaya: | siddhāntastu jñānaśriyo'bheda-
pakṣapātī, bhedābhedasvīkāre ubhayapakṣaparidṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ sannipātāpatteḥ ||
(4) anupalabdhirahasyamapi kṣudramākāreṇa bauddhadārśanikasvīkṛtāyā anupalabdhe-
laṃkṣaṇaṃ bhedāśca samāhṛtya śāstragranthebhyo'tra carcitāni ||
prastāvanā
(5) sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā tvanupalabdhi rahasyasya khilarūpeṇa svīkāramarhati,
śabdasāmānyābhāve kāryānupalabdhisāmarthya vivecanāt | śabdasāmānyābhāve ca na siddhā-
tino vimatiḥ; prastute kāryānupalabdhisthale svabhāvānupalabdhipratiṣṭhāpanamevātra tasya
kṛtyam ||
(6) apohaprakaraṇaṃ bauddhasiddhāntānusāraṃ śabdārthavivecanaparamatīva gambhīrārthakam |
śabdestāvanmukhyamākhyāyate'rtha-
stanāpohastadguṇatvena gamyaḥ |
arthaścaiko'dhyāsato bhāsato'nyaḥ
sthāpyo vācyastattvatto naiva kaścit ||
iti prakaraṇārthasaṃgrāhakaḥ iloko jñānaśrīmitrasya | eṣa grantho bāhulyena khaṇḍita udayanā-
cāryeṇa tadanusāriṇā ca śaṅkaramiśreṇeti bauddhādhikāracarcāniratairavadheyam ||
(7) īśvaravādastu viśvanirmātunityasya parameśvarasya khaṇḍanaṃ vidadhāti | prathame
paricchede śaṅkaravācaspativittokabhāsarvajñatrilocanaśatānandānāṃ jagatkartṛsādhakāni
matāni tattadvacasā samupasthāpya, dvitīye bauddhadṛśā sāmānyatastatkhaṇḍanam | tṛtīye ca
vistaravyākhyānam |
dharmakīrtikṛtapramāṇavārtikastheśvarakhaṇḍanaparasya ślokasaptakasya
tṛtīyo'pi paricchedastredhā vibhakto granthakāreṇa ||
(8) svasiddhāntānusāraṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvanirṇaya kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhī vihito
jñānaśrīmitreṇa | trikapañcakacintetyasyāparaṃ nāmadheyam | dharmayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvasthāpana-
dharmottarasya
vidhāvupalambhānupalambhānāṃ saṃkhyā nirṇayamadhikṛtya bauddheṣu matavirodhaḥ |
pañcakapakṣaḥ, jñānaśrīmitrasya tu trikapakṣaḥ | gadyapadyanibaddhe'tra granthe kārikāsu siddhāntaḥ
pradarśitaḥ, gadyabhāge ca tadarthako vicāraḥ | jñānaśrī mitra nibandhe vayameka eva bhoṭabhāṣāyā-
manūdito'bhūt ||
(9) yoginirṇayaprakaraṇe yogisvarūpaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ ca bauddhasammataṃ vivecitavānā-
cāryaḥ ||
(10) advaitabinduprakaraṇaṃ sākāravijñānavādavyākhyānaparam | atra jñānajñeyayo-
stāttvikabhedanirāśaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
(11) sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākāravijñānavādameva mahatā āḍambareṇa prapañcayati |
dharmaṃkītirasya vādasya pravartaka iti śrūyate | prajñākareṃṇāyaṃ viśadīkṛtaḥ | atra śāstre48
prastāvanā
vādasyāsya vyākhyānaṃ nāgārjunamaitreyanāthāsaṅgādiprācīnācāryasammatipradarśanapuraḥsaraṃ
samupalabhyate | dharmakīrteḥ prajñākarasya ca matāni pradarśitāni | ṣaṭsu paricchedeṣu vibhakta-
midaṃ śāstram | prathame nirākārajñānavādavivecanam dvitīye saṃkleśavyavadānacarcā, tṛtīye
madhyamāvatārapradarśanam caturthe citrādvaitaprapañcanam pañcame svasaṃvedanavicāraḥ, ṣaṣṭhe ca
yogācāravijñānavādena mādhyamakasiddhāntasya maulikamaikyaṃ samāgacchanti ||
(12) sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ tāvat sākārasiddhiśāstrasya padyātmakaḥ sārasaṃgrahaḥ |
atra tu catvāraḥ paricchedāḥ | teṣveva śāstrasthānāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ paricchedānāṃ viṣayāḥ
samāhṛtāḥ ||
3. prastutanibandhānāṃ kartṛtvavicāraḥ
atra kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyaṃ vihāyaikādaśanibandhā mātṛkāmekāmavalambyaiva sampāditāḥ |
bahutra ca granthakṛnnāmanirdeśa: puṣpikāyāṃ nāyāti | ataeva prastutanibandhānāmekakartṛttva-
svīkārakāraṇaṃ spaṣṭīkaraṇīyam |
( 1 ) kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye puṣpikāsuna granthakārollekha: | antimaśloke tenastāt
parapāragastribhuvane jñāna śriyo'yaṃ jana ityatra tasya saṃketa iti pratibhāti | ratnakīryudayana-
vādidevādibhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasthāḥ ilokā jñānaśrīnāmnā samuddhṛtāḥ |
( 2 ) vyāptinirṇayastu jñānaśrī mitrakṛtireva, puṣpikāyāṃ tathā nirdeśāt |
(3) bhedābhedaparīkṣāpi jñānaśrīmitranirmitā, tadīyasākārasiddhau tathā kathanāt |
(4,5 ) anupalabdhi rahasyasya sarvaśabdābhāvacarcāyāśca kartā nollikhitaḥ, na
vetaratra tadupalambhaḥ |
(6) apohaprakaraṇastha: sandarbho vādidevena jñānaśromitrasyaiveti nāmagrāhaṃ gṛhītaḥ
syādvādaratnākare |
(7) īśvaravādakartureva granthāntaraṃ trikapañcakacinteti īśvaravāde nirdiṣṭam |
sākārasiddhiśāstre ca tatkartubṛhadīśvaravādaḥ samullikhitaḥ |
(8) trikapañcaka cintāparākhyā kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrakṛtiriti tasya
granthasya bhoṭabhāṣānuvādāt parijñāyate |
prastāvanā
(9) ratnakorte: sarvajñasiddherādhārabhūto yoginirṇaya iti bhāṣāsāmyād viṣaya-
sāmyācca samāyāti |
(10) sākārasiddhī jñānaśrī mitra granthatvenādvaitabinduprakaraṇasyollekho dṛśyate |
(11-12) sākārasiddhiśāstraṃ sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ ca puṣpikānirdeśāj jñānaśrīmitra-
kṛtī eva |
etat sarvaṃ manasi nidhāya, ekāṃ śailī sarvatra cāvalokya, vimṛśya caikamātṛkāyāṃ
sarveṣāṃ samupalambhaṃ dvādaśa ime granthā jñānaśrī mitranirmitā iti nirṇayaḥ svata evāpatati |
ebhiḥ sahānupalabdhā sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrī mitrasya samullekhamarhati | sāpi ratnakīrtinā
svasarvajñasiddhau vyavahṛteti pratibhāti | sākārasiddhau vyāpticarcāyāṃ ca jñānaśrī mitreṇa
sarvajñasiddhiḥ kācidullikhitā, yoginirṇaye ca jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiḥ sarvajñasiddhiḥ anyatra
yoginirṇaye sarvajñasiddheḥ ślokārdhoddhāro dṛśyate | ekaiva sarvajñasiddhirjñānaśrīmitrakṛtā
sarvatrāmṛṣṭeti pratibhāti |
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye 'hetuphalagrahaṇe vyavasthitapratisandhātṛvādastu prastoṣyate'nekānta-
cintāyām' iti nirdeśadarśanena jñāyate jñānaśrīmitrasyābhipretamanekāntavādamālambya
granthāntaramāsīditi | sā tvanekāntacintā nirmitā na veti na parijñāyate ||
4. prastutanibandhānāṃ kālakramaḥ
saṃskaraṇe'tra mātṛkādṛṣṭagranthakrama evānusṛtaḥ | itaretarollekhadarśanāt kutracidanyathā-
bhāvasaṃbhave'pi mātṛkāyā ekatvād viparivartanamatra na yuktiyuktam | na ca pūrṇo grantha-
kramo'nyataḥ kutaścidāgacchati | nibandhāścātra parasparanirapekṣāḥ | udayanācāryakṛte
ātmatattvaviveke jñānaśrīmitramatakhaṇḍana vidhāvapi nibandhanirmāṇakramo nānusṛta iti lakṣyate |
itaretarollekhadarśanabalena prāptaṃ granthakramavivaraṇamatra prastūyate |
anupalabdhi rahasyam, sarvaśabdābhāvacarcā, yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam, sākārasaṃgrahasūtraṃ ca
nibandhāntare nāmagrāhaṃ nopāttāni | ato jñānaśrīmitrakṛtiṣu teṣāṃ kramikasthāna nirdeśo
na śakyakriya: | vyāpticarcāyām apohaprakaraṇe, īśvaravāde coddeśāt tebhyaḥ prāk
kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasya sthānam | īśvaravādāt pūrvaṃ vyāpticarcā nirmitā, tasyāstatrollekhāt |
sākārasiddhāvullikhitā bhedābhedaparīkṣā tataḥ pūrvaṃ nirmitetyāyāti | tathaiva vyāpticarcā-A LIGERE TO
prastāvanā
to'pohaprakaraṇasya prācīnatvam | vyāpticarcāyāmapi bhāvino'pohaprakaraṇasya nirdeśo
dṛśyate | sākārasiddheḥ pūrvamīśvaravādasya nirmāṇa niścapracam tasya tatrollekhāt |
kṣaṇabhaṅgeśvaravādayoḥ pūrvaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhiviracitā, ubhayatra tasya vyavahārāt |
advaitabinduprakaraṇamapi tathaiva sākārasiddhiśāstrāt pūrvaṃ patati | samānanyāyena sākāra-
siddhiśāstraṃ cāpohaprakaraṇakṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyayoḥ pūrvavati |
etāvatā bahuṣu sthaleṣu paurvāparye nirṇīte'pi pūrṇalekhanakramanirdhāraṇaṃ duḥśakamevaiteṣāṃ
nibandhānāmiti sphuṭaṃ vijñāyate ||
5. jñānaśrīmitrasya racanāśailī
jñānaśrīmitrasya śailī tāvadakuṇṭhā saralā ca yayā satyapi viṣayakāṭhinye nibandhā
ime viduṣāṃ manoharā : saṃjātā: | bauddhaparibhāṣāto bāhulyena muktāḥ, bhāṣādṛṣṭyā ca
naiyāyikādibhiḥ saṃbaddhāśca sarve | pūrvasūriṇo dharmakīrtiprajñā karādayastu na śailīsauṣṭhavamadhi-
kṛtya jñānaśriyamatiśerate |
viṣayakāṭhinyamantarnihitaṃ manohārikathānakādiyojanena laghukṛtaṃ jñānaśriyā |
bhautavicārākhyānametatprayuktamudayanādigrantheṣu bahutra svīkṛtaṃ dṛśyate | laukikanyāyāḥ
kautukoktayaścāntarāntarā niviṣṭā navīnatāṃ vidadhate nīrasasyāpi viṣayajātasya |
prāyaḥ sarve'tra nibandhā vicārabahulā: | sammukhasthita iva pratipakṣe dṛśyate'tra yukti-
prayogaḥ | ataeva jalpakathāvat kaṭukaśabdaprayogā api na durlabhāḥ | ādī pratipakṣavacasaiva
tanmatamanūdya tatastadviśleṣaṇaṃ yuktyā khaṇḍanaṃ ca jñānaśrīmitrasya vaiśiṣṭayam | anukṛto'sāvatra
svaśiṣyeṇa ratnakīrtināpi |
iha dārśanikeṣvapi prabandheṣu bahutra bhāṣā kavitvasuṣamāmaṇḍitā samāyāti |
alaṅkāraprayogāśca paraṃ prītikarāḥ | bhaṭṭanārāyaṇakṛterveṇīsaṃhārasya ślokaviśeṣamādhārīkṛtya
prajñā yena khalīkṛtāmbaradaśāmākṛṣya naḥ preyasī
sāsūyaṃ sadasi sthiteṣu kṛtiṣu prakhyātakīrtiṣvapi |
krūranyāyamayo nirākṛtinayo duḥśāsanaḥ sāmprataṃ
so'yaṃ madbhujapañjare nipatitaḥ saṃrakṣyatāṃ kauravāḥ ||
prastāvanā
iti śleṣapara: sākārasaṃgrahopodghātaśloko'tra draṣṭavyaḥ | sa ca nibandhaḥ kṛtsna eva
vṛttanibaddhaḥ | itaratrāpi jñānaśrīmitro vṛttavyavahāraṃ bāhulyena karoti | tatrāpi dīrghavṛttānāṃ
prayogo'dhikarucikaraḥ pāṭhakasya | chandaḥśāstropadeṣṭā āsīdasau jñānaśrīmitra iti śrūyate |
tattu prastutagranthadarśanādavitathamiti bhāti |
kavitvakhyātirapyasya jñānaśrī mitrasya bahuprathitā āsīditi saṃbhāvyate | subhāṣita-
ratnakoṣe vidyākareṇa jñānaśrīmitranāmnā lokeśvarastutimūlakaṃ ślokadvayam
atyudgāḍharayasthirākṛtighanadhvānabhramanmandara-
kṣubdhakṣī radhivī cisañcayagataprāleyapādopamaḥ |
śrīmatpotalake gabhīravivṛtidhvānaṃpratidhvānite
sāndrasvāṃśucayaśriyā balayito lokeśvaraḥ pātu vaḥ ||
udarasyedamaṇutvaṃ sahajagurutvaṃ yadi nedaṃ hṛdayasya |
svārthe kathamalasatvaṃ kathamanusattvaṃ hitakaraṇe matirasya ||
iti samuddhṛtam | paṇḍitajñānaśrīnāmnā ca
taranto dṛśyante bahava iha gambhīrasarasi
svasārābhyāmābhyāṃ hṛdi vidadhataḥ kautukaśatam |
praviśyāntarlīnaṃ kimapi suvivecyoddharati ya
śviraṃ ruddhaśvāsaḥ sa khalu punareteṣu viralaḥ ||
iti ślokastenaivoddhṛtaḥ| saṃbhāvyate cāyamapi jñānaśrīmitrasyeti, paṇḍitaśabdena svakṛtiṣu
tasya vyapadeśadarśanāt |
jñānaśrīmitrāt pūrvaṃ jaranyāyikena jayantabhaṭṭena, tadanantaraṃ ca vādidevaprabhṛtibhiḥ
darśana nibandheṣu sālaṅkārapadyaprayogo vihitaḥ ||

dṛḍhapratipakṣakaṇṭakitamārgapariśodhanaṃ vidhāya svaśemuṣīparicālanaṃ kṛtamatra nibandheṣu
jñānaśrī mitreṇetyetaddarśanāt sphuṭībhavati | tadvicāriteṣu naiyāyikagrantheṣu bahavaścirāyaprastāvanā
luptāḥ | nyāyasampradāye'gaṇiteṣu grantheṣvativiśiṣṭa eva surakṣitāḥ | tādṛśayodvaṃyorantarā
samāgatāstu praṇaṣṭāḥ | kānicit tatratyāni matāni surakṣitānyavaktanagrantheṣu | tathā
ceśvaravādamadhikṛtya prācīna naiyāyikamatāni bahūni nyāyakusumāñjalāvudayanena samāviṣṭāni |
bauddhā jaināśca sanāmollekhaṃ teṣāṃ sandarbhān bahutra rakṣitavantaḥ | dharmakīrtimudayanaṃ cāntarā
samāgatānāṃ taiyāyikānāṃ bahūni matāni jñānaśrīmitra: svanibandheṣu vidhṛtavāniti nyāya-
śāstrālocakānāṃ kṛte ime nibandhā bahumūlyā ityatra na vartate saṃśayaleśo'pi ||
7. atrāmṛṣṭā bauddhāḥ pūrvasūrayaḥ
jñānaśrīmitrakālāt pūrvameva bauddhanyāyaprasthānaṃ dṛḍhapratiṣṭhaṃ babhūva | sa ca saprasādaṃ
prācīnagranthānāmṛśati, tatra viśeṣābhijñaḥ svecchayā tān vyavaharati ca | mukhyato
dharmaṃkīrtimatavyākhyānaparasyāsya mahāyānatantraparijñānaṃ pūrṇatayā āsīt | bauddhasāhitye
nūtanatayā saṃyojite nyāyaprasthāne dharmakītikṛteḥ pramāṇavārtikasyāntarbhāvaḥ | eṣa khalu
ācāryaḥ prajñākaropajñadharmaṃprasthānānusārī prācīnānāṃ matānyapi vārtike'trānusyūtānīti
manute | ataevaitasya vyākhyānaṃ prācīnanavīnayoḥ saṃyogasūtramiti suvacam | etadartha mevetastha
nibandheṣu prācīna granthoddhārastadvyākhyānaṃ ca bhṛśaṃ dṛśyete | ebhiḥ pratipakṣapratyāyanaṃ
sukaramabhūditi na saṃbhāvyate | tathāpi prācīnārvācīnayoḥ saṃyogavidhānaceṣṭātra sādhoyasī
vihitā | evaṃ prajñākarasyāśayaḥ samarthito jñānaśriyā | kathayati cāsau tadvayākhyānavaibhavena
vārtikakārasya dharmakīrteḥ, tadbhāṣyakārasya ca prajñākarasya sthitiranavadyā saṃjāteti |
suviśāle bauddhasūtrasāhitye nitarāmabhijño'sau jñānaśrīmitraḥ sandhinirmocanasūtra
samādhirājasūtraṃ ca nāmagrāhamitarāṇi ca sūtrāṇi sāmānyata ullikhati | prajñāpāramitāsu
tāvadasya viśeṣa parijñānaṃ dṛśyate | arvācīneṣu prajñāpāramitāsārasaṃgraheṣu dignāgakṛtaḥ
prajñāpāramitāpiṇḍārthastu bahudhānenoddhṛtaḥ | maitreyanāthapādakṛtiṣu abhisamayālaṅkāro,
mahāyānasūtrālaṅkāro, madhyāntavibhāgasūtram, mahāyānottaratantraṃ ca bhṛśaṃ pramāṇarūpeṇātū-
ditāni nibandheṣveteṣu |
yogācāramataprasthāpakasya maitreyanāthapādasyaitihāsikatve viprattipattirāsīd
garīyasī | cainikasaṃpradāyānusāraṃ prollikhitagranthānāmasaṅga eva nirmātā | eṣa tāvad
viṣayaḥ kalikātāviśvavidyālayabhāṣaṇamālāyāmācāryavareṇa tuṣitena [ Dr. Tucci ]
viśiṣya vivecitaḥ | sthāpitaśca tena pramāṇopanyāsena bhoṭadeśīyaḥ pravādo maitreyanātha-
pādasyaivaiteṣāṃ kartṛtvakhyāpakaḥ | asaṅgastu maitreyakṛtīnāṃ vyākhyātā | kāle gacchati
prastāvanā
mūlakartuṣṭīkākārasya ca bhedo bahutra vismṛtigrastaḥ saṃjātaḥ | jñānaśrīmitro maitreyanāthapādasya
ślokamudddhāra | sa ca ślokastacchiṣyeṇa ratnakīrtinā maitreyanāthasyeti kaṇṭhataḥ prati-
pāditam | ato bhoṭadeśīyo'yaṃ pravādī jñānaśrī mitrakālapracalitabhāratīyapravādādabhinna
iti śobhatetarām |
maitreyanāthapādasya śiṣyo guruśca vasubandhupādasya ācāryo'saṅgapādaḥ pramāṇabhūto
jñānaśrīmitrasya | svakṛtigauravādasau prasiddhimatitarāṃ lebhe | sākārasiddhau sākārasaṃgrahasūtre
cāsya matasāroddhāro dṛśyate |
ācāryabasubandhupādasya dharmadhamatāpravibhāgo'troddhṛtaḥ | dharmaṃdharmikārikā dharmadharma-
tāvibhaṅgaśca bhoṭabhāṣāyāmupalabhyete | ubhayatra granthakartṛtvena maitreyanātha evodiṣṭaḥ |
dharmaṃdharmitā vibhaṅgavṛttistu kācid vasubandhukṛtā bhoṭabhāṣānuvādamayī dṛśyate | atra
saivollikhitā bhavet | vasubandhorabhidharmakoṣāt triṃśatikāvijñapteśca ślokodvāraḥ kṛto'tra
nibandheṣu |
vasubandhuśiṣyo dignāgastāvanmadhyakālikanyāyaśāstrasya janakatayā prasiddhaḥ |
tatkartṛkaṃ pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ jñānaśriyā samuddhṛtaṃ dharmakītikṛtatallakṣaṇena sākam | tasya
prajñāpāramitāpiṇḍārthavyavahārastu prāgevoddiṣṭaḥ |
kumāranāthanāmnā yuvarājanāmnā ca prasiddhaṃ kañcana dignāgasahāyaṃ samuddharati
jñānaśrīmitraḥ, saṃgṛhṇāti ca bhūyasā tanmatāni | ratnakītirapi rājakulapādanāmnā etameva
parāmṛśatīti bhāti | bodhisattva āryamañjuśrīḥ pramāṇasamuccayanirmāṇārthe dignāgaṃ samutsā-
hayituṃ tatsamīpa āvirabhūditi śrūyate | dignāgasahāyabhūtastu kumāranātho nānyatroddiṣṭaḥ |
jñānaśriyā svanibandheṣu tanmatarakṣaṇaṃ vihitamiti kimapi nūtanametat pramodasthānaṃ ca
prācīna bauddhaśāstrālocakānāṃ kṛte |
maitreyāsaṅgagranthavyākhyātā sthiramatistāvadatiprasiddha ācāryaḥ | tasya granthasandarbhā
api kecana surakṣitāḥ prastutanibandheṣu |
dignāgādūrdhve dharmakīrtiḥ svagranthamahimnā bauddhaprasthānaṃ bhāratīyadarśanaṃ cojjvalayā-
ñcakāra | jñānaśrīmitramatenāyaṃ yogācāravijñānavādaprasthānasya mūlaḥ stambhaḥ | asau tu
bahudhā samuddiṣṭaḥ samuddhṛtaśca | vastugatyā sarve caite nibandhāḥ dharmakīrtikṛtapramāṇavārtikena
dṛḍhaṃ saṃbaddhāḥ | prajñākarīyavyākhyā prasthānamanusṛtya dharmakīrtimatānyeṣa sphuṭīcakāra jñānaśrī-
mitra eteṣu svanibandheṣu | nyāyaprasūtinyāyavādītyādināmnā samuddiṣṭo'sāvācāryo dṛśyate,58
tadgranthāśca śāstraśabdena | īśvaravāde pramāṇavārtikaślokāḥ savistaraṃ vyākhyātāḥ |
anyatra pramāṇavārtikaślokāḥ pramāṇatvenoddhṛtāḥ | dharmakīrte pramāṇaviniścayo'pyatra
samuddhṛto dṛśyate |
prastāvanā
dharmaṃkītigranthāstu sarvāṇyevāstikaprasthānāni śithilamūlāni cakruḥ | tatra tatra
vācaspatergranthanirmāṇaṃ tu dharmakīrtimatakhaṇḍanena teṣāṃ dṛḍhīkaraṇāyeti saṃbhāvyate | udaya-
nastvasya vaidikadharmaparityāgakathāmullikhati | prasiddhaścāyaṃ bhadṛbhikṣunāmnā |
dharmaṃkīrterantaraṃ prajñākarastāvadatra nibandheṣu viśeṣādarabhāg dṛśyate | pramāṇavāti-
kālaṅkārāparanāmakaṃ pramāṇavārtikabhāṣyaṃ tu dharmakīrtimatasya dharmīyavyākhyānasampradāya
syādimo granthaḥ | bhāṣyamidamavalambya raviguptasya jinasya yamāreśca vyākhyāgranthāḥ
pravartitā iti prāgeva saṃdiṣṭam | bahumānapūrvakaṃ jñānaśrī mitra : prajñākaraṃ samullikhati |
sākāravādanayanāṭakasya tvayaṃ sūtradhārarūpeṇa nirdiṣṭaḥ | etasya pramāṇavārtikabhāṣyaṃ ca
dārśanikairavaktanaibahutra carcitam | teṣu pradhānatayollekhamarhati pramāṇaviniścayakrudvādi-
rājaḥ | vādivinode śaṅkaramiśraḥ, nyāyatattvāloke ca dvitīyo vācaspatirenamullikhataḥ |
tathaiva padārtharatnamālāyāṃ raghunāthaḥ, nyāyasiddhāntamālāyāṃ jayarāmaśca prasiddhabauddhācārya-
gaṇanāyāmetasyāpi kaṭhinīpātaṃ kurutaḥ |
eṣo'pi vaidikadharmaṃ vihāya bauddhaśāsanamāśritavāniti bauddhādhikāre udayanācārya-
vacanāj jñāyate |
anye kecana bauddhā jñānaśrī mitrasampradāyena sākṣādasaṃbaddhā api nibandheṣveteṣu
prasaṅgavaśāduddiṣṭāḥ| teṣu mādhyamikā vaibhāṣikā: sautrāntikāraca sāmānyataḥ spṛṣṭāḥ |
viśiṣya ca mādhyamikamataprasthāpaka āryanāgārjunapādo jñānaśrīmitradṛśā paraṃ sammāna-
bhājanam | ā maitreyanāthāt prācīnavijñānavādino nāgārjunaprabhāvitā dṛśyante |
ubhayamatayorbhedastāvadanatigambhīraḥ | jñānaśrīmitrastu bhedaṃ parihāya matayoretayomalika-
maikyamevorarīcakāra |
sākārasiddhiśāstre śāntidevapādasya bodhicaryāvatāraḥ pramāṇarūpeṇoddhṛtaḥ |
atrollikhitaḥ śubhaguptācāryo vaibhāṣiko bhavet | asau vārtikānusārīti
anekāntajayapatākāvyākhyāyāṃ haribhadrācāryāḥ | vārtikaṃ cedaṃ pramāṇavārtikamiti bhāti |
tattvasaṃgrahapañjikāyām anekāntajayapatākāyāṃ ca tatkṛtāḥ ślokāḥ samuddhṛtā dṛśyante |
śāstravārtāsamuñcayaṭokāyāmapyasau samullikhitaḥ |
prastāvanā
dharmākaradattāparākhyo'rcaṃṭastu dharmakītigranthavyākhyātṛṣvanyatamaḥ | sa tu bhaṭṭārcaṃṭa-
śabdena jñānaśriyā nirdiṣṭaḥ |
acaṃṭaśiṣyo dharmottarācāryastu pratyarthitvenātra svīkṛtaḥ | tatsamarthitaṃ nirākāra-

dharmottarasyāpohasiddhiruddiṣṭā | kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhau ca tatsammataḥ pañcakapakṣa: khaṇḍita
ityābhāti | bauddhasampradāye ṭīkākāraśabdenāsya dhamottarasya nirdeśastu dharmaṃkītigrantha-
vyākhyānasya tatkṛtasya vaiśiṣṭyaṃ sūcayati | jñānaśrīmitraśca tadvipakṣabhūtaḥ tamadhikṛtya
karkaśaśabdānapi prayuṅkte |
avaktanadārśanika grantheṣu jñānaśromitramatacarcā

kurvanti | āstikā jaināścainaṃ paripanthitvena gaṇayanti |

ca te ratna kīrtinibandhāvalīnāmnā granthamālāyāmantraiva sampādya prakāśitāḥ | eteṣu daśa

cāgacchanti | eteṣāṃ saṃskṛtaṃ mūlaṃ luptam | nāmadarśanāt kecana tāntrikā apareca

prastāvanāyāṃ pradattam | darśanaśāstre'sau jñānaśrīmitra śiṣya iti jñānaśrī mitra nibandhasthitānāṃ

saṃgraho vihita ityāyāti | etadadhikṛtya tena svīyādhamarṇatāpi gurorasakṛt prakaṭīkṛtā |prastāvanā

caraṇametayoḥ spaṣṭībhavati | jñānaśrī mitranibandhebhyaḥ samudrasadṛśebhyaḥ katicana ratnānyeva
ratnakīrti rāhṛtavāniti svayamasau kathayati | kavitvaguṇagariṣṭhebhyo jñānaśrī mitranibandhebhya-
stacchiṣyakṛtasārasaṃgrahāstu saṃkṣiptāḥ, nyāyapaddhatyanugāśceti dṛśyante |

tattvaviveke— āgamaśca na kiñcid vadatīti tvayaiva grāhitaḥ śiṣyaḥ | na caivaṃ cetano
grāhayitumapi śakyate, svavāgvirodhasyodbhaṭatvāt | tathāhi,
śabdasya kasyacidavastuni mānasiddhā
bādhāvidhivyavahṛtiḥ kacidasti no vā |
astyeva cet kathamiyanti na dūṣaṇāni

iti tavaiva viṣayasañcāramātreṇa ślokaḥ ityāyāti | atra prasaṅgāgato jñānaśrīmitraślokastu,
dharmasya kasyacidavastuni mānasiddhā
bādhāvidhivyavahṛtiḥ kimihāsti no vā |
kkāpyasti cet kathamiyanti na dūṣaṇāni
nāstyeva cet svavacanapratirodhasiddhiḥ ||
iti, yatra viṣayasañcāra udayanasya | ratnakīrtistu svagurunimitamimaṃ ślokaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhī
dvedhā samuddhṛtavān |
kavikhyātirapi ratnakīrterāsīditi vidyākarasaṃgṛhīte subhāṣitaratnakoṣe tatkṛta-
lokanāthastutimūlakasya,
varadakarasarojasyandamānāmṛtaudha-

ityetasya ślokasya saṃgrahāt parijñāyate |
varendrayāṃ jagaddalavihārācāryo mokṣākaragupto'pi jñānaśrīmitrānusārī āsīditi

dṛśyo'tha vyatirekasiddhimanasā kartā samāśrīyate

udayanajñānaśriyoḥ saṃbandha:

tātparyapariśuddhau kusumāñjalo ca yathāprāptaṃ bauddhamatakhaṇḍanaṃ na tirohitaṃ vidvallocanebhyaḥ |
ātmatattvavivekākhyo grantharatnaśca bauddhamatakhaṇḍanaparo bauddhādhikāranāmnā vā varīvatti |
ki tū ko vāsau bauddhācāryo yanmatakhaṇḍanaṃ rājasabhāyāṃ kṛtamācāryeṇa ? ke vā
tallikhitā granthāḥ ? kutratyo vāsāviti na tathā parijñāyate sma | manye nyāyācāryasyā-
laukikapratibhayā, tacchiṣyasya ca mithilādhipasya daṇḍabalena bauddhagranthānāṃ kutracinnāśe
kutracid vānādare saṃjāte bauddhasiddhāntā: vismṛtivilīnā babhūvuḥ | kiyatkālānantaraṃ
yāvanaviplavena nālandāvikramaśīlādibauddhavihārāṇāṃ sarvathā vināśe śiṣṭānāmapi bauddha-
granthānāṃ vilopaḥ saṃjātaḥ | yena sarvatantrasvatantrasya vācaspatimiśrasya siddhānteṣu bauddhā-
cāryāṇāmākṣepā durjñeyāḥ babhūvuḥ | yadyapi bauddhamatakhaṇḍanapūrvakaṃ vācaspatimatasamarthanamudayana-
grantheṣu bhṛśaṃ dṛśyate, tathāpi pūrvapakṣatvena dhṛtānāṃ tattanmatānāṃ māhātmyāvagamaḥ kartṛnirṇayo
vā na śakyakriya āsīt |

cakāra |
ādhunike kāle kṣīṇo'pi nyāyagranthānāṃ saṃpradāyo vartate, na tu bauddhagranthānām |
te tu bāhulyena luptāḥ | prāptāḥ prakāśitāśca kecana saṃpradāyavicchedāt na tathā jāyante sma
nyāyaśāstrapāṭhavidhau sahāyāḥ |
mahāpaṇḍita rāhulasāṃkṛtyāyanakṛtaṃ bhoṭadeśaparibhramaṇaṃ prācīnaśāstragaveṣakāṇāṃ parama-
hitāya saṃvṛttam | tena mahāpaṇḍitena tataḥ saṃgṛhītā vividhabauddhanyāyagranthānāṃ chāyāprati
lipayo vihāraprāntīyasarvakāraprayatnena pāṭaliputra eva saṃrakṣitāḥ sulabhāśva gaveṣakāṇāmiti
pramodasthānamasmākam | atrāgacchanti bauddhagranthāḥ prācīnanyāyaśāstreṇa bhṛśaṃ saṃbaddhā
yeṣāṃ samīkṣaṇena nyāyasiddhānteṣvapi pracurālokasaṃpāto jāyate | atra vācaspateranantara
mudayanācca pūrva samupalabhyante jñānaśrīmitrasya ratnakīrteśca granthāḥ | ratnakīrtiśca jñānaśriyaḥ

anena śaṅkaranyāyabhūṣaṇatrilocanādibhiḥ sākaṃ vācaspatiḥ pratidvandvitvena svīkṛta iti
dṛṣṭacaram |

udayanakṛtagrantheṣūpalabhyamāneṣvātmatattvaviveka eva prathamaḥ | tatra tvādita ārabhya

dyotakeṣu ca bahuṣu sandarbheṣu kecanaivātra nirdiśyante |

karmanirmitavaicitryaṃ yadi viśvamanīśvaram |
astvanirmitavaicitryaṃ jagadetadahetukam ||

karmanirmita vaicitryamanīśaṃ yo jagajjagau |
praṇamāmi pramāṇena tamavyāhataśāsanam ||
iti īśvaravāda [pṛ: 233, 265] sthajñānaśrīmitraślokaṃ samuddiśatīti bhāti |
gaṅgeśopādhyāyaśca tattvacintāmaṇau [ pratyakṣakhaṇḍe pṛ: 717 ] kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyasthaṃ
dṛṣṭastāvadayaṃ ghaṭo'tra ca patan dṛṣṭastathā mudgaro
dṛṣṭā kharparasaṃhatiḥ paramito'bhāvo na dṛṣṭaḥ paraḥ |
tenābhāva iti śrutiḥ ka nihitā kiṃ vātra tatkāraṇaṃ
svādhīnā kalasasya kevalamiyaṃ dṛṣṭā kapālāvalī ||
mādhavācāryakṛte sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe [ pṛ: 226 ] kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagato yat sat tat
kṣaṇikam ityādiśloko jñānajñīmitranāmollekhapuraḥsaraṃ samuddhṛto dṛśyate | atra saṃgrahe
bauddhadarśana paricchede jñānaśrī mitraprabhāvo'nyatrāpi prasphuṭaḥ |
jñānaśrīmitranibandheḥ śaṅkaramiśrasya pratyakṣaparicaya āsīt | ātmatattvavivekakalpa-
latāyāṃ tenāpohaprakaraṇādvaitabindusākārasiddhisākārasaṃgrahebhyaḥ ślokāḥ gadyasandarbhācoddhṛtāprastāvanā
vivecitāśca | vādivinode ca prakhyātānāṃ bauddhācāryāṇāṃ gaṇanāvasare bhadantajñānaśrīrapi
smṛtaḥ śaṅkareṇa| śaṅkarasya kāle bauddhaśāstrasya dhārā niruddhā babhūva, tataḥ pūrvameva bauddha-
vidyāvihārāṇāṃ tadgranthasampradāyasya cocchedāt |
jayarāmanyāyapañcānano'pi nyāya siddhāntamālāyāṃ vādivinodadṛṣṭāṃ bauddhācāryanāmāvalīṃ
samuddharati | tasya jñānaśrīmitra nibandhaparijñānamāsīdityatra tu pramāṇaṃ nopalabhyate |
jaineṣu vādidevaḥ syādvādaratnākare kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyādapohaprakaraṇāñca ilokasaṃgrahaṃ
cakāra | itarasmāt kasmāñcana jñānaśrī mitra granthādapi sandarbhāvudhāra |
nyāyāvatāra ṭippana ke devabhadrakṛte kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyagataṃ sattvalakṣaṇaṃ samuddhṛtam | jñāna-
śrīmitraśca nāmnā samuddiṣṭaḥ |
malliṣeṇanirmitāyāṃ syādvādamañjaryāṃ jñānaśrīkṛtāpohaprakaraṇasthasya etāsu pañca-
svavabhāsinīṣvityādiślokasya samuddharaṇaṃ dṛśyate | paṇḍitāśokakṛtāyāṃ sāmānyadūṣaṇadika-
prasāritāyāmapyeṣa śloka āyāti | paṇḍitāśokasya jñānaśrīmitrāt prācīnatvaṃ na
sandehātītam | atra tu prastutaślokasya kartṛnirdhāraṇe kṛte sati bhaviṣyati jñānaśriyā
malliṣeṇasya sambandhanirṇayaḥ |
svargatena paṇḍita mahendrakumāraśāstriṇā nyāyakumudacandraprākkathane apohaḥ śabda-
liṅgābhyāṃ na vastuvidhinocyate iti jñānaśriyo'pohaprakaraṇasthaślokāṃśasamuddharaṇāt
prabhācandro'pi jñānaśriyo'dhamarṇo bhavediti sūcitam | jñānaśrīmitraślokāṃśastu bhinna eva
uddhṛtāt, apohaḥ śabdaliṅgābhyāṃ prakāśyata iti sthitirityapohaprakaraṇe pāṭhadarśanāt |
śāstrimahodayena prabhācandrasya kālo nirṇītaḥ | sa ca jñānaśrīmitrāj jyāyāniti
pratibhāti | ataeva kanīyaso jñānaśriyaḥ ślokasyoddhāro'pi tasyāsambhava eva |
yaśovijayācāryasyāpratyakṣa: paricayo jñānaśrīmitreṇāsīt | anekāntavyavasthā -
prakaraṇe tena jñānaśrīmitrakṛtaḥ śloka uddhṛtaḥ | nyāyakhaṇḍakhādyasya tasyātmatattvavivekena
saha saṃbandhaḥ suviditaḥ | ato jñānaśrīmatāni tatra paramparayā āgacchanti | na ca kutrāpi
jñānaśrīmitro nāmadheyenollikhito yaśovijayena | nārāyaṇācāryakṛtā ātmatattvaviveka-
vyākhyā, raghunāthaśiromaṇerātmatattvavivekadīdhitiḥ, guṇānandavidyāvāgīśakṛtaścātmatattva-
vivekadīdhitiviveko bahudhā samuddhṛtā yaśovijayena | etebhya eva jñānaśrīmataparijñānaṃ
tasya bhavet | nārāyaṇāderapi jñānaśrīnibandhaparijñānaṃ nāsīditi bhāti, āsīt
śaṅkaramiśrasya | tasyātmatattvavivekakalpalatā punanaṃ vijñātā yaśovijayasya |

tadutpatteḥ | taditareṣu punarasya sahakāripratyayatā, teṣāṃ tu pūrve pavanādayo yathā svamupā-
dānāni, tadvikriyayā tadutpādāditi cet ? nanu sahakāritopādānate kimekaṃ tattvaṃ

'bhedo vā ? bhede kathaṃ bījasya janakatvam tābhyāmevāṅṅkarādīnāmupapatteḥ ? abhede vā
. kathaṃ bījasya na nānātvam, bhinnatādātmyāt | etayorvekatvamekatādātmyāt |

bhedānupapatteḥ | na cānupakārakāriṇo'pekṣanta iti tvayaivoktam | na ca kṣaṇasyopakāra
saṃbhavo'nyatra jananāt tasyābhedyatvāt | tathā cārthakriyāyā ekatvānekatvasāpekṣatvā-
napekṣatvavyāptatvāt | tṛtoyaprakāravirahās | anayoranyataraniṣedhasyānyatara vidhāna-

ca kramavatsahakārisamavadhānavaśāt krameṇa kāryāṇīti vyāpakānupalabdherasiddheḥ "

brūmaḥ – yathā sāmagrayā abhedaḥ, tathā kāryāṇāsapyabhedāt kathaṃ na kāraṇābhedānukāra: ?
nanu pratiniyatānekarūpāṇāṃ kāryāṇāmabheda iti keyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ ? yadyevaṃ na
khalu samagrebhyo bhinnā kācidadhyakṣagocaraḥ | saugatamate ca cinteyam | tato'bhinnā
sāmagrīti samagrā eva pratiniyatānekamūrtayo'bhinnā ityapi kīdṛśī vācoyuktiḥ ?

siddhaḥ kāraṇabhedād bhedaḥ |

1. yadvā rajñānaśrīmitra nibandhāvalau
bhedayoravyutpattireva 'buddhayanurodhādabhidhīyate | tattvatastu yathā kāraṇaṃ sāmagrī
vivakṣitā, tathā bhedābhedāvapi vaijātyāvaijātye vivakṣite iti darśitaprāyam |
nanvadyāpi na samagrebhyo'nyā sāmagrīti teṣāmeva samagrāṇāṃ sādṛśye vaisadṛśye
vā kāryāṇāṃ sādṛśyaṃ vaisadṛśyaṃ veti prāptam | evametat | na tu tatpuñjasthānāṃ parasparaṃ
sādṛśyādinirūpaṇam | kiṃ tu puñjāntarasthaiḥ saha svajātyapekṣayā senāyāḥ senāntareṇa
saha sādṛśyetaranirūpaṇavat | tatra yāvanto yādṛśā ekasāmagrī prajñaptigocarā arthā
hetusaṃmatāḥ, tāvantastādṛśā eva yadi deśakālāntaravartanastadāsau sadṛśī sāmagrī,
kāryaṃ ca sadṛśamasyā iti kāryaśabdenāpi puñja eva | yāvanti yādṛśāni kāryāṇi
jātānyekatra tāvanti tādṛśānyevānyatrāpi jāyanta ityarthaḥ | vaisadṛśye tu tāratamya
bhedena bhidyamāne kāryamapi tāratamyabhedena bhidyata ityapi kāryapuñjasyaiva tāratamyabhedena
vaisadṛśyamityarthaḥ | bhedamātravivakṣāyāmapyayameva nyāyaḥ | satyāṃ vipratipattau bhinnāyāḥ
sāmagrayā bhinnameva kāryaṃ bhavatīti etādṛśameva kāraṇabhedānuvidhānaṃ kāryasya
pramāṇānusāri | tadatikrame ca viśvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgatimavatarati | na pramāṇa-
bādhitasya ekakāraṇekakaraṇaniyamasthātikrame | tadiyaṃ bhedābhedānukaraṇavārtā naiyāyi
kānāṃ ‘gopamukhātpāyasamiṣṭatāśrutimanuharati |
tasmādekameva bījamaṅkurādikamanekaṃ janayati, evaṃ kṣityādikamapi pratyekam |
ato naikānekayorubhayorapi vyāvṛttiryato vyāpakānupalambho'yamaparaḥ kṣaṇika kṣetrapi

kiṃ ca yenaiva rūpeṇa bījamaṅkuramutpādayati kiṃ tenaiva kṣauṇīkṣaṇamiti paryanu-
yuñjānā : te'pi paryanuyujyante rūpaśabdena kimatra vivakṣitamiti ? kiṃ tāvat kalpanā-
talpaśāyino bhinnā iva bhāsamānā dharmāḥ kṛtakatvānityatvādivadaṅkuretarajanakatvādayaḥ

prāgiva paścādapi na janayedityādi ?

svarūpaśabdena vyavahṛtā rūpamityuktam | tatra' prathamapakṣe tāvanna paryanuyogasaṃgatiḥ |
kalpanānimitā hi dharmāḥ parasparaṃ dharmiṇaśca sakāśād vidyamānā iva bhānto'pi yathā
pratibhāsamasattvāt pramāṇasahatayā na kacit ' kriyāyāṃ karaṇabhāvabhājo bhavitumarhati |
yadeva hi svalakṣaṇamadhyakṣagocarīkṛtamanaṅgaṃ tata evānvayavyatirekābhyāmarthakriyāniṣpatti-
niścaye'pyanādivāsanāvaśādupajāyamāna vikalpacetasi tatastato vyāvṛttavastuvyavasāya-
balāvalambisaṃvādeṣu' 'dharmaṣvapoddhāreṇāsthāmasthāṃ kriyāyāmayamayaṃ dharma upayujyata iti

na vāryate | yathā prakāśe piśaṅgātmani pradopepyayamakhaṇḍenaiva rūpeṇa tamaso nāśamava-

prakāśapiśaṅgabhāvau bhinnau | vikalpacetasi tu bhinnavadbhāsamānāvekaikamapoddhṛtya bhinna-
kriyākaraṇatvena 'vyavasthitau vivakṣitau, [na vyavasthitau vā] na ca vivakṣāmātreṇa

pṛthvījanakena ca tatkaraṇamiti vyavahāre'pi tattvato naikasthāpyanekakarmaṇi niṣedho

sāpekṣasya karaṇamupakārābhāvāt | na nirapekṣasya, tena vinā karaṇāt | sthiraṃ ca
bījamakara jana venaiva rūpeṇa kṣitimutpādayati bhinnena vetyādi yadā visadṛśakṣityādi-
zanmopālambhaḥ pradīpo'pi cākṣaṇika eva bhavatām | tatra vartivikāratailakṣayā vekena
bhinnena vā rūpeṇaṃ kriyetāmiti samānam | yastu samādhi: sahakāriṇa eva bhinnāḥ
tasya svarūpabheda iti, evaṃ ca bruvatā paro'pyātmā ātmāpi para iti nivṛttedānīmātma-
parādiśabdebhyaḥ pratiniyatārthapratyāyanapratyāśā' | na ca devadattasya svarūpaṃ yajñadattaḥ

tadetadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayā'bhidhīyamānaṃ niyatamupahāsabhājanīkaroti |
sahakāriṇo'vadhīryaṃ ca svarūpaśabdavācyamarthaṃ pṛcchata : sahakāriṇottaramiti vyaktaṃ na
tena nānyena vātmanā janayati sthiro'pi bhāva iti niyatamanujñātaiva vyāpakānupa-

yogāt | ataeva śakyopanyāsatvamapi nānathaṃkyahetuḥ tādṛśasyāpyupanyāsāt

ddhāyāṃ śaṅkāmavakāśayati, na ca tatra viparyayabādhakasyāpi viśeṣa:, kevala' sāmā-
nyena kriyāvati jhaṇabhaṅgitayā vyāpteḥ siddhe'pi viśeṣe pravṛttyathina: saccedamitya-

mavaśyāśrayaṇīyaṃ vyāptisādhanāya, [25b] tadeva ca kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ svadharmiṇaḥ,
evaṃ sati sādhyadharmiṇyapi tadupanthasyaiva nirvṛtirālambyatām kimiyatā prayāsena

pratisandhātṛtvaṃ vocyata iti syādapi | prativiṣayamalabdhaviśeṣāyāṃ ca buddhau saṃbandho'pi
na viśeṣa vyavahārayitumīśaḥ, adhunā nibandhanādhigantā, adhunā phalasya, idānīṃ

kenaivaṃ pratārito'si ? aho mohamāhātmyaṃ yadīdṛśānapi paravaśīkaroti |
tathāhi nedamidamantareṇeti yaducyate tat khalvanyatra pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ sāmarthyāva-
dhāraṇe sati yujyate, vahnariva dhūme| cakṣurādivad vā dṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagra kāryādarśane

stīti vyaktam | dvitīyo'pi na saṃbhavī | nahi kāraṇabuddhisamanantaraṃ kāryabuddhau satyāṃ
niścayapravṛttasya idamasthānantaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mayeti pratisandhānamadṛṣṭapūrvaṃ, kadācid, yato'nyasya
sāmarthyaparikalpanaṃ syāt | evaṃ smaraṇamapyanubhavāt kutaścit paramparayā śaktipariṇāma-
dvāreṇa, kutaścit sākṣāt tat paripākabalāditi |
ra anyasyānubhave tarhi kathamanyasya na smṛtiḥ |

tāvataiva mūlyena turagatyāgino gardabhakrayaṇavṛttānta āśriyate ?

bhavati na vā ? yadi bhavatīti bhaṇasi, kimatra vaktavyamasmābhiḥ ? sabhyādayaḥ pramāṇam |

na hi dhūmaśaṃśapātvādayo'vastuni vasanti | tasmād yatra bhāvadharmaḥ sādhanaṃ tatra

yuktametat sattāsādhane | asattāsādhane tvavastudharmo heturavastuni vikalpamātra siddha
eva nāśrayāsiddhidoṣeṇa dūṣayituṃ śakyaḥ | na hi tasya vastvāśrayāpekṣā avastudharmādeva |

sādhyam | kramādiviraho hetuḥ | asya cābhāvadharmatvaṃ nāma svasādhyāvinābhāvitva-
mucyate', abhāvānāṃ śaśaśṛṅgādīnāṃ dharmo na bhāvānāmiti kṛtvā | tadanena vacasā
yāvat pramāṇāntareṇa pakṣe sādhyaṃ na sidhyati', na tāvaddhetorvyāptirityuktaṃ bhavati |
tacca kutra hetāvupalabdhamaneneti na vidmaḥ | yathā cānyatra sādhyanāntarīyakatā anyadā
pravṛtta pramāṇāntarasiddhā dṛṣṭāntena smāritā pakṣīkṛte sādhyasiddhayarthamupayujyate, nānyataḥ
sādhyasiddhimapekṣate, tathā kramādyabhāve'bhāvadharmatā vyāptisvabhāvānyadaiva kramākrameṇa
siddhatvasya | vyāptigrahaṇakāle pravṛttapramāṇasiddhākāśakamaladṛṣṭāntena smāritā
sādhyasiddhāvupayujyate, nānyataḥ sādhyasiddhimapekṣate | anyathā sarvānumānavaiyarthyāt |
kramayaugapadyena hi sattvasya vyāptisiddhau sattvasya vyāpyasyābhāvena' kramayogapadyasya
vyāpakasya viraho vyāptaḥ sidhyatītyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramayogapadyaviṣayaḥ |
vyāptirūpaṃ tathā pūrvameva niścitaṃ, sadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na pakṣe pramāṇāntareṇa sādhyasiddhayā
vyavasthāpyate, tathā kramākramābhāvābhāvenāpi sādhyaṃ prasādhya vyavasthāpyata iti naḥ
pakṣaḥ, pūrvameva vyavasthāpitatvāt | tat kuta itaretarāśrayatvam ?

teṣāmasattvasiddhiḥ asattvasiddhau cābhāvadharmatvasiddhiriti | viṣamadṛṣṭinā punarabhāva-

tarāśrayatvam ? naca pakṣadharmataivābhāvadharmatā, sādhyāvinābhāvarūpatvādabhāvadharmatāyāḥ |
atha yadyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramādyabhāvasya syāt, tadā pakṣīkṛtānāmasatāṃ nityānāṃ dharmaḥ
syādityabhiprāyāt 'pakṣadharmatāvyāpāradvāreṇa tadavyāpāro darśitaḥ, tathāpi cakrakaṃ
vaktumucitam | tadapi prācīnacarcayā carcitameva |
kiṃ ca, abhāvadharmatve vyāptirūpe sati pakṣadharmatvamiti nāyaṃ hetvantarasādhāraṇo
nyāyaḥ | na cāsyāpi hetorevam, abhāvadharmatvaṃ hi vyāptirbhavatu mā vā kramādivirahastu
kena nityānāṃ niṣidhyate ? na caite'pyasattārūpeṇa dharmiṇaḥ, kiṃ tu sadasatvasandeha-

vikalpa eva | sa hi nityagrāhī vikalpaḥ tadākārāntaramiva kramayogapadyadharmasaṃbandhe

tenaikajñānasaṃsargi śṛṅgamupalabdham harivarāṅge'pi tatsaṃbhāvanayaiva tatsaṃsargānniṣidhyate,
tathā nīlādāvapariniṣṭhitanityānityabhāve tāvat kramākramī svadharmiṇā sārdhamekajñāna-
saṃsargiṇī dṛṣṭī nitye'pi yadi bhavato nityagrāhiṇā jñānena svadharmiṇā nityena sahaiva
gṛhyeyātāmiti saṃbhāvanayaikajñānasaṃsargadvāraka evaṃ pratiṣedhamāviśataḥ |

dharmavyavasthānaṃ, yathā treguṇyasyaikatvaṃ viruddhaṃ dharma: prasādatāpadainyakriyā niyatā,
nairātmyetarayogo'niyataḥ, tathehāpi pūrvāparakālayorekātmatayā yadyakārakamakārakameva,
sarvadā kārakatve ca kārakatvameva nityaṃ, kramākramau tu kadācit kriyāśaktisvabhāvau,
yaugapadye hi vyaktamekadaiva karaṇamiti kādācitkakriyatvam, [42b] krame'pi kṛtāyāḥ

kādācitkākādācitkakriyatvayoḥ parasparaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayā virodha: siddha: 2 |
evaṃ sati pratiyogini nitye vikalpyamāne ekajñānasaṃsagilakṣaṇaprāpte viruddhasyā-
nupalabhyamānasya kramākramasya tadupalabdhirevānupalabdhiḥ | saiva vārthakriyāśakte-
rvyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | tasmād vyāpakadharmyupalabdhitayā na vyāpakānupalambhāntarādasya
viśeṣa: | yadi ca rdhātve'pi vastvavastutayā vibhāgo bhāgyahīnasya bhavato matimadyāpi
duḥsthayati, vastunyapi dharmaṇi ekatra pradeśa: kaṭhino dharmī dravarūpamanyatra jalamityādayo
vibhāgā bhaṅgavantastadanviṣyantaḥ 3 kena vāraṇīyāḥ ? tasmād vastvavastutayāpi bhedacintā
kopayoginī ?

kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye vyatirekādhikāra:
gṛhyatām | kevalaṃ paramparayā pratyakṣasyāpi janmaiva sākṣāt, vyavaharaṇaṃ tu vikalpā-
divyavadhānenaiva | anumānasya punarubhayamapi paramparayā | vyavahārāṇāmapi smṛtyabhi-
lāṣādinā vyavadhānāt | evaṃ vastvadhiṣṭhānatvamanumānera vyavadhānena duṣaṇameva |
• kevalamanumāne'pyanyatra sādhyadharmāpekṣayā yavyavadhānaṃ tato'tiriktamidaṃ vyāptigrahaṇā-
pekṣaṃ vartata iti dhāndhyaṃ dhiyaḥ | tatrāpi na sarvo'numānāntarasādhāraṇo'yaṃ dharmaḥ |
svasādhye hi sākṣātpratibandha mavadhūya viparyayavyāptyā gamakatvaṃ kāryakāraṇavyāpakānu-
palabdhiṣu | tadvad vastvadhiṣṭhānatvamapi yadi yathoktavyavadhānena viṣayaviśeṣe bhavet
kīdṛśo doṣaḥ, kasyacid bādhakasyābhāvāt ? dharmivikalpāpekṣayā tu na tāvato'pi
vyavadhānasya saṃbhavaḥ, [43a ] asādhāraṇī ca pratyāsattirdharmiṇo vikalpākāreṇa
sahekīkaraṇāt | nirākārapakṣe'pi hi vikalpāyattaprakāśatvādalīkanityākārasya
dharmiṇaḥ | tasmād dharmiṇo vastvadhiṣṭhāna paryeṣaṇaṃ pratyāsattiviśeṣāśrayatayā vikalpa -
vapuṣāpi kṛtārthībhavediti na doṣaḥ kaścit | ayameva nyāyo na vaktā bandhyāsutaścaitanyā-
bhāvāt, na kharaṃ kharaśṛṅgaṃ dravyatāviyogādityādau yojya:, nāvastuni virodha:
pratītyaviṣayatvādityādau 7 ca śaraṇam |
yadi pratītimātrāpekṣayā pratītyaviṣayatvaṃ tadā asiddhiḥ anubhavāpekṣayānekāntaḥ |
ityevaṃprakāradūṣaṇaparihāraśaktiḥ, na punarāśrayāsiddhayādidūṣaṇagaṇagaṇanā kācit |
etena vyāpakānupalabdhau hi vyāpyābhāvo'nyaḥ pratipattavya iti helayāpahastitam,
dharmirūpasya bhinnasya pratipattiviṣayasya pratipādāt, gaṇḍaśaile vṛkṣatvābhāvena śiśapā-
tvābhāvavat | tadevaṃ na prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhasya svarūpāsiddhiḥ, nityakramayaugapadyayoḥ
virodhapratipādanāt | yadāha, kramākramavirodha' iti tad vyāpakadvāreṇa punarartha
kriyāvirodhādityāha | nāpyāśrayāsiddhiravastuno'pi dharmitvapratipādanāt, vikalpena
pratipattipratipādanācca | ataeva śāstre,
tasya dharmaṇi pratyakṣato'numānato vā prasiddhiniścayaḥ
ityutsargasya parairanutpādyāpūrvarūpaṃ nakhādikaṃ sakṛt śabdādyahetutvādikamavastuni sādhya -
sādhanapratijñānamapavādo veditavya iti vyaktametat |

abhavanotpattereva saha sthitivirodhena bhāvapratiṣedharūpatvādityevaṃ prakāramabhidhānam,

kṣiptabhasmanātmānameva cchurayatīti mahāmohamagnatayā kṛpāpātraṃ mahatāmavagantavyaḥ |
yadyevaṃ bhavatāmadhyabhāvo vyavayite sa kiṃsvabhāvo yadi na vastu bhāvena vā satyaṃ na
virudhyata evāyam ? kathaṃ vā virodhadvayavyavasthā ko vāsya hetuḥ ? kādācitkatve
akādācitkatve ca bhāvasya samakālaṃ kathaṃ na vyavahriyate ? kathaṃ vā prāgiva paścādapi na
kṣaṇaparamparāprasava : ? prasave ca na sahaḥ sahānavasthāna virodhaḥ |

[1b] namo bhagavate vītarāgāya |
iha dahanādinā dhūmādervyāptiradhyakṣānupalabdhisādhana tadutpattilakṣaṇeti vyutpādyate |
pare hi purastanāstāvadagnimati dhūmasya darśanamadarśanaṃ ca tadvirahiṇītyevānvayavyatirekitvaṃ
kalpayāmbabhūvuḥ | tatra darśanādarśanaṃ yādṛcchikamapi sakṛd bhavediti ca bhūyaḥ pravṛtti
mapekṣate | nanu bhūyasāpi pravṛtte darśanādarśane ghaṭakulaṭādāvupalabdho vyabhicāra iti
cet ? kimetāvatā, tatrāpyanumānamastvityucyate, atha tadvad dhūmādāvapi mā bhūditi ?
prathamapakṣastāvad vyabhicārādeva nirasta: | dvitīyo'pyavyabhicārādeva | na hyanyasya
vyabhicāre dhūmasya kiñcit | na khalu viṣānamaniṣṭamiti bhakṣyāntaramapi heyamastu |
tāvatā ca sarvā nivṛttilabdheti kimutpattiprārthanayā, tanni [śca] yopayoginā vā pratyakṣā-
nupalambhena ? tadutpattirapi yadi darśanādarśanādeva gṛhyeta kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? anumānameva
ca vibhāgena bhavatviti tadanveṣaṇam | sa ca vibhāgo vyabhicārāvyabhicāradvāreṇa
siddhaḥ | asati ca vyabhicāre tāvataiva gamakatvam, anarthakā tadutpattiḥ | vyabhicāre ca
śatamapi tadutpattayo na samarthāḥ | tasmāt sannikarṣeṇa paryeṣaṇaṃ saṃyogenaiva kṛtārtham | ataeva
saṃyogī heturucyate vardhūmo na kāryamiti |
trilocanastvāha, pratyakṣānupalambhayoviśeṣaviṣayatvāt kathaṃ tābhyāṃ sāmānyayoḥ

aprakṛtameva kiñcit ?

vartināviṣyete, tadānyāveva vā ? tattve taddūṣaṇasyāvaśyamanuvṛtteviphalo'bhyupagamaḥ |
anyatve'pi taddūṣaṇavad guṇasyāpyananuvṛtteḥ | api nāma bhedapakṣabhāvi pṛthakpratītiprasaṅga-
dūṣaṇamabhedamupagacchan parihariṣyāmīti bhede'pyabhedasvīkārastatra bhavataḥ | yadi ca sa
evābhedaḥ pṛthagupalabdhibādhano'dhunāpyupanītaḥ syādevaṃ tatparihāraḥ kevalamekayogakṣema-
samāveśāt pramāṇāntarāvṛttimapyākarṣat | tato yadyanyatayaināṃ nākarṣet, tata eva
pṛthagupalabdhiniṣedhanamapi na sādhayet | athābhedasya pṛthagupalabdhibādhava phalaṃ na
śabdāntarāvṛttisvābhāvyāt, tathāpi dvaitābhyupagamo viphalaḥ | evaṃ bhedapakṣe'pi vācyam |
atha pṛthagupalabdhibādheva phalamabhedasya, śabdāntarāvṛttinivṛttistu bhedasyaiva tenāpi hi
saṃbhavinā svakāryamarjanīyameva | evaṃ bhedasthāpi pramāṇāntarāpekṣeva phalaṃ, pṛthagupa-
labdhibādhā tvabhedasyeti |
ucyate | ubhayamubhayasya kārya dṛṣṭaṃ bhedasyāpi pṛthakprakāśaprasaṅgadoṣaḥ,
śabdāntarāpekṣā ca guṇaḥ | abhedasyāpi śabdāntarāpekṣāprasaṅgadoṣaḥ, apṛthakpratibhāsaśca
guṇaḥ | tatredānīṃ bhedena śabdāntaravṛttimātramātanvatā sthātavyam | dvitīye tu kārye

aniyamena punaḥ prapātapatanaprasaṅgāditi vyaktamiṣṭakāmatāmātrā pahṛtahṛdayo na kiñcit
cetayata ityupekṣāmarhati | na hi tadicchātiriktamatra kāraṇamākalayāmaḥ | api ca, yadā
bhedasya paścād bhedābhyupagamaḥ, tadā pṛthagupalabdhi bādhamānasyābhedasya dvitīyaṃ kāryaṃ
kena nivāryatām ? bhedeneti cet - na, yadyanyenottarakālabhāvinā tadāsyāpi doṣāṅga-
nirākaraṇāyāparī mṛgyata ityanavasthā | atha prāktanena, tasya yadyetāvatī śaktiḥ
paścādabhedenopanīyamānamapṛthakpratibhāsameva kathaṃ na baghnīyāt ? tad yadi pūrvāpekṣayā
uttarasyāpavādakatvaṃ pūrvatarāpekṣayā kathaṃ neti cintyam | tasmāt pratyekamubhayakārya-
bhedābhedaparīkṣā
tvād bhedābhedayorekapratiniyataḥ parihāra: svīkāro vetyanibandhanametat | tataḥ pṛthak
pratibhāsāpratibhāsau sahotpattyanutpattī śabdāntaravṛttyavṛttyādayaścaikasyaikadā prasajyeran |
na copādherupādhimaṃto bhedenānubhavagandho'pi samasti | vyaktivināśe vā vināśaleśo'pi
na sāmānyasyābhyupeyate paraiḥ |
vyaktirūpeṇeṣyata eveti cet ? nanu vyaktirūpeṇeti na nijena rūpeṇeti
vivakṣitam, anyathā viśeṣaṇānarthakyāt | nijasyaiva rūpasya bhedābhedacintāyāmayaṃ
prasaṅga iti kimanena parihṛtam ? atha nijamasya na rūpāntaraṃ saṃbhavatyeva, kasya tarhi
bhedābhedacinteti siddhā nirupādhayo dharmā: | nanu bhinnasyābhedasaṃbhave'pi na śabdāntara-
vaiyarthyaṃ vidma iti kimatra kurma: ? evaṃ tarhi bhinnasyāpyupādherna bhinna : prakāśa iti
kimatra kurma iti bruvato naikāntavāde'pi doṣa iti tathāpi vyartho dvaitamatāśrayaḥ, paryaṃnte
pādaprasārikāyā [2b] aparihārāt | pariśramātiśayastvatiricyate, āhopuruṣikā
vā ? athāpi syāt tādātmyamabhyupagacchato yadā śabdāntarāvṛttyādidoṣaḥ pare:
prasajyate, tadā bhedasthāpi saṃbhavaḥ parihāraḥ | bhede ca pratibhāsabhedāpādane'bhedopanaya
iti na śakyamekāntavāde | na ca pādaprasāriketi nāpyubhayadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ | yadā hi pūrva
bheda upanītaḥ, tadā tadāsaṅgidoṣotkhāte cābhedasyopanayāt |
evaṃ punaḥ punastadāvartanaparamparayā paryavasānābhāve'pi na kṣatiriti cet ?
bhavatopanīyamānastarhi bādhako dharmaḥ sādhako vā na svasāmarthyenaivetyāpannam | upanayaśca
vacanātmanyanabhidhīyamāno bhavata uṣarbudho'pi na bādhakaḥ syāt | etena mayā prasaṅgārtha-
manaṅgīkārādityapi nirastam | na hi jīvanāya bhakṣyamāṇaṃ viṣaṃ na hinastīti śakyam |
tasmād bhautārgalayugalasamānametadubhayaparijihīrṣayobhayapakṣālambanaṃ mandamedhasā-
miti |
prayogaḥ, yad yanmātranimittaṃ tat tasmin sati bhavatyeva, yathā cakṣurādi-
sāmagrīmātranimittaṃ jñānajanma, bhedābhedamātrāpekṣaṃ ca yathoktadoṣajātamiti svabhāvahetuḥ |
tanmātranimittatvamanyānapekṣatvena vyāptam, tatsaṃbhave'pi ca tadabhāve tadviruddhamanyā-
pekṣatvaṃ syāditi vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhyā viparyayānnivartamānaṃ tanmātranimittatvaṃ tasmin
sati bhāve niyamyata iti vyāptisiddhiḥ | nāpyasiddhistanmātrāpekṣāyāḥ | na hyabheda -
mātrātiriktaṃ sahotpādanimittamupapadyate | bhedamātrātiriktaṃ vā pṛthakprakāśasya dṛśyatve |MATERYA
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
ayoguḍadahanayoḥ kṣīrodakayorvā bhede'pyabhavan prakāśabheda itarasāpekṣaḥ siddha iti
cet –na, abhrāntendriyajñānasya prakṛtatvāt | tatra bhinne eva vastunī ekīkṛtya pratipadyamānaṃ
jñānaṃ kathama bhrāntaṃ nāma ?
etena candradvayapratibhāso vyākhyātaḥ | athobhayakāraṇārabdhamekameva tad vastu
saṃjātamiti matiḥ, tadā vyabhicāra eva nāstīti siddhaṃ tanmātrāpekṣatvam | syādetat |
tanmātrāpekṣasyāpi tadbhāvenāvaśyambhāvaḥ yathā kaṭukamadhuradravyabhāvinorapi pitta-
ileṣmaṇoḥ | tadayuktam, vīryavipākāpekṣayāpi tadatatkāryakaraṇasaṃbhavād dravyāṇām,
rasamātrāpekṣātipātāt pittāderiti ||

siddhānte viprakīrṇasyānupalambhasya yādṛśī |
rūpaniṣṭheha tādṛśyā: saṃgrahaḥ kriyate sphuṭaḥ ||
pratiṣedhe sādhye'nupalabdhistṛtīyaṃ liṅgam | tacca yadyapalabdhivirahamātraṃ tat kathaṃ
kasyacit pratipattiḥ, pratipattiheturvā ? tasyāpi vā kathaṃ pratipattiḥ ? tasmādabhakṣyādi-
vat paryudāsavṛtyā anyopalabdhirevānupalabdhiḥ |
tatrāpi yadyanyamātrasya, tadaikasya
kapilabdha sarvasya niṣedhaprasaṅgaḥ | iṣyata eva tādātmyaniṣedhaḥ sarvasyeti cet ?
taddeśaniṣedho'pyanivāryaḥ | tadayaṃ viśeṣaḥ,
vedye yatra hi yanmatiniyamata: [3a] syādvā na vā tasya dhī-
riṣṭā no'nupalabdhiranyavirahajñāna sthiterāśrayaḥ ||
[yatra] vedyamāne yasya matiḥ syāditi deśakālasvabhāvaviprakarṣāṇāṃ niṣedha: | niyame-
neti, upalambhakāra [kā]ntaravaikalyasya | etena dṛśya viśeṣaṇaprāptasya bhāvajñāna sthitiriti
darśitam | ato na sarvasya niṣedhaprasaṅgaḥ | yatra ca vedyamāne yanmatiniyamena syāt,
tasyaiva dhīriṣṭā'nyasya dvitīyasyābhāvaniścaya prabandhākṣepāya kṣameti | etena na virahamātram,
paryudāsavṛttyā tvanyaviśeṣabuddhirityuktam atra ca tasyaivaikākina iti sāmarthyāt,
anyathetarasyāniṣiddhopalabdherabhāvāsiddheḥ |
tadyathā, neha ghaṭa upalabhyasyānupalabdheḥ | yathā kacit kiñciditi | tatra
dṛśyasyeti svabhāvaviśeṣa upalambhapratyayāntarasākalyaṃ coktaṃ draṣṭavyam | anupalabdheriti
pratiyogina upalabdherityarthaḥ | tacca pratiyogī hetvādhāraprāptaṃ bhūtalamanyad vaikendriya-
jñānasaṃsargi, tadanyo vā ? yasmin vedyamāne niṣedhya upalabhyameveti sāmānyokteḥ |
tatra yadi bhūbhāga upalabhya eva kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ sādhyaḥ, tadā sa eva pratiyogī kimanyā-
pekṣayā ? yadā tu nabhasi tadāpi tadevālokasaṃjñitam, anyo vā ghaṭādira niyata sthitiḥ
spṛśyaniṣedhe tvayameva |jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
etenaikajñānasaṃsargī pratiyogī vyākhyātaḥ | kacit punaranyathāpi, yathā pradīpaṃ
kavalayaturneha raso dṛśyānupalabdheriti sparśa eva pratiyogī | tayohiṃ satornaikarūpaniyatā
pratyāsattiḥ pānakavat | dūrād rūpadarśane'pi tarhi kathaṃ rasaniṣedho na bhavati, deśavipra-
karṣiṇa upalambhayogyatāyā abhāvāt, prāpyakāritvād ghrāṇarasanasparśanānām | uktaṃ ca,
yasmin vedyamāne yadavaśyaṃ vedyata eveti | nāpi rasānubhave rūpaniṣedhaḥ, tadāpi tallakṣaṇā-
yogāt | evaṃ śabdopalabdhāvapi na rūpaniṣedhaḥ | samandhakāre hi sato'pi rūpasya
jñānāvyabhicāriṇī na śabdavittiḥ |
āloke tu na tāvad dṛśyamānasyaiva niṣedhaḥ | adṛṣṭasya tu yogyasya niṣedhe'pi na
doṣa:, tallakṣaṇātyāgāt | etena devakulādau paridṛśyamāne taddeśabheryāderevābhāvasiddhirnā -
vaśyaṃ śabdāntarapratītimāpekṣeti darśitam | na tayoḥ sahapratītiniyama iti ceti |

evamekendriyajamanyad vā ?

1. atra pāṭho 'luptaḥ |
anupalabdhi rahasyam
pratiyogivirahavikalpajananāya | tatra yathā samānendriyasaṃsargijñānamanyābhāvaniścaya-
samartham, tathānyadapi sati sattve'vyabhicaritavyo'rthāntarajñānākāravirahīti na kaścid
viśeṣaḥ |
kathamiti cet ? nātrecchānicchayo: sāmarthyam | yasya tu yadanvayavyatirekānu-
kārastayorhetuphalabhāvādyupagamaḥ | yathā bhūtalaikākāraniyamāt tu jñānamanyaniṣedha-
vikalpenānukṛtānvayavyatirekaṃ, tathā pradīpamānane kṣipataḥ sparśākāramātra niyamād
rasābhāvajñānena ta[j] jñānam | na hyanayorutpattau vyavadhānāvyavadhānavibhāgaḥ |
tathānupādhike payasi praṇihitaghrāṇasyāsparśanadarśanasyāpi vikalpa eva gandhāntaram
ananubhavato'pi gandhākārajñānena tadākāraśūnyaḥ |
tatra
laiṅgikaṃ taditi cet –na, vyavadhānābhāvādabhyāsadaśāvataḥ | yatpratipattāveva hi
yaniścayo na sa laiṅgikaḥ pratyakṣasiddho vā yathā nīlaṃ na pītamiti | asti ca sanni-
hite payasi ghrāṇapraṇidhānamātrākāravikalpavato nāsti gandha iti niścayaḥ |
gandhajñānābhāvamātrasyāsādhanatve yadi niyatākāravikalpānubhavo na hetuḥ, pītābhāva-
jñānasyāpi mā bhūnnīlānubhava: | atra vā pratyakṣapauruṣamāmanato duṣpariharaṃ paratrāpi |
tadeva ca pratyakṣamekasya niṣedhyāpekṣayānupalabdhirucyate yathā tathoktam | tacca mūḍhaṃ
pratipattāramadhikṛtya pūrvasamayānusāreṇa dharmaviśeṣe'bhāvaṃ niścāyayalliṅgam | amūḍhasya
punarabhāvavato'nantarasaṃśayavinākṛtaḥ sthira evāsau niścaya iti pratyakṣapravattita
ucyate |
nanu na pratyakṣakṛtaḥ kaścidabhāvavyavahāraḥ, nāpi pratyakṣamarthābhāvaniścayena
phalavaduktam, kiṃ tu jñānābhāvaniścayenaiva | taddvāreṇaiva tvarthābhāvaniścayamantarbhāvayati iti
pratyakṣakṛtaḥ sa ucyate | sa ca tatsāmarthyajanmāpyanantaraṃ saṃśayena bhavatā paribhūyamāno mūḍhaṃ
prati laiṅgikaḥ | na hi jñānasyeva prakāśarūpaniyamo'rthasyetyadṛṣṭasyāpi sthiteravirodhāt
dṛśyānupalabdhiḥ śaraṇam | amūḍhasya tu vyāpakānupalabdhi: daśyasattāyāṃ darśanaviṣayatvena
vyāpteḥ | etadvivecanāsāmarthyāt tu prācyo mūḍha ityeke |
tadayuktam | yathā hi jñānamaprakāśamanavasthāyi tathā dṛśyaṃ bahirapīti tadvadeva
[4a] pratyakṣeṇānivāryavirahavyavahāram, kevalaṃ jātyaiva jñānaṃ dṛśyam | bahistu kiñcit
kathaścit kadācit | tatrābhyāsaviśeṣavataḥ pratipatturjñānāntarasāmānya iva bāhya-
viśeṣe'pi pratyakṣamātrādeva jhagiti niṣedhasiddhirasakṛdanubhūyamānā kathamapotuṃ śakyā ?

[pra. vā. 4. 270]
jñānāntaraniṣedha eva sāmarthyamuktamanubhavaścaivameveti cet –na, yathā hīdaṃ nopalabha iti
pratyakṣādanubhūyate, tathedaṃ nāstītyapi jhagityevābhyāsavataḥ | anabhyāsavatastu jñānābhāva

vyavasyantīkṣaṇādeva sarvākārānmahādhiyaḥ |
[pra. vā. 2. 107]
ityuktam | mṛduprajñādhikāreṇa ca sthānasthāneṣu yatnaḥ | tasmāt paṭudhiyaḥ pratyakṣādeva

pravṛttiḥ | pratyakṣāpāṭava eva hyanumānaṃ prārthyate | tatpāṭavaṃ ca vikalpajananenāvasthāpyate,

duṣparihara : pratyakṣasyābhāvavyavahāraśaktisaṃbhavaḥ, pratiṣedhastu sarvatrānupalambhāditi tu na
pratyakṣapratikṣepaḥ, kiṃ tu liṅgāntarasya dvāveva vidhisādhanāviti yathā | tadayamambhasi
gandhaniṣedhaḥ pratyakṣakṛta evāvyavadhairna laiṅgikaḥ | ki cātra liṅgaṃ gandhābhāvāvyabhicāri ?
jñānakāryānupalabdhiriti cet ? yadā svagrāhijñānaṃ kāryahetustadedaṃ yuktamapi yadā tu
pratyakṣameva tat, tadā pratyakṣayogyasya tannivṛttiryadi na dṛśyānupalabdhirghaṭasyāpi mā bhūt |
tadidaṃ pratiyogijñānarūpatālocanavañcanāphalameva | [4b] ayaṃ ca vādī
yadīndriyasādguṇyamaniścinvannetadāha, tadā sannapi gandhādirnopalabhyata ityāyātam |
atha niścinvannalaṃ kāryānupalabdhyeti draṣṭavyam | parokṣasaṃbhāvite ca kāraṇādau kāryādya-
nupalabdhi yatnena yojayati, saṃprati ca doṣaleśabhayāt pratyakṣasaṃbhāvite'pi saṃśeta
itītyasaṃbaddham | tasmāt sthitametat, yasmin vedyamāne yadavaśyaṃ vedyata eva tasyābhinne-
ndriyagrāhyasyānyasya vānindriyagrāhyasya vā buddhiranupalabdhiḥ | sā ca vyavahārameva sādha-
yati, anyathā pratyakṣasiddheḥ | tadarthaṃ ca virajñānasya sthiteḥ sthairyasyāśraya ityuktam | na
tu virahaniścayasyeti | yathā ca niyatasahopalambhayorekajñānamanyaniṣedhāya, tathā
niyatāsahopalambhayorityāha na veti | vedye yatra hi yanmatiniyamato na syādityarthaḥ |
yathā nīlamidamanīlaṃ na bhavatīti | atrāpi vyavahāra eva sādhya: | etena paraspara-
parihāra sthitilakṣaṇo virodho vyākhyātaḥ |
nanu yasminnavedyamāne yanmatiniyamena bhavituṃ saṃbhāvyata ityanenaiva gatametat |
adṛśyo'pi hi tādātmyena niṣedhyamāno dṛśyatayā saṃbhāvita eva niṣidhyate | anyathā
dṛśyādṛśyatayā svayameva bhedābhyupagamāditi kimanena pṛthagvacaneneti cet ? evaṃ tarhi
na vā syādityayamabhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsalakṣaṇo vyākhyāyate | pravṛttāpi yanmatiyaṃtra vedye sati
niyamena nivartata ityartha: | niyamaśca sattābādhane'bhāva eva yuktaḥ | yathā neha
śītamagneriti | etena sahānavasthānalakṣaṇo virodho vyākhyātaḥ |
nanvandhakāre niyamenānupalambha iti nāvaśyaṃ viruddhaparigraha iti cet ?
naikapratipattrapekṣaṃ lakṣaṇametat kiṃ tu sāmānyena | asti ca nirālokasyāpi rūpasya
darśanaṃ kaiścit tenāpi vā saṃbhāvyamañjanaviśeṣādineti | sattocchede tu niyama
evetyadoṣaḥ | nanvatrāpi śītaṃ yadi syāt, nāgnerekarūpaniyatā pratipattiriti kathaṃ
pūrvato viśeṣa: ? naivaṃ sparśanāgamye niṣedhasyābhimatatvāt | tarhi pravṛttāvapi śītasya
buddhiragnau vedye sati niyamānnivṛtteti pratyetumaśakyaṃ na [viruddham], anyadaitatpratīteḥ188

vivakṣitatvāt | tarhi prāggṛhītavirodhasmaraṇavyavahitavyāpāratvānnaṃ pratyakṣasya pravṛtti
to'bhāvaniścayaḥ syāt | mā bhūt, kevalaṃ vyavadhāne'pi tathā vi[ruddha] buddhirevābhāva-
niścayāṅgaṃ nānyamātrasyetyanupalabdhivyavasthānibandhanasya na kṣatiḥ |

tadvati vā gośabdasaṅketa ityarthaniṣṭhāyāṃ sa eva doṣaḥ, gavāparijñāne gotvasāmānyāṃ-
parijñānāt, gotvasāmānyāparijñāne gośabdavācyāparijñānāt | atha gotve tadvati vā
gośabda itīdṛśākṣareṇa yadi saṅka tastadā doṣaḥ | yadā tu [9b] puraḥ sthitaṃ piṇḍameka-
mupada deśakālāntaraviprakīrṇāśeṣavyaktisādhāraṇarūpa vikalpasthāyinaṃ prakaraṇāde:
pratipattāramavadhāryāyaṃ gauriti saṅketaḥ, tadā yatraivāsau tat sādhāraṇaṃ rūpaṃ nirūpayati
tameva gośabdena vyavaharatīti kathaṃ mithaḥ prārthanādoṣa: ? tāvatā ca gotve tadvati vā saṅketa
iti vyākhyātṝṇāṃ siddhāntānuvāda eṣaḥ, na tu saṅke takatṛ ṇāmupadeśakramastādū giti cet ?
evaṃ tarhi yadyagavāpoḍhe gośabda itīdṛśākāraṃ sa tākārakīrtanaṃ tadā'yaṃ doṣaḥ |
yadā tu vivakṣitavyaktiṣvekākārapratyavamarśavartini prakaraṇādavadhārite pratipattari
saṅketakaraṇamayaṃ gauriti, tadā ka doṣāvakāśaḥ ? sa hi svavikalpatalpaśāyinī: sakala-
vyaktīragovyāvṛttādyakṣaramanapekṣya svayaṃ tadvijātīyāśeṣavyaktivyāvṛttā gośabdavācyāḥ
pratipadyamāno yatraiva vijātīyavyāvṛti pratipadyate tā eva gośabdena vyavaharatīti,
tāvatā agovyāvṛtte gośabda iti siddhāntānuvāda eva na saṅketākāraḥ, abhimate
gośabdavṛttāvagośabdena śeṣasyābhidhātuṃ śakyatvāt | sa tu vijātīyavyāvṛttaḥ sādhā-
raṇākāro vikalpe sāmānyasya pratibhāso vyaktervā svātmaiveti paścānniśceṣyate |
itaretarāśrayastu nāstīti siddham | siddhaṃ ca puṇḍarīkaśabdaśrutau śvetaśatapatrapratipattivad
gośabdaśrutāvapyagavāpoḍhapratītau jātivādināpyavaśyābhyupagantavyamapohaviśeṣaṇaśemuṣī-
nāntarīyakatvaṃ vidheriti | na ca saṃbandhagandhamātraṃ sākṣādeva dvayoḥ pratītirmukhyopa-
sarjanabhāveneti bhedaḥ | dharmavācī vā guṇaśabdaḥ, anyāpohadharmaṇo vidhirūpasya
pratīteḥ |
yat tṛtīyākārasyāropitabāhyayoranyanivṛttikṛtaṃ sādṛśyaṃ dūṣayan vācaspati-
rāha'. –naca svalakṣaṇadharmo vyāvṛttirbhavadbhirabhyupeyata iti tad duṣṭameva | atha bhāvi-
kīti vivakṣitaṃ tatreti cet ? tathāpi nopayoga:, kalpanārūḍhasyaiva dharmidharmabhāvasyeṣṭa
tvāt | kevalaṃ kiṃ na vidhinaiva vyapadeśa: pratyakṣasyāpi vā parāpohaviṣayatvavyavahāra-
prasaṅga ityavaśiṣyate |
atra bramaḥ | iha kācid vyavasthā tattvaleśamāśritya prayojanaviśeṣādanyathā
sthitāvapyanyathā kriyate, yathātmatadutpāda iti | utpādo hi prāgabhāvaviśiṣṭasya vastunaḥ

apohaprakaraṇam
sata eva dharmaḥ | atha ca prāgabhāvalakṣaṇatattvaleśamāśrityāsata iti vyavasthāpyate
satkāryavādaśaṅkāsaṅkocāya | yathā vā'nenaiva kṛtaṃ karma ko'nyaḥ pratyanubhaviṣyatotyeka
santānaprajñaptimāśritya kṛtanāśākṛtābhyāgamavañcanā vimohāya tathādyāpi vidhiviṣayā-
bhidhānaṃ [10a] vastuto vastuna eva parāropitavācyatāsvīkāraśaṅkānirākaraṇāya
nāntarīyakapratītir[pya ] poha eva vikalpaviṣaya iti vyavasthāpyate | atona vidhinaiva
vyavahāraḥ | yadā tvapoha eva mukhyārtha: śabdasyetyāropaḥ, tadā vidhirapi puraskriyate |
yathoktam,
śabdestāvanmukhyamākhyāyate'rthaṃ iti |
pratyakṣe tu vivādābhāvānnaivaṃ vyavastheti yuktam | anyāpohaviśeṣaṇaṃ tu vidhistatrātiśayo
netyuktameva | śāstraṃ hi,
yathā vā
tat paricchinatti tato'nyad vyavacchinattītyādi |
niṣedhyāpekṣayā tu tatrānupalabdhiśabdena niṣedhavyāpāra : puraskriyata eva |
[vidhivṛ]tteragrahaṇaṃ nāma prasajyapakṣe niyatarūpānubhavādabhāvavikalpotpādanaśaktireva,
tathā vidhivikalpānāmapi tantre'nurūpānuṣṭhānadānaśaktireva niṣedhagrahaṇamagnirmaṃyā pratīta
ityanuvyavasāyaprasavaśaktiśca | paryudāsapakṣe ca niyatasvarūpasaṃve[da]namevobhayatra niṣedha-
grahaṇam | ubhayaṃ caitadabhimataṃ śāstrakārasya | kacit tasya prastāvānurūpaṃ prasajya-
pratiṣedhādhikāreṇa,
rūpe tasya na kiñcanetyādīni
vacanāni, kacit tvatadrūpaparāvṛttavastumātraprasādhanādityādīni paryudāsāśrayāṇi |
natvekaniyamaḥ | tato yaṭṭīkākāraḥ svāpohasiddhau tadarthāvatārataralastrilocanaścā-
vocatām ācāryaḥ prasajyapratiṣedhavallabha unnīyata iti tannirākṛtam | na ca bhedābhāvāt
viśeṣaṇavyavahārahāniḥ, rāhoḥ śiraḥ gotvaṃ sāmānyamityādivad vivakṣākṛtasya
anapāyāt | kiṃ ca vyavahriyata eva bhavatāpi ghaṭābhāvapradeśayoḥ piśācatvābhāva-
stambhayorvā viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhāvaḥ | tat kathamasmākaṃ niṣedhe niḥsvabhāvābhāvavādi-
tvāditi cet ? nedānīṃ svarūpanirūpaṇamabhāvasya, kiṃtu pratītinirūpaṇam | sā ca
śakyā apahnotum | paryudāsapakṣe'pi tadvidhirevānyaniṣedha iti na pratītikṣatiḥ |
nāpi viśeṣaṇabhāvasya | anenaiva vākyena vidhiniṣedhayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyapradarśanāt |206
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
ataeva virodhacodyamapyavadyaṃ na, svābhāvena hi vidhevirodho, nānyābhāvena, sahaiva sthānāt |
tasmād yuktamuktam,
tatrāpohastadguṇatvena gamya iti |
athavā tasyārthākhyānasya guṇo'yameva yadanyaniṣedhanaṃ nāma, tenāsau gamyata iti
vyavahartavyam | yacchāstram, tadanyaparihāreṇa pravarteteti śabdaniyogaḥ, vyartho'nyathā-
prayogaḥ sthāditi | etena tātparyārthatvamapohasya darśitamavyāpitvaparihāraśca | eṣa panthāḥ
śrughnamupatiṣṭhata ityatrāpi prakṛtapathāntarāpekṣayaiṣa eva | śrughnapratyanīkāniṣṭasthānāpekṣayā
śrughnameva | araṇyamārgavadvicchedābhāvādupatiṣṭhata eva | sārthadūtādivyavacchedena panthā
eveti sulabho niyama:' | tarjanīnirdeśād gatārthaḥ panthā eveti cet ? paravyavacchedaḥ
tāvadastīṣṭaśca | prayogastu gatārthasyāpi loke dṛśyata eva | abhyāgacchati, [10b]
brāhmaṇau dvāvityādivat | yathā hi sārthapuruṣādivyavacchedena kaḥ panthāḥ śrughnamupatiṣṭhata
iti praśnaḥ, tathottaramapyeṣa panthā iti | sarvatraiva hi pratipādyaśaṅkāṅkitasyaiva vidhi-
pratiṣedhāviti | yadi ca śabdaśrutikāle kalito na parāpohaḥ kathamanyaparihāreṇa
pravṛttiḥ ? tato gāṃ badhāneti codito'śvādīnapi baghnīyāt |
yattu goḥ pratītau na tadātmā parātmeti sāmarthyādanyāpohaḥ paścānniścīyata iti
matam - tadasaṅgatam, prāthamikasyāpi pratotikramādarśanāt | na hi tatkālavyutpanna -
saṅketo'pi gāmānayetyuktaḥ parato nivṛttāvarthāpattimanusarati | na ca gośabdādanyāva-
korṇapratipattau goniścayo yuktaḥ | tathā pratipattau vā paścādapi kathamarthāpatterudayaḥ ?
pararūpaparikarī hi gaurgṛhītaḥ | kathaṃ sa tadanākīrṇatāsamarthane samartha : ? tasmād goḥ
pratītirityago'poḍhapratipattirucyate | ataḥ svārthapratītikāla evārthāntarāpohasya pratīti-
kālaḥ, candraprayoge candrapratītikālavadavadātatāyāḥ | yathā ca śuklimāpratītau kīdṛśīndu-
pratītiḥ, pararūpasaṅkīrṇapratītāvapi kīdṛśī gopratītiriti samānam | nāpi na saṅkīrṇa
nāsaṅkīrṇamavagantuṃ śakyaṃ vastu, paścādapi sāmarthyasyāśakyatvācca | tasmānna niṣedha -
bodhāyārthasāmarthyālambanaṃ śreyaḥ |

tāsāṃ [ca] tadvatīnāṃ rūpamatajjātīyavyāvṛttamityarthaṃtastadavagatergā badhāneti codito

iti | evamapohasya vācyatāvyavasthāyāṃ nimittānyabhidhīyamānāni śāstre'pohasya
śabdānmukhyasphuraṇavirodhīnyūhanīyāni bhāvavāciṣu | abhāvavācakādhikāre cāyameva
mukhyo viveka ityuktam | bhāvavāciṣūpasarjanatayā vivekasyāmukhyatāṃ khyāpayati | viśeṣato
hyeṣa boddhavyaḥ | abhāvavāciṣu padārtha evāpohaḥ | bhāvavāciṣu punaḥ padārthasyānyataḥ
apohaḥ, padārtha[va]ccānyasya | enayoścoktimātreṇa bheda iti | yadi tathāvidhanibandhanā-
dhīnā'pohasya vācyatāvyavasthā, artha eva tu mukhyamākhyāyate, hanta tarhi sarvadharmānabhi-
lāpyatāsamayo'stamayamāyātaḥ, tadarthaśca samārambha iti sūcitam |
yaccoktaṃ vastuvācyatāropaniṣedhārthamapohasya prādhānyenābhidhānavyavastheti, tatrāpi
svayamarthavācyataiva svīkriyate, parasya tvanyathopadiśyata iti mahatī prekṣatetyāśaṅkayāha,
arthaścaika ityādi |
ayamarthaḥ, artho hi dvividhaḥ bāhya āntaraśca anyasyābhāvāt | tatraikastāvad bāhyaḥ
adhyavasāyādeva vācyo vyavasthāpyate, na svalakṣaṇaparisphūrtyā | kathamiti cet ?
anubhavādeva | yathā hi pratyakṣacetasi deśakālāvasthāniyatāni parisphuṭarūpāṇi
svalakṣaṇāni pratibhāntyanubhūyante, tathā na vikalpakāle | vikalpakāle hi vijāti-

anubhavaviṣayaḥ | yacchāstram,

vastubhedaḥ, na ca pratibhāsabhedādapara: svarūpabhedaḥ | anyathā trailokyamekameva vastu syāt' |
nanu dūrāsannadeśavartinorekatra śākhini spaṣṭa spaṣṭapratibhāsabhede'pi na [śākhi] bhedaḥ,
arthakriyābhedābhāvādityarthaṃkriyābhedopakṛta eva pratibhāsabhedo bhedakaḥ |

bhāgiti cet ? na brumaḥ pratibhāsabhedo bhinnavastuniyataḥ kiṃ tu ekaviṣayatvābhāva-
niyata iti | [11b] tathā hi, yo yaḥ kacid vastuni pratyakṣa pratibhāsād viparītaḥ
pratibhāso nāsau tenaikaviṣayaḥ, yathā ghaṭagrāhakāt paṭapratibhāsaḥ, yathā vā śaṅkhagrāhakāt
pītapratibhāsaḥ | tathā ca gavi pratyakṣapratibhāsād viparītaḥ pratibhāso vikalpakāle
iti vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhi: | ekaviṣayatvaṃ hi pratibhāsābhedena vyāptam, savyetara-
nayanadṛṣṭavad dṛṣṭam | avyāptitastu yadi pratyakṣāntaramapi viparītapratibhāsaṃ syāt, vastu
ca dvirūpaṃ bhavet | tacca dvayamapi nāstīti vyāptireva | āśrayabhedabhāvini ca jñāne
pakṣīkṛte tadviruddhaḥ pratibhāsabhedaḥ siddhaḥ | tato yatrārthakriyābhedādisaciva: pratibhāsa-
bhedastatra vastubhedaḥ ghaṭapaṭavat | taṃ punaḥ sahāyaṃ vihāya pravṛtto niyamenaika viṣayatāṃ
pariharatītyeko'tra bhrānta eva pratibhāsaḥ śaṅkha pītapratibhāsavat |
tatrāpi śaṅkha eva viṣaya iti cet ? śuklatāmaspṛśantī buddhiḥ śaṅkhaviṣayeti
suvyāhṛtam | śaṅkhamātraṃ pratyetīti cet –na, tataḥ parasya śaṅkhamātrasyāsphuraṇāt | pṛṣṭha-
bhāvini vikalpe sphuratīti cet ? astu, na tu nirvikalpa: pītapratibhāsaḥ śaṅkhaviṣaya
iti siddham | evaṃ dūrataḥ śikhariṇi piṇḍākārapratipattirapi na pippalādibhedāvasāya-

na bhinno'thaṃ ityekasyāpite bhrāntibhāve yadi na pratyakṣapratibhāso bhrāntaḥ, tadānya-

gocaratvāsamarthanāt | parokṣatāśrayastu kāraṇabheda indriyagocaragrahaṇaviraheṇaiva kṛtārthaḥ |
nanu vastuviṣayatve pratyayābhedaprasaṅgaḥ tvayaivokta iti tatparihāreṇaiva vastuviṣayatvaṃ
siddham, na cānyad vastvastīti tadviṣayatvaṃ ceti cet — naivaṃ, yataḥ pratibhāsa [12a ] -
vejātyasyātadviṣayatvena vyāptisādhanādasau prasaṅgo'smadīyaḥ | asmākamapi vyāpti-
vighaṭanāyaiva prayatna eṣaḥ | kāraṇavaijātyakṛte pratibhāsavejātye saṃbhavini kuto vā
tadviṣayatvena vyāptiriti ? etadapi kadā yujyate ? tadviṣayatvamātreṇa vā kāraṇa-
bhedo vyāpta: śakyo darśayitum | tattāvannāsti, kāraṇabhedasya vastuno'pratītyaiva
caritārthatvāt | atha na gavo [? satyo] dbhāvanametat kāraṇabhedādapi saṃbhāvyate prati-

cet ? aho niruḍhatā mahatī | ātyantikakāraṇavejātyasya hi phalametat | ekaviṣaya-

tvāderullekhaḥ | ātyantike tu sarvasādhāraṇasya dharmasyeti na tāvataivātadviṣayatvam |
asti cāvāstavadharmasya mādhuryasyānuvṛttirgāndhāre'pi |
anyādṛśaṃ tanmādhuryamiti cet ? vikalpanyastasyāpyagnitvamanyadeva | na caikarūpe
apyullikhyamāne'vāntaradharmapratibhāsayoreka viṣayatvam śuktirajatavat | na hi śukti- -
pratibhāso rajataviṣayo rajatapratibhāso vā śuktiviṣaya: sādhāraṇadhavalatollekhe'pi |
tasmād yathā'gnivikalpe vastusphuraṇe'pyavāntaradharmasya gardabhatvasyāsphuraṇāt na gardabha
viṣayatā, tathāvāntarasyāgnitvasya sphuraṇe'pi svalakṣaṇākārasya pratiniyatasyāsphuraṇāt
nānyadravyasphuraṇamiti nyāyaḥ, svalakṣaṇasyevāgnidravyatvāt | tataḥ kāraṇabhedo jñāna-
pratibhāsasya bhedako'stu | vastuviṣayatvaṃ tu na dvayorapi pratibhāsayoriti sthitametat |
tasmānna svalakṣaṇaṃ viṣayaḥ śabdāderiti siddham |

apohaprakaraṇam
kiṃ ca evaṃ vidhiniṣedhayorapo[hatvādu ] ccāraṇameva na syāt | tau hi dharmiṇo
vā syātām, dharmāṇāṃ vā yathā vṛkṣo'sti nāsti vā, vṛkṣo nīlo na vā nīla iti |
tatra prathamaḥ pakṣastāvannāsti | bhāvābhāvaniyato hi vṛkṣo vṛkṣaśabdena codita iti bhāva-
niyamapakṣe'stīti vyartham, nāstītyasamartham, virodhāt | abhāvanirūpaṇe tu viparyayaḥ |
asti ca vṛkṣapadaśrutī vidhiniṣedhāpekṣeti, bhāvābhāvasādhāraṇo'yaṃ vṛkṣapadād vṛkṣa -
pratibhāso na bāhyo vṛkṣa iti nyāyaḥ |
yattu nyāyadarśane tātparyaṭīkākāreṇa jātimadvayaktivācyatāṃ svavācaiva prastutya
anantarameva na ca śabdārthasya jāterbhāvābhāvasādhāraṇyaṃ nopapadyate, sā hi svarūpato
nityāpi deśakālaviprakīrṇānekavyaktayāśrayatayā bhāvābhāvasādhāraṇī bhavantyasti-
nāstisaṃbandhayogyā | vartamānavyaktisaṃbandhitā hi jāterastitā | atītānāgatasaṃba-
ndhitā ca nāstiteti | sandigdhavyatirekitvāt [12b] anaikāntikaṃ bhāvābhāva-
sādhāraṇyamanyathāsiddhaṃ veti' vilapitam tāvatā tāvanna prakṛtakṣatiḥ | jātau bharaṃ
nyasyatā svalakṣaṇāvācyatvasya svayaṃ svīkārāt |
api ca jātirapyastyādipadaprayogāt prāgabhidhīyamānā śabdena vartamānavyakti-
saṃbaddhā vā abhiveyā, atītānāgatavyaktisaṃbaddhā vāṃ, ubhayasaṃbaddhā vā, asaṃbaddhā veti
pakṣāḥ | na caikatrāpi trāṇaṃ prācīnacodyacaturaḥ kṣamate | prathame pakṣe hi bhāvaniyamaḥ
dvitīye tvabhāvaniyamaḥ | tṛtīye'pi yadi sadasadvyaktiyogādasyāḥ sattvāsattvavyava-
hāramanorathaḥ, tathā yairyairāśrayairvartamānavyaktiyogo'syā vyavahriyate, yairyairvātītā-
nāgatavyaktiyogaḥ, tānāśrayāṃstathaiva pratipādayet śabdaḥ | na hyanyathobhayavyaktisaṃbaddhā
pratipāditā bhavati | tathā ca sati sa evāstyādipadāprayogaprasaṅgaḥ ||
athaivaṃ matiḥ yat tadubhayavyaktisaṃbandhirūpaṃ tadasyā: śabdena coditameva, na tu
tatsaṃbandhinīnāmubhayīnāṃ vyaktīnāṃ pratītiḥ | na hyekasaṃbandhipratītiḥ saṃbandhyantarapratīti-
mavaśyamanvākarṣati putrādipratītivaditi cet ? evaṃ sati saṃbandhināmapratītau na saṃbandha -
sthāpi pratītiḥ | yataḥ,
dviṣṭhasaṃbandhasaṃvittirnaikarūpapravedanāt |
dvayasvarūpa grahaṇe sati saṃbandhavedanam ||
1. tula0 tā0 ṭī0 pṛ: 684 tathā ratna0 niba0 pṛ: 56, paṃ 11 - 16
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
tato yathā tattvataḥ kasyacit putro'pi pitṛsaṃbandhānavadhāraṇe puruṣamātrarūpaḥ pratīto
ghaṭavat svatantraḥ, tathā sāmānya saṅghātamapi vastu svatantraṃ pratīyamānaṃ na sāmānyarūpatayā
pratītaṃ bhavatīti caturthapakṣapratikṣepaḥ | tadāpi saṃbandhināmanākṣepādastyādipadāprayogaḥ
siddhaḥ, svatantre hi tasminniścīyamāne tasyaiva bhāvābhāvābhyāmastyādiprayogeṇa bhāvyam,
nānyasya | saṃbandhāvadhāraṇe'pi hi naikasaṃbandhino bhāvābhāvābhyāmitarasyāstyādipada-
prayogaḥ | na hi caitrasya bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ tatputratvenāvadhārito'pi maitro'sti nāsti
veti saṃbandhamarhati, kiṃ punaḥ saṃbandhāboghi sāmānyam ? anyādṛśastatra saṃbandha iti
cet ? kīdṛśo'pi vā bhavatu, pratītimanārūḍhaḥ punarasatkalpa eveti nānyadoyabhāvā-
bhāvābhyāmayaḥśalākākalpasya pratītasyāstyādipadaprayogo yogamanveti, atiprasaṅgāt |
svarūpaṃ cāsya sadāvasthāyi pratipāditamityastipada vaiyarthya, nāstipadavirodhaśca tadavastha: |
tasmānnānyathāsiddhaṃ bhāvābhāvasādhāraṇya maikāntikaṃ ca bāhyaviṣayatvasādhane
vikalpapratibhāsasya | niyamavatī hi viṣayavyavasthā nimittavattathā vyāptā' |
na ca viṣayasadasattāprasādhanādanyat nimittamupapadyate, atiprasaṅgāt | tatastadabhāve
vyāpakābhāvādabhavantī viṣayavattā sadasattvaprasādhana eva niyamyamānā tena vyāpteti
tadvirodhini kathamavatiṣṭhet ? yajjñānaṃ yatra bhāvābhāvasādhāraṇapratibhāsaṃ, na tena tasya
viṣayavattvam, [13a] yathā gojñānasyāśvena | bāhye ca bhāvābhāvasādhāraṇapratibhāsaṃ
vṛkṣavikalpajñānamiti vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhiḥ | tadviṣayatvavyāpakasya bhāvābhāvaprasādhanasya
hi viruddhaṃ tadaprasādhanarūpaṃ sādhāraṇyam | evaṃ jātimadvayaktivacane'pi doṣa eva |
vyakteścet pratītisiddhiḥ, jātiradhikā pratīyatāṃ mā vā, na tu taddoṣānmukti: |
yaccoktaṃ kaumārilaiḥ, sabhāgatvādeva vastuno na sādhāraṇyadoṣaḥ, vṛkṣatvaṃ hyanirdhārita
bhāvābhāvaṃ śabdādavagamyate, tayoranyatareṇa śabdāntarāvagatena saṃbadhyata iti | tatrāpi
vṛkṣatvamiti yadi jātivivakṣitā, tadā taddaṣaṇenaiva nirvṛtiḥ | athāparāmṛṣṭabhedābhedameva
vṛkṣatvam tadā tadavaśyambhāve'bhāve vā niyataṃ, śabdena ca tathaiva khyāpitamiti
kimastyādipadenādyāpi ?
syādetat | tanniyatatve'pi vṛkṣatvāṅga eva śabdena codito na sattvāsattvāṅga
iti cet ? tayoraṃśayostarhi bheda: kālpanikastāttviko vā ? kālpanikatve iyaṃ

vasīyate'satyabhyāsa iti viśeṣaṇamapekṣyam |
nanu pratyakṣe'pi na gṛhītakṣaṇasyāvasāya:, kiṃ tu santateḥ, na cāsyāḥ pratibhāsa
iti kenāsyāpi saviṣayatvaṃ, kṣaṇe santato cobhayābhāvāt | anumāne tu parīkṣaiva
vartate |
na cānyat pramāṇamasti, yasyobhayasaṃbhavena viṣayaḥ kaścidityasaṃbhavametat |
tadekaikena vidheyatve sthitaviṣayaka sthitira khilasya bāhyasyāntarasya vā vācyatvamiti |
atrocyate | tattvavyavasthāmāha ubhayasaṃbhavenaiva viṣayatvaṃ, kevalaṃ sāṃvyava-
hārikāpekṣayā saṃvṛterevādhara saṃvṛttimapekṣya tattvamiti vyavahriyate, kṣaṇabhedāvatāre saṃvyava
hāravilopāt vyāvahārikaṃ prati pratikṣaṇakṣīṇatāyā abhāvāt tattvataḥ pratyakṣeṇobhaya-
saṃbhavābhāvaḥ, iti na doṣaḥ | atha pṛthagjanasya dṛśyavikalpyayorapyabhedagraho niyata
evetyavasito vahniḥ pratibhāsita eveti cet – na, pratibhāsāntarasmaraṇena tatpratibhāsa-
bhramabhraṃśasya kṛtatvāt | yathā ca vikalpapratibhāsādanya eva vastupratibhāso darśayitum
adhyakṣa śakyaḥ, tathā nādhyakṣa pratibhāsādanyo'stīti tatraiva vastupratibhāsaviśrāmāt
tadvijātīyasya vastupratibhāsatāvyudāsaḥ śreyān | tasmād yuktamuktam,
sthāpyo vācyastattvatto naiva kaścit |
iti | [20b] athavā vastvantarāvācyatve'pi tatrāpohastadviśeṣaṇatvena gamya iti
apohasya vācyatā svīkṛtaiva | tathāpi kathaṃ sarvadharmāna bhilapyatvamityāha,
vācyastattvato naiva kaścidartha iti |
ayamabhiprāyaḥ | paryudāsapakṣe tāvad vasturūpavat tasyāpyadhyavasāyamātrakṛtaṃ vācya-
tvam, na pratibhāsādadhyakṣavat | prasajyapakṣe punaranyanivṛttimātrasyānyadāpi na viśeṣaḥ,
tathāpyasau nārtha iti noktadoṣaḥ | yada vā yaḥ śāstre, tasmāt siddhametat sarvaśabdā-
vivekaviṣayā vikalpāścetyupasaṃhāra: tasyārthaniṣṭhāmupasaṃhāreṇeva darśayati, -
vācyastattvatto naiva kaścidarthaṃ iti |
saṃvṛtau pratibhāsādhyavasāyamātreṇa vācyatāyā darśitatvāt,
tattvata ityāha |

na bhavedaghaṭajātīyatvāt | [22b] atha yajjātīyaṃ buddhimadanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi

jāyeta, hanta na tarhi sakṛdapi buddhimataḥ kumbhakārāderutpadyeta | bhavati ca tatastajjanyam
ityekaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
yathā vā saugatānāmapi na dhūmo'nyasmād bhavatīti śaṅkanīyam, aniyatahetukatvena
nirhetukatvaprasaṅgāt | nirhetukasya ca,
nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vā'hetoranyānapekṣaṇāt |
apekṣāto hi bhāvānāṃ kādācitkatvasambhavaḥ ||
[pra. vā. 3. 34]
tathāsmākamapīti dvitīyaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
evaṃ ca sati yathā bhavatāmayaṃ niyamaḥ sidhyati sa dhūmo'gnyanvayavyatirekānu-
vidhāyī padārthaviśeṣaḥ, sa cāgniryastasya janakaḥ | tad yadyasau śamayamāno dhūmastadāgni-
kārya eveti, tathāsmākamapi tatkāryaṃ yad buddhimatpūrvakam | sa puruṣo yastatkāroti |
tathā yadi cetanāvantamadhiṣṭhātāramantareṇa [23a] kacidapi kārye niścetanānāṃ pravṛtti -
nivṛttī syātāṃ tadānīṃ kāryakriyāyā avirāmaprasaṅgaḥ | tathā hi yadyacetanānāṃ svarasataḥ
pravṛttistadā nirabhiprāyavyāpāratayā sarvadā pravṛttiḥ syāt | na hyakasmāt pravṛttināśo
yuktaḥ | tataśca kāryasyāvirāmaḥ | athaudāsīnyam, tadā kadācidapi pravṛttinaṃ sthāt,
viśeṣābhāvāt| adhiṣṭhāyakena tu prayatnavatā kadācita pravartyanta iti yuktaṃ paśyāmaḥ,
nācetanena | tasyecchāyattapravṛttinivṛtyorayogāditi tṛtīya bādhaka pramāṇam |
iha khalu kāryatvaṃ kādācitkakāraṇasannidhimattayā vyāptam, kādācitkakāraṇa-
sannidhiścānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ kartṛvyāpārādhīnaḥ yathā turovemādīnāṃ sannidhiḥ |
vipakṣe ca kādācitkakāraṇasannidhisattā nāsti | na hyacetanaḥ kāraṇāni sannidhāpayituṃ
śaknoti, śaktau trā ghaṭādāvapi kartṛvyāpāranivṛttiprasaṅgāt | tataśca vyāpakānupalabdhyā
vipakṣānnivartamānaṃ kāryatvaṃ buddhimatpūrvakatvena vyāpyata iti pratibandhasiddhiriti caturthaṃ
bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
tathā deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgo bādhakaḥ | tathā hi kāryatvaṃ deśakālaprakṛtiniyamena
vyāptaṃ yadi prayatnavantamantareṇa bhavet, na deśādiniyamena bhavet | karturicchayā hi
kvacid deśādāvanyadeśādivyavacchedena jāyeta | tadabhāve sarvatra deśādau bhavediti
īśvaravāde pūrvaṃpakṣasaṃkṣepaḥ
vipakṣād vyāpakānupalabdhyā nivartamānaṃ kāryatvaṃ prayatnavannāntarīyakatvena vyāpyata iti
pratibandhasiddhiḥ pañcamaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇamiti ||
yat śaṅkaraḥ, nirabhiprāyavyāpārebhyaḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ deśādiniyamo na syāditi |
tathā nāpi kaścid viśeṣa: kṣityādihetūnāṃ prāsādādihetubhyo yenāmī nirabhiprāya-
vyāpārāḥ santaḥ prayatnavanirapekṣā : pratiniyamavatā ca vyāpāreṇa tadvantaḥ syuriti ||
' vācaspatistu kaṇikāyāmīśvaravādamutthāpayannāha, yadi punaracetanāni cetanāna-
dhiṣṭhitāni kāryaṃ kuryuḥ, tato yatra kacanāvasthitāni janayeyuriti na deśakālapratiniyata-
prasavaṃ kāryamupalabhyeta | hetusamavadhānādhīnajanmatayā kāryaṃ na pratyekaṃ kāraṇairjanyata
iti cet ? [ satyam, ] samavadhānameva tu ' kāraṇānāṃ kutaḥ ? kādācitkaparipākād
adṛṣṭaviśeṣāditi cet ? nanvayamapyacetanaḥ kathaṃ yathāvatkāraṇāni sannidhāpayet ?
no khalu yatra kacanāvasthitāni daṇḍādīni vinā kumbhakāraprayatnamadṛṣṭaviśeṣavaśādeva
parasparaṃ sannidhīyante, sannihitāni vā kāryasyeśate | tasmāt kāraṇasamavadhānavyāpta-
tvāt kāryotpādasya tasya copalabdhimatpūrvakatvābhāve'nupapattervyāpakanivṛttyā vipakṣāt
kāryotpādo nivartamāna upalabdhimatpūrvakatvena vyāpyata iti pratibandhasiddhiriti ||
evaṃ [ 23b] sati bhavatu kartṛmātra siddhiḥ, sarvajñatā tu kaṃthamasya, dṛṣṭānte tadanvaya-
sthābhāvāditi cet ?
na
atra trilocanaḥ, naitadasti | yato nāsmābhirupāttabheda: kartā sādhayitumiṣṭaḥ,
ki tarhi ? sādhyasāmānyam | tasya ca yena viśeṣeṇa saha vāstavaḥ pratibandho'sti
so'pyupādānādisākṣātkāraṇalakṣaṇo viśeṣa: sādhyasāmānye niścetavye'vaśyaniścetavyaḥ,
tatyāge sādhyasāmānyatyāgaprasaṅgāt | ca śakyaṃ tyaktum sādhyasāmānyasya
kṣityādidharmavyāpakatvāt | tatpunaḥ kṣityādyapādānaṃ paramāṇucatuṣṭayam sarvakṣetrajña-
samavetasiddhirūpāṇi karmāṇi | dikkālau copakaraṇam | sarvakṣetrajñalakṣaṇaṃ ca sampradānam |
kṣetrajñopabhogalakṣaṇaṃ ca prayojanam | etat sarvaṃ pratyakṣataḥ pratipadyamānaḥ kartā pratyakṣī-
kṛtasakalaviśvavibhāgaḥ sarvajñaḥ | na cāsyopanyāsapūrvako'nvayo dṛṣṭānte pradaśyate,
yenānanvayādidoṣagaṇasyāpatti: syāt ||
