jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalī
syādetat | mahābhūtotpattedvaryaṇukādikramasya ghaṭaniṣpatterapi dvayaṇukādikrama-
viśeṣānupalabdherayaṃ ghaṭaṃ kurvan kumbhakāro dvayaṇukamapi karoti | na ca tasyopādānam
upakaraṇaṃ vā kulālaḥ pratyakṣataḥ pratipadyate | tasmādayamanekāntaḥ, yo yasya kartā sa
tasyopādānādi jānātīti ||
atrocyate | bhavedanekānto yadi kulālo dvayaṇukasya kartā bhavet | na hi
yāvadantyāvayaviniṣpatteraṅgaṃ tat sarva kulālaḥ karoti, dṛṣṭasāmarthyakāraṇaprayokkulakṣaṇa-
tvāt kartṛkatvasya | tasmād dvayaṇukamapi mahābhūtavat sandigdhakartṛkatvāt sādhyameva |
tadevaṃ yat sādhyavādinā sādhayitumiṣṭamanumeyasāmānyaṃ tad dūṣaṇavādinā pratibandhuṃ
na śakyate | yastu dūṣaṇavādinā pratibandhumiṣṭo viśeṣa:, nāsī sādhyasāmānyavādinā
sādhayitumiṣṭa: | kiṃ tarhi ? sādhyasāmānye niścetavye tena vāstavapratibandhasya viśeṣasya
siddhirbalād bhavantī nopekṣyate | evaṃ sādhanāyattāṃ viśeṣasiddhimācāryo manyamāno
yad dūṣaṇamavādīt, – yāvatīmarthagata sādhanaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatīṃ dūṣaṇamapi | yadyasau
viśeṣo na sādhanena viṣayīkṛtaḥ kathamatastatsiddhiḥ ? sidhyan vā kathamaviṣayaḥ ?
viṣayaścet, kathaṃ svāśrayāṃ doṣagati na spṛśediti, tannirastam | yataḥ sādhanavādī
sādhanādhīnāṃ yadi viśeṣa siddhimabhyupagacchet tadaitat syāt | na ca naiyāyika : sādhanā-
yattāṃ viśeṣasiddhimupajīvati | kiṃ tarhi ? sādhyasāmānyapratibandhākṛṣṭasya viśeṣasya
siddhim, yathā bauddha: kṣaṇikatva siddhī tena vāstavapratibandhānnairātmyasiddhimupajīvati |
na hyātmani nitye vibhau ca sati sarvavastuviṣayaṃ kṣaṇikatvamanumātumīśaḥ ||
mīmāṃsako'pi darśanasparśanābhyāmekamavayavinaṃ niścinvan niścetavyānuṣaṅgiṇa
indriyasya nānātvaṃ niyataviṣayatvamindriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayagrahaṇaliṅgatvaṃ jñāturjñānasādha
natvaṃ gandhādiguṇavyatiriktaṃ [24a ] ca guṇādhikaraṇamaniyata viṣayaścetana ityetā-
vato'rthānupajīvati | tathā sādhyaviśeṣo'pi naiyāyikairupajīvyata iti sarva samānam
anyatrābhiniveśāt | tasmāt siddhaṃ sarvajñatvamiti ||
vācaspatistu', syādetat | utpattimattvamupādānādyabhijñakartṛmātra vyāptaṃ ghaṭādiṣu
duṣṭaṃ tanmātrameva pṛthivyādīnāṃ gamayet | nityasarva viṣayajñānavatkartṛpūrvakatvaṃ tu kuta-
styam ? na caitad ghaṭādau dṛṣṭāntadharmaṇi dṛṣṭam ||

kriyātvaṃ tadeva karaṇaṃ gamayet yat tadupalabdhinirvartanasamartham, na ca kuṭhārādayaḥ
samarthā iti pakṣadharmatābalāt kuṭhārādivilakṣaṇamadṛṣṭacaramapi cakṣurādi upasthāpayatīti |
tadatrāpi samānam | na hyaparimeyāniyatadigdeśaindriyakātīndriyakatrasasthāvarādilakṣaṇa-
kāryotpādayogapadyamasati sarvaviṣaye jñāne nitye vā seddhumarhati | no khalvīdṛśaṃ

vipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva |
prayogaḥ, yo yaḥ pratyakṣakṛtaḥ [25b] kāraṇatvaniścayaḥ, nāsau dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyava
sāyī, yathāgnau jaṭharajātajātavedaḥsādhāraṇarūpaṃ pariharan | pratyakṣakṛtaścāsau buddhimatīti
vyāpakaviruddhavyāptopalabdhiḥ | pratyakṣakṛtatvaṃ hi dṛśya viṣayatvena vyāptamadṛśye tasyā-
pravṛtteḥ, taduviruddhaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviṣayatvam tadvyāptaṃ dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyitvam |
ki ca yadi dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇamavadhūya dhīmanmātreṇa vyāpti vivakṣitā evaṃ sati yadā
buddhimadabhāve kumbhakāryasyābhāvamupadarśayed vyatirekapratipādanāya tadā dṛśyādṛśya-
viśeṣaṇarahitacetanamātrasyābhāva: kena pramāṇena siddhaḥ dṛśyānupalabdheśyasyaiva
pratiṣedhe'dhikārāt ? anyathā tṛṇādinā vyabhicārasyāśakyaparihāratvācca ?
na
ca dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhirbuddhimanmātrasya vyatirekabodhasādhanībhavitum
arhati, ātyantikaviṣayabhedasya vyaktatvāt | anyathā tṛṇādijanmanyapi dṛśyapuruṣa-
viṣayaivānupalabdhistadvayabhicāra sthirīkaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt | na hi lābhe praveśaśchede
niḥsaraṇamiti nyāyyam | tasmād dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpoḍhapakṣe vyāptigrahaṇakāle vyatireka-
grahaṇopāyābhāvād avyāpteḥ punarapi vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ | na ca nabhasyubhayābhāva-
vibhāvanamupāyo vyatirekagrahaṇasya, kāryābhāvasya buddhimadvayāpārābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayā
nupapatteḥ | tadaparakāraṇasākalye hi tanmātrābhāve'bhāvaḥ kāryasya tadabhāvaprayuktaḥ
pratyetuṃ śakyaḥ | yathā trikapañcaka cintāyāṃ cintitam | dvayostu kacinnivṛttimātram
akāryakāraṇabhūtayorapi sulabham |
kiṃ ca buddhimatkāraṇavyāpāravirahāt vihāyasi kāryatvābhāva uta kāraṇamātra-
viprayogāditi ko niṣṭaṅkaḥ ? tathā ca sati viphala : sakalo yatnaḥ | anvayo'pi hi
kāraṇamātreṇa kāryamātrasya gṛhyatāmutasvit puruṣaviśeṣaṇena kāraṇeneti sandeha eva |
atha dṛṣṭa evāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ, dhūme dahanātmavatu | yadyevaṃ dṛśyaśarīra-246
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
rūpo'pi viśeṣaḥ pratīta eva, kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ, citrabhānorbhāsurākāravat ? sa tarhi
viśeṣaḥ kāryeṇa vyabhicaryaṃta iti cet ? vyabhicayaṃtām | kārye'pi kāraṇavad yathā
paridṛṣṭaviśeṣaniṣṭha evānvayo bhavatu ghaṭavat saudhādāvapi dṛṣṭatvāditi kiṃ naśchinnam ?
etaccānvayamātraṃ gajanimolitena dūṣaṇamavadhīryābhidhoyate | vastutastu pratyakṣānupa-
lambhayorekasyāpi vyāpārāyogānnānvayo na vyatirekaḥ | asti ca kāryatva murvīdharādau,
na ca darśanātikrānte kartaryanvayavyatireko spṛśati | tādṛkcetanakṛtetaratvābhyāṃ ca
rāśyantarābhāvād gandhādivadasādhāraṇānekānta eva | tasmānna pratyakṣeṇa kāryamātrasya
vyāptigrahaṇamiti siddham |
[26a] yātāścaivaṃ yadamī pratyakṣānupalambhāviśiṣṭakāryaṃ jātyullekhenaiva kārya-
kāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravṛttayo na kāryamātrollekhena | tathā hi pratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttisama-
nantaramīdṛśāt jvaladbhāsurasvarūpavastuviśeṣādīdṛśaṃ dhavalimaliptakaṇṭhāmbakavikārakāri
vastu jāyata ityanenākāreṇa hetuphalabhāvavyavahāraḥ sarvāpara
kāryakāraṇajātivyudāsena
viśiṣṭameva jātiyugmamullikhan pravartate | iyameva gatiḥ sarvatra hetuphalabhāvavyavahṛtau,
īśvarānurodhāt tu prasiddhanyāyolla[ṅghanametat ] iti paśyāmaḥ ||
kaḥ punaratrāparādho yadi tārṇādibhedamudasya vahninā dhūmamātrasyeva bhūdharādi-
bhedamapyudasya kāryamātrasya buddhimatā vyāpti pratīyāt pratyakṣam ? yathaiva tarhi varhiṣā
kāryajātiviśeṣasya dhūmasyāvāntarasūkṣmajātimātramantarbhāvya vyāptigraho na tu tadvi-
jātīyasparśa:, tathā buddhimatāpyastu vastrādeḥ | yathā vātyantavisadṛśorapi kāryajātī:
antarbhāvya bhūtimanmātrasya cetanena vyāpti jighṛkṣasi tathā vahnināpi gṛhṇīyāḥ |
indriyapratyakṣasyaiva hi vyāpāra ubhayatra kathaṃ bhinnāṃ vṛttimāśrayeta ? vyabhicāradarśanā-
darśanakṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet ? tatrttārha darśanādarśanaṃ saṅkalpamanārūḍhaṃ gacchattṛṇa-
sparśavadakiñcitkaramiti tadanurūpavimarśenāvaśyabhāvyam | na cāsti |
na hi kaścidagnidhūmādiṣvanvayavyatirekagrāhipratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttau kāryajātiḥ
akhilānalādutpadyata iti saṅkalpamanubhūya bhūyo vyabhicāradarśanāt yato vā kāryāntarāṇi
vahnimantareṇāpyupalabdhānyupalabhyante vā tato dhūma evānena janyata iti niścayaṃ pari-
cinoti, kiṃtu jhagityeva pratyakṣānupalambhāntaramasmādagnyāderidaṃ dhūmādīti jāti-
viśeṣadvayaṃ hetuphalabhāvavyavahārabhājanī kurvannanubhūyate'nusandhānapratyayaḥ | pratyakṣagocare
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
[anvayavyatirekayo]rna kaścid viśeṣaḥ | yadā ca vikalpāntarasthitasya jhagiti kaṇṭakād
vyathetyanupalambhapūrvikādhyakṣa vihitā hetuphalabhāvagrāhiṇī matiḥ, tadābhivyakto vyabhi-
cāradarśana vimarśavirahaḥ, samasamayāsambhavād vikalpānām | tadihāpyasmāt śilpina
idaṃ pṛthubudhnodarādyākā kāryamityavāntarasūkṣmabhedamudasya vyavahāraḥ | yadā tu paṭa-
śakaṭādikamapi puruṣādutpadyamānaṃ paśyati tadedamapīdamapi puruṣeṇa janyata iti
matiravisaṃvādinī samudeti ||
kiṃ ca vyabhicāro nāma ki siddhāyāmeva vyāptāvanumānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati ?
atha vyāptireva mithyeti vyavasthāpayati ? atrāpi pakṣe svasāmarthyena sphuratyeva vyāpti-
grāhiṇa pramāṇe | yad vā tasyaiva prāmāṇyakṣayamādadhānaḥ, adyāpi sarvatra viṣaye niyate vā ?
niyate'pi kimiṣṭivaśāt, atha pratyakṣasya tatraiva pravṛtteḥ ? prathamaḥ pakṣastāvanna yukto
virodhāt | na hi [26b] sādhyāvinābhāvalakṣaṇā ca vyāptirhetoḥ sādhyābhāva saṃbhavakṛta-
śvānumānābhāvaḥ saṅgacchate, anyatrāpi vyāptāvanāśvāsācca |
evaṃ vyāptigrāhiṇi pramāṇe prāmāṇyādapracyutibhṛti vyāptimṛṣātvabodhanamapya-
sambaddhaṃ boddhavyam | sarvatra ca vyāptigrāhiṇa: prāmāṇyakṣaye dhūmādagnirapi nānumātavyaḥ,
anyasya vyāptigrāhiṇo'bhāvāt | kimidānīṃ śaraṇamīśvarānumānasya bhaviṣyati ?
svecchayā ca niyate viṣaye vyāptivihitau pramāṇaṃ varākamudāsīna miti na kaścit
heturaheturvā tattvataḥ, dhūme'pi svecchayā vyāptikhaṇḍanaprasaṅgāt | niyata viṣayatvaṃ tu
vyabhicāragocarasyāpi pratyakṣasya katham, yāvatā yathā niyatajātipravṛttaṃ vyāptigrāhi
sarvaviṣayamiṣṭam tathā vyabhicāragocaramapi sarvaviṣayamevānyūnānatiriktaśaktitvād
ubhayo: ? tadekaviṣaya eva vyāptigraho vyabhicāravedanaṃ ceti kimadhunā sādhanamasādhanaṃ
vā syāt ? bhavatu vā bhavaduparodhād bādhabodhina: pramāṇasya niyataviṣayatvam |
tathāpi na khalu sakṛdeva vyabhicāravatāṃ bādhabodhaḥ, kiṃ tu krameṇa | tadā ca vyabhicāriṇā-
mapi vyabhicāradarśanamāhatya nāstīti dhūmasya tato viśeṣābhāvāt punarahetutvam, hetutvaṃ
vānyasyāpi |
na ca sarvasyānyasya vyabhicāradarśanairdhūme vyāptiviśvāsa iti vācyam | evaṃ hi
purastāda dhūme vyāptigrahaṇānantarameva parvatanitambe dhūmād dahanānumānaṃ na śārdūlāditi
na syāt, vyabhicāradarśana vilambāpekṣaṇāt | aśakyaṃ caitadanyatra vyabhicāradarśanairabhi -248
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
mate vyāptiviśrāma iti | vyabhicāraviṣayāṇāmadhyanantatvād deśādiviprakarṣavatāṃ
gocarīkaraṇakālāpekṣayā puruṣāyuṣasya kanīyastvāt | tasmād vyabhicāradarśanavanniyata-
viṣaya eva vyāptigraho nirapavādaḥ, śuddhekādhyavasāyasya vibhāgena pravṛtteḥ | ataeva ca
svābhāvi kavikalpasyaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇe'dhikāro naupādhikasya |
asti hi śuddhaviṣayajanitālocanājñānamātrāpekṣo bālatiryaksādhāraṇo vikalpaḥ |
sa śuddhaḥ svābhāvika iti cocyate, yadvaśāt paśavo'pi kṣutpipāsāpraśamādisādhanāni tatraiva
samarthānyavadhārayantaḥ punastadanvitayā tathaiva tatastatra pravartante, nivartante vānanvitayā |
asti ca saṅketasmaraṇasacivālocanājñānajanito [vikalpa:], yathā dīpāt kajjalamā-
lokayato nīlamidaṃ rañjanādyapayogītyeva vikalpa: pūrvadṛṣṭārthakriyāsmaraṇasahāyānubhavabhā-
vitastādṛgaupādhika ucyate | na ca tadā nīlavikalpa ityeva pradīpādakhilaṃ nīlamutpadyata
iti prekṣaḥ kaścinniścinoti | kiṃ tu yadeva kajjalāvalokanamātrānurūpavikalpapuraskṛtaṃ
[ 27a] vastu kajjalaśabdasaka tayogya jātiyogāt svarūpaviśeṣād vā tadeva pradīpakāryaṃ
vyabhicārālambane coktam |
evaṃ dhūme'pi dhavalamidaṃ vastu varjāyata iti saṅketānusārī vikalpa aupādhika
evākṣipati kāryatvena tuhinādikam | śuddhe tu vikalpe dhūmajātireva parisphuratīti tata
eva tuhinādervyāptau nirāso na vyabhicārālambanaṃ sādhviti boddhavyam | tadvat kārya-
vikalpo'pi sarvatra aupādhika eva | apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi svotpattāvandhaḥ | kārya-
miti saṅketasmaraṇasahāyādindriyajñānādutpattiriti na hetuphalabhāvavyavahārasyāṅgam |
tato yadyapi puruṣāt ghaṭodayadarśane ghaṭo'yamasmāditi vikalpavat kāryamidamasmādityapi
sulabho vikalpaḥ, tathāpi svābhāvikatvābhāvānna tatpuraskṛtasvarūpasya tatkāryatvavyavasthā |
naisargika vikalpa viṣayīkṛtasya tu bhavatu |
nanu śuddhāvasāyagocare'pi vikalpaḥ saṅketasmṛtijanito dṛśyate'yaṃ ghaṭaḥ pauruṣeya
iti nāmollekhāt | tataḥ so'pyaupādhikaḥ prāptaḥ | na tanmātravikalpane smaraṇasya
aprayojakatvāt, vācakāṃśollekha eva tasya sāmarthyāt | yadyapi ca vācyavācakā-
kārotkalitākhaṇḍavikalpodaya: smaraṇasāhāyakena, tathāpyapodvāradvāreṇa tanmātre tad-
vyāpāra ucyate, mṛnmayatvamātre kulālasyeva | jātyantarasamavāyikāryatvadhavalatādi-
dharmakalpanaṃ tu saṅketasambandhagrahaṇādiprācīnavyāpārasmaraṇamantareṇa śuddhādhyavasāyasya
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
tanmātrajātyullekhenaiva kṛtārthatvād bālakādivat atastanmātraviṣayaiva pratyakṣakṛtā
vyāptirityanavadyam | tasmād vyāptigrahaḥ pratyakṣakṛto vyabhicārapratyayo vā bhinnaviṣaya
eveti siddham |
evaṃ tarhi vyabhicāradarśanena sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā duḥstheti cet ? eva-
metad yadi buddhipāṭavaniyamaḥ sarveṣām | mandabuddhistu sādṛśyādinā jātiviśeṣa-
pravṛtte'pi pratyakṣa jātyantareṇaikīkṛtya vyāptigrahābhimānādanumānamātiṣṭhamāna: paṭunā
pareṇa vyabhicāramādarśya vyāptidurgrahamāpādyate | ataḥ sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā |
yathā dhūme pravṛtte'pi pratyakṣe vyāptigrāhiṇyucchaladbahalarūpamanalavyāptimanusmaran māruto-
ddhṛtadhūlipaṭalādanalamanumāpayan vāṣpodayena prasiddhoṣabudhavedhuryeṇa vyabhicāramādayaṃ
vāryate, tato'pi kāraṇāt jātiviśeṣaviṣayaiva vyāptiḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti siddham |
yadi hi dhūmaikajātipratibaddha pratibandhabodhamadhyakṣam tadā sādṛśyāpekṣo'nyatra
tadrūpāropaḥ, sadṛśāntaravyabhicāreṇa ca vāraṇaṃ yuktam | yadā tu kāryajātau sarvatra
vyāptigrahaḥ, tadā kiṃ sādṛśyāpekṣayeti ? yadi tarhi jātiviśeṣapratibaddha evādhyakṣeṇa prati-
bandhabodhaḥ kathamatyantavijātīyo'pi [0tīyā api] ghaṭakuṭakuḍyādayaḥ sādhāraṇarāgayogino
[27b] haridrādidravyasaṃskāramanumāpayanti ? kathaṃ vā kuṭhārādi cchedakriyāyāṃ dṛṣṭa-
vyāpāra karaṇamatyanta vijātīyāpi buddhiḥ kriyātvenānumāpayati ?
evamatyantavijātīyā api kailāsakuliśādayaḥ sādhāraṇakāryatvādidharmaṃkāḥ
puruṣamanumāpayiṣyantīti cet ? naivam, vyāpyasya gamakatvāt tadapekṣayaiva sajātīya-
vijātīyatāyāścintyatvāt | vyāpyaṃ ca nirvartyavikāryakarmāpekṣayā dvividhaṃ dharmirūpaṃ
dharmarūpaṃ ca | tatra sarvathāpūrvotpattau dharmiṇo vyāptirucyate, dhūmādivat | tadā ca
dhūmāntarameva sajātīyam, vijātīyamanyad vastu | yadā tu pūrvaṃsthitasyaiva dharmāntaro-
tpattivyavasāya:, tadā dharmavyāptirucyate, payasi auṣṇyādivat, tadā ca auṣṇyāntara -
meva sajātīyo dharmaḥ, nādhunā dharmijāterapekṣā |
evaṃ rāgo'pi ghaṭakuṭādidravyavejātyamavamatya svayaṃ svajātīya kāryāpekṣayaiva
rāgadravyasaṃskārasya gamakaḥ | ataeva tadviśeṣe kacit kuṅkumasya samparka : kacit haridrā-
deranumīyate | na caivaṃ pūrvasthite bhūdharāmbhodharādau kāryatvādimātranirvartakaḥ puruṣa
iṣṭaḥ kiṃ tu kumbhādivadapūrvakotpādaka eva | tadā ca dhūme dhavalatādivat kāryatādayaḥ

santo'pi jātyantarasamavāyino dharmā vyāpterbahirbhāvādakiñcitkarā eva | tasmād
dharmivastuvyāptigraho na dharmamātra pratyāsattimanurudhyate | nāpi dharmavyāpterdharmiṇaḥ sa-
jātīyatām | śuddhekavimarśāpekṣayā ca sajātīyetaravyavasthānamuktam | nāto rāgavaddhami-
vaijātye'pi kāryatvādīnāṃ gamakatvam | anyathā pāṇḍudravyādapi havyāśanānumāna -
prasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ, vyabhicārottarasya dūṣitatvāt |
indriye tvevamanumānam | yadanthakāraṇasannidhau kādācitkam, tat kāraṇāntarā-
pekṣam yathā pāthaḥ pṛthvīsannidhāvaṅkaraḥ, viṣayamanaskārālokasannidhau ca kādācitkī
buddhiriti svabhāvahetuḥ | anapekṣatve vipakṣe kādācitkaṃ virodhādanavasthāyīti
bādhakāt vyāptisiddhiḥ | yat tadanyadapekṣyaṃ tadindriyamiti vyavasthā, tato na kriyā-
tvena kāraṇānumānaṃ, nāpi pratyakṣaṃ vyāptigrāhi | avaśyaṃ ca svābhāvika vikalpāmukhī -
kṛtajātibhedapuraskāreṇaiva sāmānyagrahaṇameṣitavyamadhyakṣasya, anyathā yadā pratyakṣeṇa
vyāptimekāmupadarthyāyaṃ ghaṭa iti saṅketaḥ kriyate, tadā kimasau kāryatvādidharmayogi
viśvamāviśati ? vyabhicāradarśanena ca niyataviṣayatāmupanīyate ? upadeṣṭhaiva vā sarvānya-
jātiṣu niṣedhan viṣayaniyame niṣṭhāpayati ? atha sāmānyaviṣaya eva nāsau samaya: ?
evaṃ vācakajātibhede'pi draṣṭavyam | kāryaśabdastu pratyakṣamanapekṣya vikalpamātra-
gocarite parāpekṣodayamātre niveśita iti na viśeṣavṛttiḥ | yadi tu so'pi pratyakṣa-
vartinyayaṃ kāryaṃ [28a] iti niveśyeta, so'pi tatparyāyāntaravānniyatavṛttireva syāt |
tasmāt kāyajātiviśeṣaviṣayīkaraṇameva nisarga: pratyakṣasya | yadi ca kāryajātibhede
pravṛttamapi pratyakṣaṃ kāryamātramadhiṣṭhānīkaroti, kāraṇe tarhi pravartamānaṃ kāraṇamātrameva
vyāpakamavadhārayatu, kasmādupādānādivedana viśiṣṭamavalambate ? tato yadi na bhavadabhi -
prāyānurodho'dhyakṣasyobhayatra sāmānyāvalambinā viśeṣāvalambinā vā bhavitavyamanena,
sāmānyālambane kāryāt kāraṇānumānamiti kā vārteśvarasiddheḥ ? viśeṣāvalambane ca
kāryamātravyāpterasiddheriti | tasmādanubhavād yuktambha viśiṣṭāmeva kāya~jāti hetuviśeṣa-
vyāptāmupadarśayati pratyakṣamiti |
prayogaḥ | yad yat kāryakāraṇabhāvagrāhi pratyakṣam, tad viśiṣṭajātiprati
niyatavyāpāram, yathāgnidhūmayoḥ | tathā cedaṃ buddhimatā kāryasya vyāptisādhanamiti sva-
bhāvahetuḥ | nāsyānyathāvyāpārāśaṅkayānekāntaḥ, kāraṇānupalabdhibādhitatvāt | kāraṇa-
bhedo hi kāryabhedasya kāraṇam, anyathā sarvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt | na cāsya kāraṇa-
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
bhedo'sti viṣayendriyālokādilakṣaṇasamānasāmagrī prabhavatvāditi | dṛṣṭānte sādhya -
śūnyatāśaṅkāyāṃ ca yad yat pratyakṣam, tat tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva sāmānyāvalambanam,
yathā vyabhicāragrāhi pratyakṣam, pratyakṣaṃ ca vyāptigrāhīti svabhāva eva | sa evānekānta-
parihāraḥ | buddhimatkāryayorapi vyāptigrāhiṇi dharmiṇyayameva vā prayogaḥ | athavobhaya-
trāpi yad yat sambandhagrāhi pratyakṣaṃ tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva, yathā vācyavācakayoḥ,
sambandhagrāhi ca pratyakṣaṃ kāryakāraṇayorapi pūrvavat | tadayaṃ yadi tattvataḥ kṛtsno'pi
kāryagrāmaḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaḥ, tathāpi kāryajātīnāmatyantavilakṣaṇānāmānantyāt,
pratijātibhedaṃ ca vyāptigrahaṇāpekṣaṇāt, yāvajjātikaṃ kāryaṃ puruṣapūrvakaṃ paricchinnam,
tāvata eva tadanumānamāñjasamiti yuktamuktam,
siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi |
tathā ca vahvereva dhūmabhasmāṅgārapākapāra[do]tsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛtiṣu kāryeṣu
yatra yatraiva pratibandhasādhakamadhyakṣaṃ pravṛttam, tata eva tadanumānam, nānyasmāt | evaṃ
devakulakalasaprāsādasyandanadukūlādiṣu vastuvṛtyā pauruṣeyeṣvapi yajjātīyeṣveva puruṣayopa
labdhirāsīt, tajjātikādeva kāryāt tadanumānamanumanyāmahe | dhārādharadharādharādijātau
punastadvyāpārānavadhāraṇāt kānumānavārtā, jātivaijātyasyātyantikasya sambhavena
vyāpteragrahāta ? gṛhītavyāpteśca kāryasyādarśanāt ||
krīḍāparvatakādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumā
nāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam |
kiṃ cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyanti cedīśinaḥ
kā vārtā phalasāmyasaṃvidi kuto he toviśeṣa sthitiḥ ||
[28b] iti hyanta raślokaḥ ||
kīdṛśī punaḥ kāryajāti: prayatnavatā vyāptetyāśaṅkaya tasyā apyānantyāt
saṃkṣepārthamucyate, yadṛṣṭerarthakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavatīti | tatra ca kṛtabuddhiriti
na sādhanabuddhiḥ, nāpyupādānādyabhijñalakṣaṇaprakṛtasādhyabuddhiḥ kiṃ tu kuvindādisvabhāva-
sādhyabuddhiḥ | tadabhāvāñca na sākṣādbhavadīyahetvasiddhiḥ prakṛtasādhyasiddhirvā vivakṣitā,
kiṃ tu ātyantika vaijātyapradarśana metat | tadddvāreṇa ca hetorasiddhiravyāptirvābhimataiva |
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
tathā hi śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādau kulālādi[sama] śilpibuddhirāvirasti,
naṃ malayamakarālayādau | tasyāḥ śilpibuddherbhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamātyantikamantareṇa
ityabhiprāyaḥ | vyāpteragrahaṇe smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśe vā devakulādāvapi na syādiyaṃ samānaṃ
śilpibuddhiḥ | tato yathā dhūmādagnibuddhirbhavantī gardabhādabhavantī dhūmād gardabhasya niyataṃ
jātibhedamāpādayati, tatheyamapi pariniścitapauruṣeyabhāvebhyo bhāvebhya: kailāsakuliśā-
dīnām |
kathaṃ punaranumānābhāva eva pratyetavya iti cet, kumbhakārādambhodadambholi-
prabhṛtisambhava iti svapne'pi śaṅkāvirahāt | anyathā kuvindapādamardanādanāvṛṣṭikaṣṭam
āviśet na lokaḥ, paracakrākrāntikātaro vā kṣitidharajaladhivyavadhamabhilaṣaṃstata
eva nirvṛttimāsādayet | kuvindasthānīyastatrāparo'pekṣyata eveti cet –na, samāne
kāryajanmani vijātīyakāraṇagaveṣaṇānupapatteḥ kuvindenaiva sādhyasiddheḥ | na hi paṭāntare
api kuvindādaparasyāpekṣā |
asti ca vastraviśeṣe viśiṣṭaśilpino'pekṣeti cet ? asti, yāvadeva tu
bastrāntareṇaikajātiparāmarśo dṛḍhaḥ, ata eva kuvindasyaiva śilpina: kalpanam | tadvi-
marśābhāve pauruṣeyatāyā eva sandehaḥ | merumandarādayastu na kenacit pauruṣeyeṇaika-
pratyavamarśabhājaḥ | tadeṣāmadhyakṣa siddhamatyantavaijātyaṃ śāṭhyādapahṛvānaḥ samānaśilpyanu-
mānaviraheṇa svīkāryate | siddhe ca jātibhede yādṛk kāryaṃ kumbhādi puruṣapratibaddhaṃ
siddham, na tādṛggarbhārbhakādi | yādṛk cedaṃ na tādṛk puruṣavyāptamiti siddhā asiddhiḥ
avyāptiśca dvayoḥ| evaṃ ca sthite prakṛtasādhyabuddhayajananadvārāṇi dūṣaṇāni dūram
apāstāni ||
PARA EKSPONDERE
tataśca
na hi vayaṃ prakṛtasādhyabuddherabhāvāt kāryatvādihetorasiddhi brūmaḥ | ki tahi ?
mandarādau kuvindasamaśilpibuddherabhāvādambarādisajātīyakāryatvāsiddhim |
prakṛtasādhyabuddhivedhuryamiti na kaścid doṣaḥ | kuvindasādhyāpekṣayā ca vyāptigrahaṇa-
smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśa eveṣṭa iti na bhūṣaṇavikalpāvakāśaḥ | kṛtakatvamātrapratītistu na
vivakṣitaiva | abhraṣṭasmaraṇānāṃ tāvad bhavatyeva puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ kṣityādiṣviti tu
dūramapakṛṣṭam |
bauddhakṛtasya hi [29a] kṛtabuddhiniṣedhasyāsiddhiḥ prastutā abhidhātum | na ca
sāśakyā, kṛtabuddhiśabdena śilpibuddherasya vivakṣitatvāt | puruṣakṛtabuddhibhāvavibhāvanaṃ
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
punaranupayogi | pratīta eva tasmin duṣaṇacinteyam | tatrāpya bhraṣṭasmaraṇānāmityasaṅgatam,
atyantavaijātyasiddheḥ sindhvāderanyato na vyāptipratīteḥ, smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśasya pari
hartumaśakyatvāt | ata eva jagat kenacit sṛṣṭamiti pralāpamātre ka āśvāsaḥ ?
prakṛtasādhyabuddhayāsiddhicodanaparihārādeva va vedeṣvapītyādi pratyādiṣṭam |
yadi tu pauruṣeyavākyāderatyantaṃ vedasya vaijātyamupadarśayet mīmāṃsakaḥ, tat kiṃ
samayamātreṇa parājetavyaḥ ? na tu tayoḥ svarūpadvāraka: śaktidvārako vā kaścid
viśeṣo'sti | tathā ca tat dvayamagṛhītasaṃketasya puraḥ paṭhitvā pratīhi kasya kīdṛśaṃ
viśeṣaṃ vyākurvīta śrotā, kiṃ na vā paśyasi garuḍādimantrakṛtaṃ viṣāpākaraṇādi ?
tadetadāyātam,
tasmāt,
eka: kāryaviśeṣameva kalayan hetorviśiṣṭaṃ nijaṃ
lakṣyāgneriva kāryamātramamunā vyāptaṃ samutpaśyati |
tajjātīyakameva kāryamaparo nāvaiti tadvetukaṃ
hanta dhvāntaviśeṣa eṣa viduṣāmadhyakṣavastunyapi ||
yad vācaḥ puruṣānvayavyatiricostaṃdbhāvabhājaḥ sthitā
nānyasmād vacasaśca vaidikagirāṃ bhedo'sti śakyātmanoḥ |
tulyātīndriyasūcanā ca niyataṃ naikatra cāśvāsanaṃ
vedastena na pauruṣeyapadavīmaprāpya viśrāmyati ||
yadi tat, kā kathā vicāragocarātītātyantikajātibhedeṣu kumbhādambhoda-
dambholiprabhṛtiṣu tajjātiniyatapratīteḥ pauruṣeyatāyāḥ ? yadapyanityatāsādhanāyopā-
labdham, tadapi nyāyabāhyam | pratyakṣeṇa pratibandhabodhādhikāre hi tādṛśī sajātīye-
taratvamīmāṃsā | anityatve kṛtakatvamātrasya viparyayabādhakapramāṇādanumānasvabhāvāt
pratibandhasiddhiriti na tatra jātiviśeṣānurodhaḥ | jātiviśeṣānavacchinne tu kṛtakamātre
vyāptisādhanasamarthamasamarthaṃ vā tat pramāṇamiti cintanīyam | śaktau na doṣasparśa: |
ata eva tatra ghaṭaśabdabhedena bhedodbhāvanaṃ dṛṣṭāntadāntikavaidharmyābhidhānamiti na
yuktam | yato dharmirūpādākṛṣṭadharmadvayasya vyāptivyavasthāpanād dharmavastveva dharmīti
tadbhedābhidhānasya dharmimātrabheda evārtha: |jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalauṃ
ihāpi tarhi kāryeṣu dharmiṣu pauruṣeyatvaṃ sādhyaṃ kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti na viśeṣaḥ
kaściditi cet ? ucyate, kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti ko'sya bhāṣitasyārtha: ? kiṃ tāvanmukhya-
tayā dharmamātre kāraṇasya kuṅkumādereva rāge vyāpārādevamucyate ? utasvit kāryena
kārye vyāptisiddheḥ, dhūmatvamātraṃ heturitivat ? yathā kṛtsno dhūmaḥ sādhyavyāptaḥ, tathā
yāvat kāryaṃ tat kṛtsnaṃ puruṣavyāpārajanmakamiti niścayāt | tadetadubhayamapi nirastam |
kṛtakatvamātramanityatvavyāptamiti tu kāyapara eva bhāvanirdeśaḥ, yāvat kṛtakaṃ tat
sarvamanityamityayamevārtha: | [29b] atrārthe pramāṇabale milite siddhe ca dhvaneḥ kṛta-
katve ghaṭa eva kṛtako'nityo dṛṣṭaḥ kathaṃ śabdaḥ syāditi niravakāśamevetyayamevārtho
dharmimātrabhedo'yamityanayā rītyā prakāśyate |
yathā hi svabhāva
hetvadhikāraprastāvāt sādhyasādhanadharmo vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayā
bhinnau vyavasthāpitau tathā dharmyapi śabdādiḥ, anyasya taddharmaṇo'bhāvāt | na cānyatra
dharmaṇi kṛtakavastunā anityavastusādhane dhvaneranityatāsiddhiḥ | tasya ca dharmiṇo ghaṭa-
śabdabhāvena bhedamāpādayan dūṣaṇamabhidhāya nigṛhyate dharmimātrabhedadvāreṇa prastute tu
kāryahetvabhimānād dhūmasthānīya : kāryarāśiḥ sādhyaśca bhinno'gnivat puruṣaḥ | kevalaṃ
nāgnivat taddeśakāla eva | kiṃ tu janmadeśakāle sannihito niśceyaḥ, bhasmakumbhābhyām
ivānalakulālau | tato yathā kulālapūrvo'yaṃ ghaṭo ghaṭatvādityupanyāse'pyutpattikāla-
deśasannihitavyāpāra : kulālo niścīyate, ghaṭaśca heturvastutaḥ, tathā puruṣe'pi sādhye
vastveva heturna kāryatvadharmaḥ, tathā sati puruṣavyāptāt kāryād vilakṣaṇaṃ kṣoṇīdharādi-
kāryamati vadatā sādhanavaisadṛśyamudbhāvitam, na dharmivesadṛśyam | tadā hi tadudayadeśa-
kālameva dharmi, na ca kalasādikāladeśāt kailāsādikāladeśavesadṛśyaṃ kaścid vaktumupa-
krānto yena dharmavai sadṛśyodbhāvanaṃ bhavet |
tasmād dahanarūpamātrād dahanānumānavat sādhanavai sadṛśyodbhāvanametadasiddhim
avyāpti vā darśayituṃ dharmiṇa iti tu viplavaḥ pareṣām | ayamevārtho yādṛk kāryatvaṃ
devakulādau puruṣavyāptaṃ pratītam, na tādṛg yugandharādāvityanayā diśopadiśyate |
yajjātīyaṃ devakulādi puruṣavyāptaṃ na tajjātīyaṃ yugandharādītyarthaḥ | atyantavejātyācca
kāryaśabdamātrasāmyamucyate na punarakāryavyāvṛtteḥ kacit nyūnabhāvaḥ | vyāptau tu kārya-
tvāderanantarbhāvaṃ brūmaḥ | ataeva sanmātreṇa sāmyaṃ nopayogi mūrtatvādineva dahanā-
numāne |
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
mañjaryāstu paryanuyogo'sthānapatitaḥ | ghaṭādijātireva puruṣavyāptā siddheti
vadatānyatra saṃśayamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt | kulālādimanuṣyakṛtabuddhiśca kṛtabuddhiruktā |
tadabhāvaśca jātibhede uttarīkṛtaḥ | sa cobhayasiddhatayā na visarjanānyavakāśayati |
na cātyantikajātibhedamantareṇopapadyata iti niveditam |
evaṃ vācaspaterapi viśeṣagaveṣaṇaṃ kṛtabuddhivaidhuryasyābhidheyaprayojanayoraparijñāna-
prayuktamiti veditavyam | yadi hi kṛtabuddhirnāstīti prakṛtasādhyabuddhirnāstīti vivakṣi
tam, tadā pratītikalahe'muṣmin kuto viśeṣādanyatra sā bhavati parvatādau tadabhāvānneti
cintyate | yadā tu kṛtabuddhirnāstīti [30a ] samāna śilpikṛtabuddhirnāstītyabhidheyam,
tatra ca na vivāda: | prayojanaṃ ca kumbhādibhyo'mbhodharāderatyanta vaijātyakhyāpanam |
tadavyaśakyaparihāram | tato gṛhītavyāptikebhyo'tyanta vilakṣaṇāt kathaṃ prakṛtasādhya-
buddhirityabhipretam ? tadā plavata eva sakalamevaṃvidham | utpattimanmātre ca vyāpti-
nirasanāt hantotpattimadityādyuttara kāladaṇḍakhaṇḍitameva | tena ghaṭe dṛṣṭavyāptikasya
ghaṭasajātīyameva buddhimatpūrvakam | yadā tu prāsādādāvapi vyāptigrahastadā tajjāterapi
tatpūrvakatva siddhirityapyuktam |
yaccā[tha] yajjātīyamityāśaṅkaya, ki kāryajātīyam ? tathā na dṛṣṭamityuttaram,
tadapi svābhāvika vikalpāvabhāsina : sāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa vyāptigrahaṇayogyatāsamartha-
nāt karthitam | tasmād yadapi aupādhikavikalpapratibhāsināpi rūpeṇa tajjātīya-
vyavahāro duṣpariharaḥ, vyāptigrahaṇe tu pratikṣiptatvānmahān viśeṣa iti |
ata eva vittokavikalpā api na kiñcit | tathā hi, yadyasmadabhiprāyapraśnaḥ,
tadā viśiṣṭeva kāryajātirdevakulakalasādilakṣaṇā buddhimāptā yaduṣṭehi parokṣakriya-
syāpyanubhūtasajātīyaśilpyanumānam sā na siddhā sindhubhūdharādau | kāryatvamātraṃ tu
na vyāptamityuccaistarāṃ tanvanta evāsmahe | tatra kimebhirvikalpairiti cintaya | yadviśeṣād
viśiṣṭā kāryajāti: sa viśeṣa: kimanirūpitarūpa evetyapi pāpīya:, pratyakṣasiddhānāṃ
kāryajātīnāṃ parasparavesadṛśyasyāpahrotumaśakyatvāt | vyāptistu viśiṣṭāyāṃ jātī
bhavatu kāryamātre vetyatra paramāpātato vimantumarhati | kathamanyathā svayamapi vastutva-
syāgnikāryatvāsaṃjananaṃ vyabhicāramālambya parihṛtam ? vyabhicārabuddhīnāṃ niyatajāti-
viṣayatve vivādābhāvādityāvirbhāvitameva | tasmādākārārthakriyāsāmarthyādivedanāt256
citrākāre jagati
jyāyasī |
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
niyatamīśvaraprasādādevālaukikamekākāramālokitamasyetyupekṣaiva
yadapi prācīnamupādānodāharaṇamasya kāryamātre vyāptisamohayā, tadapi naupa-
yikam, tatrāpi pratyakṣavyāpārasyāśakyasādhanatvāt,
naisargikavikalpaviṣayatvāt,
upādānasya dṛśyādṛśyasvabhāvatvācca | tat kimidānīmupādānena kārya rāśervyāptireva
nāsti ? āhosvit pramāṇāntaragamyā bhavatviti cet ? ubhayatra saṃśayaḥ, sato'pi
vyabhicārasya viparyayabādhakānumānasya vānullekhasaṃbhavādidānīmekāntahetorabhāvāt |
tadayaṃ sopādānaṃ sarvotpattiriti sarvatantra siddhānto'virodhādanuvṛttaḥ, yāvacca kāryam
ālokayāmastāvadupādānavadevetyavigānena vyavahāro'pi | na ca kāryaparyantabodhaḥ
pṛthagjanasyeti tanīyasāpi viparītāṃśena saṃśayo durvāra: | buddheśca buddhirupādānaṃ niścitā
iti vijñānasya vijñānā[ nyā]nupādānācca sidhyatīti na virudhyate, tato yadi siddhāntā-
dapi [30b] tadvyāptivyavasāyo na kācit kṣatiḥ | pratyakṣāt tu mā bhūt, kevalamatra
pakṣe'cetanopādānatvaheturekadeśasiddhaḥ śaṅkayeteti vyavasthā | sā cāyātaiva, ki kriya-
tām ? viparyayabādhakapramāṇalābhe tu sāpi na syāt | kevalaṃ pratyakṣeṇa kṛtsnakārya -
vyāptivāde'nudāharaṇamevedam | ataḥ pratyakṣasya jātiviśeṣe vyāpāraniyamaprasādhanād
viśeṣahetvabhāvādityādyapi dhvastam ?
yatpunaraparasya' viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsapauruṣam, tatrāpi prathamadvitayaṃ
tāvad bādhakaṃ dhūmasyeva siddhāyāmeva tadutpattau tatsādhakapratyakṣānupalambhasya viśiṣṭa-
jātyadhikāreṇa pravṛttisādhanād viśiṣṭameva ghaṭādikāryaṃ prati śakyam | evaṃ ca yadi
buddhimantamantareṇa jāyeta sakṛdapi tato na bhavet, aniyatahetutve vāhetutvamiti na
kāryamātraṃ prati tasya puruṣādutpattiprasādhanābhāvāt | tataśca tat kāryaṃ yat puruṣapūrvam
ityapi niravakāśam ||
nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ, svakāraṇāyattasannidheradṛṣṭapariṇāmasahakāriṇaḥ
kāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasya satatamabhāve'pi kāryāṇāṃ kādācitkatopapatteḥ, yadapekṣayā nitya-
śakterapi īśvarasya śaśtranna karaṇa] [tva]m | ekāvasthāniyame hi kāraṇāntarāṇāṃ pravṛtti-
nivṛttisādhanīcchā prārthyeta | sa ca nāsti, bījasyocchūnataratamādibhāvavat pariṇāma-
1. śatānandasyeti prāntalekhaḥ |
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
paramparāparicayasya teṣāmapotumaśakyatvāt | astu vā ekāvasthāniyama īśvarasya
icchāyā api nityatvāt tadavastha: kāryāvirāmaḥ, anitye tu yadapekṣo'syā: kadācid
bhāvaḥ, tadapekṣayā kāryagrāmasya yadi syāt kīdṛśo doṣa: ? kumbhādikāryakrame'pi tarhi
ki puruṣecchayā, yadapekṣo'syāḥ kramaḥ, tadapekṣa eva kumbhāderapyastīti vaktuṃ śakteḥ ?
tadayuktam, pramāṇena dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya hetorapohitumaśakyatvāt | prastute tu pramāṇā-
bhāvāt kāryakādācitkatāmātramāśritaṃ tadanyathāpyupapatsthata iti kutaḥ puruṣāpatti-
niyamaḥ kāryasya ?
atha kumbhāde: kadācidbhāva: puruṣādhīno dṛṣṭa iti kāryāntarasyāpi tatheti
cet ? evaṃ tarhi tadeva darśanādarśanamātraṃ vyāptisādhanamāyātam, kimatra viparyayabādhako-
panyāsaśauṭīryeṇeti tṛtīyamapi nirastam ||
yaccocyate, kāraṇasannidherdhīdhanādhīno niścita iti tatrāpi tathā darśanamātrā -
śraye etadeva vācyam | viparyayabādhakaṃ ca na kiñciduktam | pratyakṣānupalambhaśaraṇīkaraṇe
ca vātopaghātādimilajjambālabījādisāmagrathā anaikāntikatvādi sarvamākṣepaparihāra-
sametaṃ kāryavadavagantavyaṃ sāmagrī viśeṣa eva vyāptiyogya ityetatparyantam | tanna kāraṇa-
sāmagrayā: puruṣeṇa vyāptisiddhiḥ, yato vipakṣe vyāpakānupalambhādasambhava iti caturtha-
mapi karthitam ||
tāva taiva vācaspaterapi [31a] hṛdayaśūnya: pralāpo'pahastitaḥ | yathā hi vi-
tatānāṃ tāvadajananabījamuktamavasthāviśeṣābhāvo nāma | yadyapi daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ puruṣā-
deva milanamupalabdhaṃ tatprayatnasacivānāṃ ca kāryārambhaḥ, tathāpi sarvatra sarvadā vā
tathaiveti niyamayituḥ pramāṇasyābhāvāt kāryotpādavyāpakasyāpi kāraṇasamavadhānasya
buddhimadadhīnatvena vyāptaya siddhestadavastho doṣaḥ | yathā ca kāraṇāntaradaśāviśeṣāśraye -
ṇaiva kāryāṇāṃ kadācid bhāvastathā prakṛtaviśeṣo'pīti pañcamaṃ ca pañcatāmañcitam ||
kāraṇamātrāpattisādhanaṃ punaretaditi darśitaṃ śāstre ||
etenaiva śaṅkaroktamapi nāpi kaścid viśeṣa ityādi kāvyaracanāmātramā
pāditam, pratibandhasādhakapramāṇaparyādānāt | yadyapi ca nirabhiprāyavyāpāratvena prāsā-
dādihetubhyo bhūbhūdharādihetūnāṃ na viśeṣastathāpi prayatnavadapekṣānapekṣābhyāṃ yadi syāt
ko doṣaḥ ? yathā pārthivatvā viśeṣe'pi lohalekhyatvālohalekhyatve | avaśyaṃ ca nirabhi-
33jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalī
prāyatvāviśeṣe'pi viśeṣa eṣāmeṣitavyaḥ śakteḥ kathamanyathā kāryavaijātyamātyantikam ?
tadasau śakti: prayatnavadapekṣāve mukhyamapi yadi kṣameta kā kṣatiḥ ? kiṃ ca karturapi
karādivyāpāramantareṇa samīhāmātrāt na mūrtakāryasiddhirupalabdhā, tamativartamānānāṃ
bhūdharādīnāṃ kā gaṇanā samīhāmātre ?
karādayo'pi samīyā pravartyanta iti cet ? samīhāpi sanniveśini śayādi-
vyāpāravirahe na kiñcitkarītyuktam | tato yayā śaktayā karādivyāpārapāravaśyamapāsya
mahīdharādihetavo nirabhiprāyatve satyapi na kāryakarmaṇi pratihanyante tayā samīhāmapi
nātikrameyuriti ka evaṃ śraddadhīta ? na hi dhūmodayakāle ucchaladbahalarūpa vastu vahnī-
ndhanajanyatayā sambhāvitamekābhāvaniścaye niścīyamānamanyābhāve'pi na bhāvaśaṅkāyāṃ
niveśayati, tādṛgetadapi ||
śarīrasvīkāre tu prādeśika kāryānityāne kāsarvajñatvāt sādhu sādhita: sudhī-
bhirīśvaraḥ | etenaiva vā vyabhicāra : kāryatvādeḥ | na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāmityādi[va]canād
darśanādarśanamātrādanyamupāyamasya vyāptisādhanāya spṛśati tacca kṛtottaram | yadi ca
darśanādarśanameva śaraṇam, tadā yathā samīhāvataḥ kāryakriyā dṛṣṭeti kārye sati samīhā-
vato'numānamiṣṭam tathā karādimata eva mūrtakriyā dṛṣṭeti karādivyāpārānupapattau
puruṣasyākriyaiva kasmāt na niścīyate ? na khalu kāryahetuvyāpakānupalambhayoḥ prāmāṇye
kaścid viśeṣaḥ | yadi tu darśanādarśanamātramanāsthāya pramāṇāntaramekaniyataṃ syāt,
syādekasādhyabuddhiḥ, tadabhāve tu pratibandha [31b] eva tayoḥ parasparam, na bādhā tulya-
kakṣatvāditi prakaraṇasamaḥ parābhiprāyāt |
prayogaḥ, yo na svāṅgavyāpāravān nāsau mūrtanirvartanasamartho dṛṣṭaḥ, yathā kulāla
eva saṃhṛtakarā divyāpāradaśāyām | nāsti ca svāṅgavyāpāraḥ prakṛte puṃsīti vyāpakā-
nupalabdhi: | nāśrayāsiddhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyanyāyeneti vastutastarhi dūṣaṇāntarameva yuktaṃ,
kaḥ pratihetoravakāśa iti cet -na, bhūyodarśanasya vyāptisiddhāvana ṅgatvapratipādanārthamasyo-
panyāsāt | yadi bhūyodarśanamupāya: tadaivamapi syādityutteriti vyāptigrahaprakārāṇām
ayogādanekānta iti sthitam |
astu vā vyāptigrahaḥ kathañcit tathāpi neśvarasiddhipratyāśā phalavatī, buddhi-
mataḥ sādhyasyaikatvaniyamaniścayābhāvāt | ekatve hi tasya siddhe nityavibhusavaṃjñatva-
īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam
siddhirīśvaravyavahāramāropayet | yadā tu bhinnadeśakālakalitaṃ kāryajātamanekena saṃkhyāti-
krāntena kartrā kṛtaṃ sambhāvyeta, na tadā vibhutvanityatve, svasvaviṣayopādānādimātravedana-
siddhau ca ka sarvajñatvam ?
atha bahūnāṃ vyāhṛtamanasāṃ vyāpāre kāryasyānutpattirupanyasya vilopādiprasaṅgaśca
syāditi cet ? pratyekaṃ vaibhavādiguṇayogādīśvarāṇāṃ vyāpāre syādapīyamāśaṅkā, adya
punareko'pi tādṛ na sidhyatītyucyate | arvācīnaśaktayaśca bhūyāṃsa ekamanekaṃ ca kāryam
ārabhya niṣpādayanto dṛśyanta eva | nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenaikena bhāvyam, balīyasā
vā, sūtradhāravat senānīvad vā | atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvṛttitvāditi cet -na,
tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt, svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcidekasattvādighaṭanā-
darśanāt | tatrāpi kaścideva prathamaḥ prayojaka ityapi nāsti, anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyā
anivāraṇāt, nīcasthāpi prayojakatvasambhavāt |
tasmād bhramaramadhumakṣikāvalmīkajantuvat kṣudraprāṇibhirapaye ke kamainākādikaraṇa-
sambhāvanāyāṃ kā vārtā viśvasyaikena kriyāyāḥ ? tatrādṛṣṭajanmānastāvat tāvataiva
kṛtārthīkṛtacetanānumitayaḥ kṣitidharādayaḥ | te ca kṣudrajantava upādānamatikṣudraṃ pṛthivyā-
didravyamupakaraṇaṃ sukhādisampradānamātmānaṃ sthitisukhādi ca prayojanaṃ jānanta eva
valmīkajantuvat pravarteran | siddhe ca nāvaśyamadhiṣṭhāyakā dṛśyeran vicitraśakti-
karmākṣepāt svabhāvaviprakarṣād vā | ye'pi dṛṣṭajanmāno vṛkṣādayaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ, tatra
cintaiva nāsti | adṛṣṭapuruṣavyāpārāstu ye bindhyayugandha rādiparisaradbhāvāste'pi piśā-

tathānumīyamānā api jantavaḥ svakīyakaramukhādijñānenāpyante bhaviṣyanti |

alam |

prabhāvātiśayasahāyāpekṣāyāṃ ki śilpena ? na tadantareṇa tasya śaktiriti

iti, upayuktasarvajñapakṣasya mukhyatayā vakṣyamāṇatvāt | athavā vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyayostatra

kṛtāyā anekato nivṛtterasādhanatvāt | yadi ca kathañcidasau na svīkurute, svīkārayituṃ
tarhi caraṇamadanādinārādhanīya : prativādīti,

prasaukyamapāye'sya na hyanekatvamīhitam ||

iti | dṛṣṭānte'siddhireva tāvadekena karaṇasya | siddhāvapi vā sandeha eva kasya, yadartham

saṃśaya hetava eveti |
tathā ca śaṃkara evāha, na karturekatvenācetanopādānatvasyāvyabhicāra ityādi |
yat punarāha, na caivamacetanopādānatvasya prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānamātreṇa vyabhicāra iti, na

|| prathamaḥ khaṇḍaḥ ||

iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā ||
iti | dṛṣṭo'nto dṛṣṭāntaḥ siddhānta iti yo'rthaḥ prayatnavanmātreṇa vyāpteḥ siddhatvāt,
ekānekarūpānatikramāñca vastunaḥ | sthitvā pravṛttyādiṣūpanyasteṣu vādina iṣṭasiddhiḥ kimastu
ekatvapakṣe, asiddhimātraṃ vānekatve, atha vyāptireva nāstīti siddhānte saṃśaya eva
ubhayatrāpīti praśnārthaḥ |
atra cānantaramabhedasādhanādhikāreṇa sandigdha vipakṣavyāvṛttikatvodbhāvanena
dattamevottaram | atastṛtīya eva pakṣaḥ | na hi prayatnopayogamantareṇāpi kāryajanmani

kāladeśādyaniyamaprasaṅgo bādhakaḥ ? tadayuktam, [yataḥ] pratiniyataśakterasarvakālabhāvinaḥ
svakāraṇāyattasannidheḥ kāraṇadaśāviśeṣasya vyatireke'pi vyatirekaḥ kāryasya saṃbhavanna
prayatnavannāntarīyakatvamupakalpayituṃ kalpate | sarvaṃthā hetvanapekṣāyāṃ tadbādhakamupapadyamānaṃ
kāryasya hetumātreṇa vyāpti sādhayet | na tu hetuviśeṣeṇa prayatnavatā |
nanu kāraṇaṃ nāma sarvatra kalāpa eva, saca na vyagrāvasthāyām | tatsaṃhatiśca
prayatnavantamantareṇa yadi syāt, nityameva syāt | evaṃ deśe'pi vācyam | tataśca
sa eva deśakālaniyamaprasaṅga iti, caitanyanirapekṣatvena kalāpakāryatvasya vyāpakasyābhāvena
kāryatvādayo'saṃbhavantaḥ prayatnavadapekṣatvena vyāpyanta iti cet ? evaṃ tarhi so'pi prayatna -
vān yadi kṣaṇika: prādeśikaśca tatkṣaṇaikadeśatvameva sarvakāryagrāmasya syāditi sanātana
evāṅgīkartavyo vyāpī ca | tataśca sa eva deśakālāniyamo'dyāpi prasakta iti
kimasyopagamena ? atha so'dṛṣṭamapekṣya janayanniyataṃ janayet ? jaḍānāṃ tu nādṛṣṭaṃ
locana miti |
evaṃ tarhi tadadṛṣṭaparipākasahāyā eva pratyayā niyatamutpādayiṣyanti nirālocā
apīti kiṃ caitanyeneti cet ? evaṃ bruvataḥ kulālāderapi vaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ, na hi tatrāpi
nādṛṣṭamasti sahakāri | na caivam | tasmād viparyayaḥ | yā yā sāmagrī sā nādṛṣṭā-
pekṣayā puruṣaprayatnaṃ viphalayati | [ 39a ] yathā sūtrapiṇḍadaṇḍacakrādiḥ | sāmagrī cajñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
girisāgarādijaniketi viruddhavyāptopalabdhi: | prayatnaviphalīkaraṇaṃ hi tadanapekṣatvam
ambarādau siddhaṃ niṣedhyam | tena yad viruddhaṃ prayatnāpekṣatvaṃ tadvayāptaṃ sāmagrītvam, tasthā
yatnakāryatvāt |
atrocyate | yadi prayatnakārya sāmagrī sarvopasaṃhāreṇa sidhyed yuktametat | na
caivam, na hi tatrāpi viparyaye bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti | yathā hi kārya svakāraṇāyattasannidheḥ
kāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasyāpekṣayā asarvakālabhāvi saṃbhāvyate, tathā sāmagrathapi kiṃ na syāt,
yato nityaṃ bhāvaprasaṅgaścodyeta ? tataścānirvātita vipakṣavṛttiśaṅkā sāmagro yadi prayatnāpekṣāṃ
niyacchet, sākṣātkāryatvādibhireva kīdṛśo'parādhaḥ kṛtaḥ, yena tadupanyāse saṃśayitasya
sāmagrī śaraṇamupakṣipyate ?
• mṛdādayaḥ puruṣādeva milanto dṛṣṭā iti cet ? kāryamapi prayatnavata eva jāya-
mānamupalabdhamiti kiṃ nocyate ? yathā ca yadyapi kimapi kāryaṃ prayatnavato dṛṣṭam, tathāpi
kāryāntaraṃ tiraskṛtyāpi buddhimantaṃ bhaviṣyatīti śaṅkā, tathā sāmagrayapi saṃbhāvyamānā
kamarthaṃ puṣṇāti ? tato'nukkasamametat | tasmāt sāmagrīmapi madhye prakṣipya kumbhādiṣu
sāmagrayāstathā darśanameva pramāṇayitavyam | tathā ca sati kāryameva pratyakṣānupalambhaiḥ
prayatnavannāntarīyakaṃ siddhamityeva sādhu | kimatra vyāptisiddhaye bādhakapramāṇopanyāsa-
śauṭīryeṇa ? atha vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa pratyakṣānupalambhā jātiviśeṣameva viṣayīkartuṃ śaknuyuriti
na kāryamātraṃ prayatnavatā vyāptaṃ sidhyet ? tadarthaṃ viparyayabādhāśrayaṇam, evaṃ tarhi sāmagrayā
api prayatnavatkāryatve ta eva pratyakṣānupalambhāḥ śaraṇamiti evaṃvidhā saṃhatiḥ prayatnavatā
kriyata iti yuktaḥ sarvopasaṃhāraḥ | tathā ca,
na vyagrādudayaḥ kacinna ca cayaścaitanyaśūnyād bhaved
bhāve ki na sadā sadātanatanorapyeṣa doṣaḥ samaḥ |
tasyādṛṣṭamapekṣya kālaniyame kiṃ cetasā cet tadā
kumbhādāvapi śilpino viphalatā naitañca tadvyatyayaḥ ||
kumbhādau yadi darśanādabhividhiḥ kiṃ vyatyaye bādhayā
pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ kimu matā na vyāptirevaṃ sati |
teṣāṃ jātiviśeṣa eva viṣayo yadyevamevaṃvidho
vyūhaścetanato bhavediti bhavedanyatra ko niścayaḥ ||
iti saṃgrahaślokau !!
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
na ca sāmagrayantarasyātatpūrvakatve asthā api mā bhūditi yuktam, asarva-
vyāpināmapi dharmāṇāṃ pradeśavṛtterdarśanāt lohalekhanasyeva pārthive, asiddhaśarīra-
pūrvaṃkatvasyeva vā kārye | tatra bādhakānna sarvavyāpitvamiti cet ? tadasphuraṇe tarhi
saṃśaya: kena nivāryate | yathā hi na parasya bādhakaṃ kalāpāntare'pi kāryāntarādau vā
cetanāpekṣāyāḥ, tathā bhavato'pi sarvajātau tayāvaśyaṃbhāvyamiti na sādhakamasti |
yathā ca tava kacidbuddhimadapekṣā darśanamasti, tathā parasyāpyekatra dṛṣṭasya [39b] dharmasya
bhinnajātīyāvyāptidarśanamasti | tato lohalekhanasya śarīravyāpārasya ca kacid
bādhakādarśanaṃ sandehasādhanamupayuktameva parasya, anyathā saṃśayasyaiva nirbījatāprasakteḥ |
na ca sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ prārabdho'dhunābhidhātum yatastadvadatra bādhakānupadarśanaṃ
bādhakaṃ syāt prativadituḥ api tu sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva | tacca siddhaṃ,
dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭimātreṇa vyāpterasiddhe: nibandhanāntarasyābhāvāt | etena kṣityādihetūnām
acetanatve sati niyatapravṛttitvena prāsādādihetuvat prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānāsiddhirityapi
pratyuktam | acetaso'pi kālādiniyatāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakatvasādhaka-
pramāṇasya tadvadevābhāvāditi |

samānanyāyatayā āṃgatameva buddhipratibandhaṃ paraparitoṣāya sādhāraṇānai kāntikatvena
dūṣayitumāha,
sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthāna viśeṣārthakriyādiṣu |

iti | vāśabdaḥ samuccaye | eṣu satsu yadiṣṭaṃ caitanyaṃ tasya dṛṣṭānte sādhanavati dharmaṇi
siddhirasiddhiśca ghaṭādau viṭapādau ca yathākramam | tato vyaktaṃ vipakṣaikadeśe vṛttireṣāmiti
bhāvaḥ | etena yadi kṛtakādivad viparyayabādhābhidhānamaśakyam, dhūmādivat pratyakṣā-
nupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekapratītiḥ prayatnena saha kāryādīnāṃ bhaviṣyatīti gatyantaram

iti | yadā kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk kalasasya vyatireka: pratyetavyaḥ, tadā na sādhyā-
bhāva[kṛto ghaṭa] vyatireka: pratītaḥ syāt, sādhyābhāvasya sandehāt | na hi tathāvidha -
śarīropādhikena cetasā vyāptirjijñāsitā, yato'nupalabdhi viśeṣeṇa niṣedhaḥ sidhyet,
kiṃ tu prayatnavanmātreṇa | tasya ca yathā vṛkṣādijanmasamaye saṃbhāvanā niṣedhasyāśakya-

bodhayituṃ na śaknotīti sandigdhavyatirekaḥ |
nanu sādhyābhāve sādhanasya bhāvasaṃśaye sandigdho vyatireka iti yuktam, na tu
kulālavyāpārāt prāk kumbhabhāva: sandihyata iti cet ? tadayuktam, sādhyavyatireka-

sādhyasādhanadharmitvaṃ dṛṣṭāntayordoṣa ucyate |

na ca tāvatā vyāptigrahaḥ | anyathā pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāpti pratipadya pavanopaghāta -

siddha iti syād vyāptiḥ |

tu
tacca kāyavatkāle'pyasti viśeṣasaṃbhave sāmānyasyāvaśyaṃbhāvāditi tadapekṣayā vyāptigrahaḥ

nantaramupajāyamānamapi tadupāyavādinaṃ pramāṇīkaroti, sādhanamapi vā kṛtakatvaṃ vastutaḥ
asādhanāṅgo vyāpakatvenopanīyamānamanityatāsiddhau |

viṣayaḥ kiṃ na vyavasthāpyate ? na hi lābhe praveśaḥ, chede niḥsaraṇamiti labhyam |
vahnistu deśakālaviprakṛṣṭo'pi tadātmā sannihita iva svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭa [40b]-
pratyakṣādiyogyatayā tadanupraveśamāsādayatīti yuktam, yatastadekādhyavasāyāt sarva eva
dhūmavyāpakatayāvadhāryamāṇo na duṣyati, jāṭharaṃ tadayogyatayā tathā niścāyi | ata eva
dhūmādabhimate śikhini pravṛttirasaṃśayānasya yujyate | itarathā pratyakṣāyogyenāpi vyāptiḥ
āśrayabhujā gṛhyamāṇā dhūmasya tadyogyāyogyadahanasāmānyaviṣayaiva vyavatiṣṭhata iti

svarūpaviśeṣaniṣṭhaṃ pramāṇaṃ sāmānyena vyāpti prapadyate |
anityatvena tu kṛtakatvasya vyāpti viparyayabādhakapramāṇamadhigacchad bhūtvā-

pravartamāno'bhimatānityai kāgrabuddhiḥ kaścit pravṛttimarhati | ataśca sāmānyaparyavasitamapi
pramāṇaṃ na viśeṣeṇa vyāpti gṛhṇātīti siddham | uktaṃ ca nyāyānusāriṇā śaṃkareṇa, yat
pramāṇaṃ yāvatīmarthaṃgati vyāpnotītyādi | yat pramāṇaṃ yatsvabhāvasāpekṣapravṛttikaṃ tannaiva

anyanivṛtterupalakṣaṇād vyāptigraha iti | yadyeṣa eva nyāya:, tadā tadicchatāmanibandhanaḥ

uktakrameṇa gardabhenāpi tasya prasaṅge vahnāvapi hastakatyāgāt | yadā tu gatyaṃntara mapi tatra
prakṛtāsaṃbhavi saṃbhavi, tadā kuto vandīkaraṇaṃ śaraṇam ?
evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāraḥ tadatiprasaṅgabhayādevāśrīyate, na tu sa eva
samaya iti cet ? evaṃ sati bhavataiva kimayamatiprasaṅge bharo datto neti kośapānaṃ
kartavyam, yo hi pratyakṣānupalabdhī vihāya vihāyasi vavyāpāranivṛttyā dhūmanivṛttim
ādāya vyāptimabhidhatte, taṃ prati yathā vastumātrasyāpi tatra vyāpāroparamāttenāpi
vyāptisiddhiḥ syādityatiprasaṅgaḥ, tathā yo'pi pratyakṣānupalabdhīruddhūya tadyogyapuruṣa -
viśeṣavyāpāraviraheṇa vyomani ghaṭādikāryatvanivṛtti darśayitvā tena vyāptimasya
manyate, taṃ prati puruṣamātrasyāpi tatra nivṛttyā tenāpi vyāptiḥ, tathā kāryāntaratvasyāpi
nivṛttyā tasyāpi syāditi vyaktamatiprasaṅgamātrametat, na nyāya iti paśyāmaḥ |
dhūme gardabha divyabhicāradarśanāśa vastumātreṇa vyāptiriti yuktam, puruṣamātrasya
tu vyabhicārānupalabdherna damatiprasaṅgamātrodbhāvanaṃ bhaviṣyati | naivaṃ samānanyāyānām
ekatra bādhakadarśanamanyatrāpi śaṅkāmutpādayati | yadi hi vihāyasi ubhayanivṛttidarśanaṃ
pratibandhasādhakaṃ bhavet, vastudhūmayorapi na bādhyeta, tatra tu bādhyamānamanyatrāpi katham
ekāntāvasāyasādhanaṃ syāt ? na ca pakṣīkṛte neva vyabhicāra ityapi, na pakṣīkaraṇaṃ
mantraprabhāvaḥ, kiṃ tu vyāptigrāhakadārḍhyam | tacca yadi nabhasi ubhayābhāvamātram, tadā
tatra bādhakādhigaterastaṃ dāḍhamiti satyapi [42a ] pakṣīkaraṇavyabhicārāśaṅkā na
nivartata iti |

iti saṃgrahaḥ ||
tasmāt nākāśe dvayanivṛttyā vyāptisiddhiḥ, siddhavyāptikayostvabhāvadarśanaṃ
gṛhītavyāptismaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt | na ca vyāptigrāhakaṃ kiñcidupapadyata ityuktam | tasmāt
anvayamātrabhāve'pi vyatirekābhāvādanekānta eveti sthitam | vastutastu vyatirekavadanva-
yo'pyasya durlabha eva | yasya hi pratyakṣāgocaratayā abhāvaprayuktaḥ kāryābhāva iti
pratyetumaśakyaṃ tasyānvayo dūrotsārita eva, pratyakṣagrāhyatvāt tasya | pratyakṣaṃ hi paridṛśyamāne
vastuni deśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi svapravṛttiyogya
mevāntarbhāvya vyāptimavakalpayet na svabhāva-
viprakṛṣṭamapīti uktaprāyam | tataścānvayamātraṃ gajanimīlitenāvadhīrya vyatirekābhāvenaiva
duṣaṇamuktam | vastutastu nānvayo na vyatireka iti prayatnavanmātre sādhye kāryatvamasādhā-
raṇameveti vā darśayitumāha,
saṃśayo'thavā
iti | pratyakṣādiyogyāpekṣayā sādhāraṇānaikāntikam, caitanyamātrāpekṣayā asādhāraṇam
ityartha: | nanu śarīropādhibuddhikṛtaṃ kārya sidhyat buddhimātrakṛtaṃ sidhyatyeva, śiśapākṛtamiva
vṛkṣakṛtam, viśeṣe sāmānyānapavāditi kathamucyate'nvayābhāvaḥ ? evaṃ sati vyatireko'pi
tadapekṣayā syāditi cet ? kā no hāniḥ, buddhimati kāryahetoranvayavyatirekavattvābhyupaga-
māditi ? uktamatra, evamanvayavyatirekakalpane jāṭharacitrakā digatenāpi rūpeṇa dhūmādanumi-
tamagni saṃśayāno nābhimataikāgracittaḥ pravarttatetyādi |
api ca na tatra saṃbhavītyeva pratyakṣeṇa yatkiñcidvastuno rūpaṃ kāryasya vyāpakam
avadhāryate, api tvadhyavasāyāpekṣayā | adhyavasāyaśca puruṣeṇa kṛta eva iti buddhimatā
veti viśiṣṭa viṣaya eva pravartate, tādṛśyeva puruṣādiśabdasya rūḍhe: | na tu karādivyā-
pāranirapekṣeṇa caitanyamātreṇeti, caitanyamātraṃ sadapyudāsīnamanvayagrahaṇakāle'dhyava-
sāyasya viśeṣonmukhenaiva pravṛtteḥ, sāmānyaśabdatve'pi vā prakṛtaviśeṣamākṣipyaivāgni-
vyāptivat | sa cādhyavasāya: pratyakṣavyāpārānusārī tadyogyameva rūpaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt,
na tu tadayogyamapi jāṭharādivat tārṇādivacca evaṃ puruṣeṇāpi vyāptī kasyacit
"jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
śarīropādhividhurasya buddhimātrasya tadayogyasya pratikṣepaḥ syādeva | apratikṣepastu kharvādi-
bhedasyaiya | ayameva nyāyaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣeṇānvayagrahaṇe |
[42b] athāṅgārasaṅgādagurukhaṇḍajanitaṃ dhūmamupalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣayogyatayā
indhanādyantareṇāpi tadanvayaprasaṅga iti cet ? tatkimidānīṃ pramāṇaviṣayapratiniyamam
anādṛtya yatra kacit pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ yena kenacidanvayaṃ pratyetviti vivakṣitam ? evaṃ
sati hetumadābhāsavyavasthāvilopāt sarvasya sarvasiddhiriti pratiniyatasādhanānveṣo
viphalaḥ |
atha pratyakṣeṇa svayogyamullaṃghyāpi vyāptigṛhītetyucyate ? tadasiddham | yadāpi
pratyakṣaṃ svapravṛttiyogye'pi vastunyavāntarabhedāpekṣayā sāmānyamudāsayadanvayaṃ pratipadyate,
tadā kaiva kathā svapravṛttyayogyasyātyantaṃ vijātīyasya ? na cāsmākaṃ pakṣa: pratyakṣayogyeṇa
sarveṇa vyāptiriti kiṃ tu pratyakṣayogyeṇaiva tatkṛtā vyāptiriti | anyathā gardabhādibhirapi
dhūmakumbhāderevānvayaprasaṅgaḥ | kimataḥ param ? kathaṃ punaratrāvāntarabhedāpekṣa eva vyāptigraho
na darśanayogyatāmātrāpekṣaḥ ? vikalpastu vāsanāprabodhamātrārthamapekṣitapratyakṣādisannidhira-
niyatodayākāratayā na pratiniyataṃ viśeṣamāveśayitumarhatīti |
satyam, ataeva vyatirekasādhanyā anupalabdheravatāraḥ | tatra yathā vahni -
puruṣābhyāṃ dhūmakumbhayoranvayādhyavasāye sahāyatāmanupalabdhi pratipadyate, pūrvasthitiranyata
utpattiranyata āgamanamiti tridhā bhinnasaṃbhavavyatirekaṃ sādhayantītarathānupayogāt,
tathā yadi gardabhānvaye vedanamātrānvaye vā pratipadyeta, syādeva tābhyāmapi vyāptiḥ,
nānyathā, yato na pratyakṣamātraṃ vyāpti pratipadyate, nāpyanupalambhamātraṃ kiṃ tu pratyakṣānupa-
lambhāvanyonyasahāyāviti nirṇītaṃ śāstre bahuśa: | asmābhirapi trika pañcaka cintāyāṃ
kiñciditi |
na ca gadaṃbhādyanvaye tasyāḥ sāhāyakamasti | etena dhūmaviśeṣāpekṣayānupalambha-
vyāpārābhāvo vyākhyāta iti naivavādini kaścit paryanuyogaḥ | yastu pratyakṣa gocare'pi
tatkṛtāṃ vyāptimupavarṇayati tasya tadviṣaya eva vyāptigrahaviraha iti duḥsthā vyavasthā |
tataśca tasyaivāsau paryaṃnuyogaḥ | tasyāpyanupalabdhivyāpārābhāvānneti cet –na, [yataḥ]
pratyakṣa yogye'pi tatkṛtavyāptivādino'nupalambhavyāpāravirahe'pi tatkṛtavyāptimicchataḥ
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
kaḥ pratiroddhā ? yadi hyasya vrīḍā syādapratyakṣayogya eva tadvayāpāraṃ kathaṃ varṇayet ?
athopādānādividā prayatnavatā kāraṇadarśanādeva gardabhasya nirāsaḥ, kimatrānupalabdhyā ?
evaṃ tarhi dṛśyamānenaiva vyāptimupavarṇayan [ na ca] darśanapathātikrāntena, na ca
śarīropādhi vyavadhūya caitanyamātramupalabdhaṃ kacit | yadi ca darśanabalādeva vyavasthā
caitanyamātrādhiṣṭhitaṃ śarīraṃ kumbhādi janayat dṛṣṭameveti na gardabhenānvayavirodhaḥ, tat
kathamanupalabdhi[43a]pratikṣepa: ? vyāpakagatā: sāmānyadharmā eva vyāptau sādhakāḥ
itareṣāṃ vyabhicāradarśanenānyatra śaṃkāvakā [śā ] deva na gardabhenānvaya iti cet ? nanu
vyabhicāradarśana miti tadabhāve'pi bhāvadarśana mityanupalabdhivyāpārābhāve'sādhanatvam
upanīyamānamanupalabdhereva sādhanāṅga niścaye vyāpāraṃ paridīpayati |
yadi ca viśeṣe vyāpāraśaṃkākula: sāmānyamanusarati bhavān, upādānādya-
bhijñamapi viśeṣamapahāya caitanyamātreṇa gadaṃbhasādhāraṇena siddhasādhanayogyena tato'pi
vā sāmānyena kāraṇamātreṇa vyāptimabhidhattām | evaṃ hi sati sarvathā dūrīkṛtaḥ
śaṃkāvakāśaḥ syāditi | etāvattu sāmānyamavamanya upādānādyabhijña viśeṣe sthitirna
tu tadapyavajñāya yathādṛṣṭa iti kimatra sāmarthyamanyatra jāḍyāt ? pratyakṣānupalambhavādi-
śaṃkāvakāśini
nastu yāvati yādṛśi sāmānye pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāro na tatra śaṃkā,
cana vyāpāra iti nāsī kacana svayamicchayā vyāptimupanayatyapanayati [vā] pramāṇenaiva
samarpaṇāditi na doṣaḥ |
nanu so'pi hetumātrakṛtaṃ vā kāryagrāmaṃ bruvan pratyakṣayogye'pi pratyakṣavyāpāropa-
lambha ki na paśyati ? paśyatyeva viparyaṃyabādhakādāgamācca tasya tadābhyupagamāt |
pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ tu śarīraviśeṣādhika eva cetasi sa pramāṇayati | icchāyāmapi
karādivyāpāroparame kāryābhāvāt taddvāreṇaiva kulālādivyapadeśaviṣayasya samudāyasya
pratyakṣatvavyavahārāt | na tviyaṃ gatiḥ prayatnasacivacittamātre | tadāpyanumānādanvayaḥ
pratyeṣyate | na ca pratyakṣasyaiva kaścidanurodhaḥ | upalambhānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatireka-
niścayaḥ kartavyaḥ | sa copalambhaḥ pratyakṣarūpo'numānarūpo veti nātra nirbandhaḥ |
atra cintyate | kiṃ tadeva śarīropādhikaṃ cittaṃ prayatnavañcittamātraśabdenābhi-
matam, utānyat ? tattve kimanumānena, pratyakṣasiddhau vivādābhāvāt | tena cānvaya-
vyatirekau siddhau kāryamātreṇa ca tadvyabhicāro vyaktaḥ | anyatve liṅgābhāvadoṣaḥ,290
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
bhāṣaṇāde: kāryastha śarīriṇaiva caritārthatvāt | na ca tenānumitenāpi vyāptiḥ svī-
kriyate, vyatirekāniścayāt pūrvavat | evaṃ tarhi bahiṣāpi dhūmasya vyāptinaṃ deśakālā-
vasthāniyatena, kiṃtu vahnimātreṇa | tacca dṛśyamānādanyenaiveti vikalpe vyabhicārādi-
doṣa: sādhāraṇa iti tādagviśeṣavirahiṇā sāmānyena vyāptirvaktavyā |
tathehāpīti cet ? evamapi jāṭharādigatenāpi rūpeṇa vyāptiprasaṅgo dhūmasya |
tasmānna sāmānyamityeva vyāptāvadhikriyate, nāpi viśeṣa ityeva pratikṣipyate, [43b ]
dhūmānumānasyaivocchedāt, abhimate śikhani pravṛttisandehāt | tato yadi na sveccheva
saṃgrahaparicchedasādhanī, tadā pramāṇavyāpāramanviṣya vyavasthāprakrame kiñcit sāmānyaṃ
svīkārapravṛttenāpi pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣiptamarthādeṣitavyam, yadviśeṣātikrameṇa nāsyāvatāraḥ |
yathā jvaladbhāsurākāra pātikrame dhūmavyāptigrāhiṇa: | kiñcittu pratyakṣasvīkṛtam
apyanupalabdhi: pratikṣipati, pīṭharādivat sāmarthyāt |
sā hi dahanābhāve kāryābhimatābhāvaṃ sādhayantī dahanabhāvaprayuktatadbhāvavibhā-
vanādayogavyavacchedena tatkāryaṃtā sādhanapravṛttāpyanyasya hetutāṃ sādhayatyeva, yadabhāve
svayaṃ na vartate | anupalambhapūrvake tu pratyakṣa prāgbhāvādibādhana pravṛttayānupalabdhyānekavastu-
rūpasattvābhāve'bhāvasiddhau yadekavastusvabhāvasannidhau sannidhiradhyakṣeṇa pratīyate prāgapi
tadabhāvaprayuktābhāvavibhāvanāt taddhetubhāvasādhane yadapravṛttiyogyatayā pratikṣiptam
adhyakṣeṇa tatpratikṣiptameva |
tato na jāṭharāderanvayaḥ | nāpi kāladeśa[daśā] bhedabhinna svabhāvapratikṣepaḥ,
sarva pratyakṣa svajanmayogyatayā svīkārāt | nāpyanupalabdhyā, sā hyatādṛvasvabhāvā-
bhāve'bhavantī tadvijātīyahetutāṃ pratikṣipatīti yuktam, na tu tasyaiva, anyathā tadā-
śrayaṇaveyarthyāt | nanu deśādibhinnasvabhāvābhāve'vyayaṃ dhūmo dṛṣṭaḥ, na deśādibhinnasyā-
pyekākāra
pratyavamaśaṃpratyayena paridṛśyamānarūpeṇa sahakīkaraṇāt darśanāyogyasvabhāvād
anyatra | ataeva vahnimātraśabdābhidheyaṃ tadeva paridṛśyamānayogyādbhedākṛṣṭāvapyabhedāva-
bhāsāt |
nanu deśādiviprakṛṣṭamapyadarśanayogyameva | satyaṃ, kevalaṃ kadācit kacit | sva-
bhāvaviprakṛṣṭaṃ tu satyatyanta vijātīyatayā svīkāraparihārayorbhedena vṛttinaṃ virudhyate |
tato yathānumānavādinā sāmānyamanusaraṇīyamavyāptimasaṃbhavaṃ vā parihartu tathā
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
dṛśyaviśeṣāpekṣayātiriktasāmānyamapi parihartavyamativyāptiparihārāya evaṃ sati yathā
darśanāyogyavahvisāmānyaparihāreṇa tadyogyāvāntarasāmānyena vyāptirekatvavyavasthā ca
yuktā, na prayatnavanmātreṇa, pratyakṣa pratikṣiptatvāditi |
tatra vyāmohāt pramāṇāntareṇānvayamicchan tattvānyatvābhyāṃ paryaṃnuyujyate |
dahane tu tatpakṣeṇaiva samādhirityuktam | tasmāt pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptijighṛkṣāyāṃ
[44a] tadyogyasāmānyāpekṣāyā ghaṭaviṭapādau dṛṣṭānta iṣṭasya siddhirasiddhiśceti sādhāraṇā-
naikrāntikatvaṃ kāryasya | caitanyamātreṇa tu tadayogyenānvayavyatirekayorekasyāpyaniścayāt
'sandigdhānvayavyatirekatvaṃ vaktuṃ yuktamuktam,
saṃśayo'thaveti |
siddhaya siddhayoriti prakaraṇāt | tābhyāṃ bhāvābhāvāvuktau | yathāha - upalabdhireva
sattā anupalabdhirasatteti | tataḥ kāryatvādisādhanavati dharmiṇi dṛṣṭānte sādhyatveneṣṭasya
prayatnavanmātreṇa sasvāsattvasandehāt, tadadhiṣṭhānānadhiṣṭhānābhyāṃ ca sarvasaṃgrahādekatānvaya-
vyatirekānupapatteryuktamasādhāraṇānakāntikatvam |
nanu tathāpyanekānto'pyastu anvayamātraṃ kimiti pratikṣipyate, kāryotpattī
buddhereva vyāpāradarśanāt ? jāṭharasādhāraṇenāpi rūpeṇa tarhi dhūme'nvayaprasaṅgaḥ, dahana-
vyāpāradarśanāt | tataśca tadapekṣo vyatireko'pi syāditi prācīnadoṣaḥ | pratyakṣapratikṣepastu
sādhāraṇaḥ |
nanu jāṭharādyabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvānna prācīnadoṣaḥ, satyapyanvaya iti cet ? kailāsa-
karaṇakauśala vikalenāpi kalasasya karaṇaṃ kiṃ na kīrtyate ? atha karaṇakauśalasāmānye -
nānvayo'tra ? tatrāpi dāhakamātreṇeti na vyaktayupakṣepeṇa kiñcit | jātyapekṣayā tu
tadānyadāpīti kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvaḥ ? atha dāhakatvamātraṃ paridṛṣṭaviśeṣād bhinnāṃ
jātimāsthāya vyabhicāra ucyate, tadā tadapekṣayānvayo'pi kutaḥ, pratyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭāyā
eva jāte radhigamāt ? anvaye vā punavrvyābhicārānupapatteriti |
yatpunaḥ sajātīyena pratyakṣataḥ pratibandhaniścayamāśaṃkya, na hi sarvatra samāna-
jātiranumīyate, pratyakṣaśca yasmādasamānajātiḥ apratyakṣadha rūpādivyaktibhiranumīyate
cakṣurādigrāmaḥ, tathā candramasaḥ pṛthivyāśca parabhāgādhobhāgāvityuktam tadapi
pāpīyaḥ | tathāhi na tāvad vyāptiśūnyamanumānam, vyāptiśca sāmānyena sāmānyasya
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvaloṃ
bhavantī kathamasamānānumānamanusaheta ? tathā ca sā dvidhaiva pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ viparyaya
bādhakād vā | ubhayathāpi dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭasajātīyasyaivānumānam | anyathānyajātīyena dharmeṇa
vyāptimupādāyānyajātīyamanuminotīti mahatī prekṣā |
sāmānyato dṛṣṭānumāne'pi hi yadeva gatisāmānyamanyasthāna prāpti nibandhanamupalabdham,
tadevādhikaraṇāntare niścīyata iti kathaṃ vijātīyadharmānumānam ? athādhārabhedāpekṣayā
sāmarthyasādhyamavāntarabhedamabhipretyocyate tadanuktasamam | na hi kaścit anumānavādo
tanmātreṇa viśeṣamanicchan [44b] phalinamanumānaṃ samarthayitumīśaḥ | yadi ceśvarānumāne'pi
tādṛśo vyāptiḥ syāt, tanmātra viśeṣa siddhayā ceṣṭasiddhiḥ syāt, kastatra matsaramācaret ?
na ca tanmātraviśeṣāpekṣayā na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyata iti vaktuṃ yuktam,
kacidasamānajātyanumāne'pi tathocyate, tanmātraviśeṣaśca sarvatrānumāne'sti | viśeṣato
dṛṣṭasya sāmānye'pi tadeva niścīyata iti tadapekṣayā na sarvatra tadevānumīyata iti vaktavyam,
bhedādhiṣṭhānatvāt samānajāticintāyāḥ |
tat punaraprakṛtameva | sa tu na sarva: pratyakṣo'numīyata iti | yadi prakṛtamagnivat
pratibandhagra he pramāṇamadhikṛtyocyate, tadā pratyakṣasyaiva sarvatrānumānam anyatrāpadiṣṭapramāṇa-
pravṛtteḥ | atha viparyayabādhakāpekṣayā, tadā na vaktavyaṃ na kaścidviśeṣo'gnisādhanāt
īśvarānumānasyeti | anityasādhanāditi tu vaktumucitam | atha kāryahetutāmātreṇaivam
ucyate, tadā kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pratyakṣānupalambhasādhana eveti sa eva doṣaḥ | na ca
viparyayabādhakaṃ kiñcidastīti carcitameva | deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgaśca hetumātrāpatti sādhaya-
tyapi | tasmāt prakṛtaprameyānavagāhanāt lavata etat na sarvaḥ pratyakṣo'numīyata iti |
anumānakālāpekṣayā tu sarva: parokṣa evānumoyate, na ca tatra kācid vimatiḥ
ityanuktasamam | indriyaṃ tu na sākṣād buddheranumātuṃ śakyam, pratibandhāgrahaṇāt | buddhikāryaṃ
tu keṣucit satsvabhāvābhāvavattatirikta kāraṇasāpekṣatāmāvahatīti tādṛśīndriyaghoṣaṇā |
tatrārādiṣu dṛṣṭajātīyameva sāpekṣatvaṃ [yathā] sādhyate tathā parabhāgādhobhāgāvapi
ghaṭādikāryeṣu | avagaikasāmagrī pratibaddhau sāmānyato dṛṣṭāvevānumoyete iti sādhyaśūnya-
mudāharaṇamapi ityalaṃ bahunā | athavā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpyate, kāraṇa -
viśeṣeṇa tu kāryaviśeṣa eveti nyāyaḥ | adhyavasāyamātrato vā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryaviśeṣa
iti pravādaḥ | tatrāyaṃ kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpta mitibruvāṇaḥ
pramāṇāvaṣṭambhena nāma prasiddhimullaṅghayet |
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam
tacca pramāṇaṃ vyāptisādhakaṃ dvividhameva pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ vā, viparyayabādhakaṃ vā,
anayoḥ pratyakṣānumānasvabhāvatvāt anyato niścayāyogāt | tatra tāvaduktakrameṇa
kāryasāmānyasya,
no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśād vyāptiḥ samastasya ca
pratyakṣānupalambhato na tadatajjātīyabhedaspṛśaḥ |
prāgbhāvādiniṣedhapūrvakatayā dhūmādivajjanmadhī-
ranvetīdṛśamīdṛśāditi yataḥ sāmānyabhedadvayam ||
idamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhamasyopalambha upalabhyata ityevaṃ [45a ] hi
pratyakṣānupalambhayorvyāptigrahaṇakramaḥ | tatredamityekajātīyatayā eka pratyavamarśapratibhāsi
dhūmādikamanekakāryajātyantaravyudāsenānekakāraṇajātyantaravyudāsena cāsyeti vahnayādeḥ
ityarthaḥ | tataḥ kāryakāraṇayoḥ pratyekaṃ tajjātīyetarayoritaretarato bhede parāmarśapūrvikā
pravṛttiḥ, anyathā sāmathvaiyarthyābhyāmanupayogāt |
tathā hyakāryarāśivyavacchedena vā kāryāntaravyavacchedena vā idametad bhāvā-
bhāvānuvidhāyītyavadhāryeta ? ādye pakṣe etāni vastuni etanniyatāni ityayamartho
netadvastviti, ekākāravirahādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteḥ | nanu kāryatvādinā sāmānyena
idamiti kāryaṃ sanniveśo vetyādi vaktuṃ śakteḥ, asiddhametaditi cet ? ucyate, ih
bhāvābhāvavidhānabuddhidvidhā saṃbhavati, dharmiviṣayā dharmaviṣayā ca, kāryasya nirva-

sādhanasādhu, vyabhicārālambanaṃ tu durbalamiti kimatra prāptam ?
guṇe'pi dravyavat tasmāt sajātīyaparigrahaḥ |

iti kiṃkṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet ? upādhikṛtaḥ | kina bhinnadharmiṇordharmayorapīti
cet - na, vaiṣamyāt | acetanopādānaṃ dhūmasthānīyaṃ kāryahetvabhimānāt na ca kaścittasya
dharmibhedādbhedamāha - yadā tvacetanopādānatvādacalādī cetanāpekṣatvaṃ vivakṣitam tadā
dhūmatvena dhūmo vahnimānityevaṃprāyā sthitiḥ | evaṃ ca sati dhūmadvaye dhūmatvayorbhedaḥ
prasañjanīya iti kathaṃ sāmyam ? evamevāstviti cet na, bhidyamāno hyupādhirupādhi
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānam
mantamapi bhindyāt | bhedaścaikapratyavamarśabahirbhāvalakṣaṇo na dhūmamupādhi spṛśati yena
svagataṃ bhinattu, yathā kumbhāmbhodharādiracetanatvopādānatvamityacodyametat |
nanu na dṛṣṭastāvaddharmibhedena dharmabheda iti cet ? yadrūpapuraskāreṇa pratibandha-
sādhaka pramāṇavṛttistasyābhede bhidyamānāpi dharmijātirabhinnavadābhāsamānā na bādhikā |
tadbhede tu tadgataṃ dharmāntaramabhidyamā[51a]namapi bhinnavadābhāsamānaṃ na sādhaka miti
nyāyaḥ | anyathā jaladharāthināpi kumbhakārasya paryeṣaṇāprasaṅgaḥ | tadapāyespi vihāyasi
balāhakodayadarśanānneti cet – na, tatprabhavasyaiva ghaṭasyeva tasya maruto kṣepaḥ kiṃ na
saṃbhāvyate ? atha ca vāridhāritvamātramubhayatra dṛṣṭamiti yathā tatra saṃjñābhedamātrabhedo
vyavasthāpyate, tathātrāpīti yuktam | pratibandhaniścayo hi pramāṇaviṣayasvabhāvaniyame sati
bhavati, tadviruddhāniyamarūpaṃ ca sādhāraṇatvam |
pramāṇapratibaddho hi niścayastadviṣayasvarūpollaṅghe'pi bhavan pramāṇāpramāṇasādhyaḥ
syāt | na caivam tasmānnānekāntaḥ | nāpyasiddhiradhyakṣavyāpārānusārāt | tadiha
pāṇḍutvasyāgnivyabhicāro dṛṣṭa iti dṛṣṭāntasya sādhyaśūnyatāniṣedha eṣaḥ | ata eva
nānumāna miti pratibandhābhāvādaniścayaphalamidamubhayatra | na tu siddhavyāptikayordahana-
pāṇḍutayorvyābhicāreṇa sādhanavaidhuryam, vyāptisiddhāvanumānāpavādasyāśakyasādhana-
tvāt vyabhicārasyaivāyogāt | sarvopasaṃhāravatī hi vyāptiḥ, tadbhāve tadbhāvaḥ kathaṃ
syāt ?
tato'yamarthaḥ | yathā pāṇḍutvānnāgnimattve'numānaṃ tasya tatrāpratibandhāt | sa
ca vyabhicāreṇābhivyaktaḥ | anyathā tatrāpyanumānamaṅgīkṛtyaiva svasthamāsīt | sa ca
vyabhicāra: pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpetarasādhāraṇaṃ dharmaṃ sarvamapratibaddhatve niyatamādarśayatīti
yathoktasādhāraṇatvākṛṣṭādapratibandhāt | tathaiva yathā kāryatvādimātrādapi na cetanādhiṣṭhānānu-
mānamiti | ato vyabhicāradarśanamupakārakameva parasya | tasmāt pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpa-
parāmarśāt tathāvidhopādhikameva kāryatvādisādhanaṃ dhiya iti siddham | tathāvidhasya ca
vāstava eva pratyāsattibheda iti saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇamāpatitam |
tena dharmijātibhedasya dharmabhedakatvaṃ siddhamapīti kathaṃ sarvatra tanniṣedha: ? atha
sarvatraiva yadbhedakatvaṃ tanniṣidhyate kacidabhedakatvamapītyartha:, tadā siddhasādhanam | uktaṃ
hi pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpāpekṣayā tadubhayavyavasthānamiti | tathā ca sati bhedasthitireva,jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
kṛtakatvādisparśaṃścāparibhāvakatayā kriyate | na hi tatrāpi pratyakṣabalād vyāptirupapādayituṃ
śakyā, kiṃ tu viparyayabādhakānumānāt, tadabhāve'nanumānasyeṣṭatvāt |
tato'bhūtvābhavanābhidhānadharmamātrasya bhūtvābhavanena dharmeṇa vyāptisādhakaṃ dharmiṇo
yadi jātibhedamudāsayati dhūmasyāgninā vyāptisā[51b]dhakameva mahānasādi, tadā prastute
kimāyātam yatra pratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā jātibhedaniṣṭheva vyāptigṛhītirītiriti ? yadi tu
prakṛte'pi kāryavastustomagatāḥ kāryatvādaya eva dharmāḥ pratītavyāptayaḥ syuḥ, tadāyaṃ na
doṣaḥ | kevalamupāyaprakāradvayasyāpyayogādayukteva vyāptiriti darśitam | tatra viparyaya -
bādhakapramāṇaparicayasteṣāmasaṃbhavo, bauddhagandhereva kasyacit tathā yatnadarśanāt | na ca
prakṛte vaktuṃ śakya iti tatrāsthāmavadhūya | pradeśāntare ca,
nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vetyādinā
[pra. vā. 3. 34]
karaṇamātre viśeṣatyāgena kāryamātra pratibandhaṃ viparyayabādhakabalena sūcayato nirvṛti vidadhāno
bhagavān vārtikakāraḥ parasya darśanādarśanamātreṇa vyāptivādinaḥ tadyogapratipādane pratyāsa
pratyakṣānupalambhabalāvalambanamavalokayan tadāhṛtya dūṣayituṃ jātibhedakṛtaṃ dūṣaṇamudbhāvayatīti
veditavyam | tasmāt pratyakṣavyāpārāvadheyajātibhedasyātyantaṃ vyaktatvāt saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇī-
kriyamāṇamapyakiñcitkaramityuktam ||
athavā, astu ghaṭādyapekṣayā kṣoṇīdharādīnāṃ jātibhedo yataḥ, -
siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi
ucyeta | krīḍāparvatādayastu pauruṣeyāstadekajātibhavāḥ, taiḥ sahaikahetavaḥ kiṃ na
bhavanti ? tato'yamarthaḥ, yo yaḥ śailaḥ sa sarva: pauruṣeyo yathā krīḍāśaila: śailaśca kailāsa
iti | evaṃ kulyāmahāsarovaraprabhṛtayo nadīsamudrādīnāmudāharaṇānyūnīyānī tyā-
śāha,
ayamarthaḥ,
vastubhede prasiddhasyetyādi,
krīḍāparyaṃta kādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumā-
nāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam |
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam
ki cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyantyamī cennagāḥ
kā vārteśvarasādhanasya kimihopāttaṃ samāptaṃ ca kim ||
jātibhede siddhe'dhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyānusāra: pūrayedapi pratyāśām, abhede tu tadapi
nirāspadam | na hi sajātīyakumbhāntare tadvijātīyasya nirmātuḥ siddhirityanubhavāt
abhyupagamād vā bhinnaiva jātiranayorna samānaṃ hetumāvahati saṃjñāmātrasāmye'pīti |
kaḥ punarayaṃ niyamo ya ukta prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigraho nānyathetyāśaṅkayāha,
anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit |
ghaṭāde: karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ ||
[pra. vā. 1. 15]
iti | na hi sudūramanusaratāpi sa kaścitpratibandhasādhana vidhilaṃbdhavyo yaḥ kumbhakāreṇa
mṛnmayamātravyāptiprasaṅgaparihārakārī prayatnavatā kāryamātravyāpti sādhayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ |
kumbhakāreṇa hi kāryamātra vyāptisādhanāya prabhavatastadviśeṣa mṛnmayasya sāṃdhane kaḥ śakti-
vyāghātaḥ ? astu vā prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigrahaḥ | yattūktam,
no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśādityādi
tato'nyathā bhaviṣyatīti āśaṅkaya jaladharārthinā kumbhakāraparyeṣaṇāprasaṅgamuktameva
prakārāntareṇa] [52a ] saṃbhāvayantāha,
anyathetyādi |
yadā hi bādhātmakoddeśenāpi pravartamāna : sāmānyenaiva vyāpti sādhayati tadā
kuto mṛnmayāt kulālānumānaṃ kuryāt kāraṇamātrasya siddhe: ? yadāpi pratyakṣāpekṣayā
hetuviśeṣeṇa kulālena karaṇavyāpāropadheyaviśeṣasya kumbhādikāryaviśeṣasya vyāptistadāpi
kutastatprasaṅgaḥ ? yadāpyadhyavasāyamātrāpekṣayā sāmānyena viśeṣasya tadāpyayaṃ dūrataraḥ |
evaṃ tu vyavasthāto'nyathāvyāptigrahaṇe viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya bhavatīti kathaṃ mṛnmayāt
kulālānumānamaprasaṅga ? tatkāryakumbhādyapekṣayā atyantavisadṛśādapi prasaṅge kathaṃ
kiyatāpyaṃśena pratyāsannāt na syāt ? tathā caivaṃ sajātīyādapyavāntarabhedānusāri-
pratyakṣavyavasāyāpekṣayā nānumānaṃ pratibandhāniścayāttadā kaiva vārtā vijātīyād ?
atyantavijātīye dṛṣṭavyāptikasyeti daṇḍāpūpanyāya eṣa iti darśayituṃ mṛnmayagrahaṇam |ZA PRVNAREA PO
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
nanūbhayathā vyākhyāne'pi vyabhicārādeva nānumānaṃ, tatkathamatiprasaṅga iti
cet ? uktakrameṇopakāraka eva vyabhicāro'smākaṃ na bādhakaḥ | tathāhi pramādvayavyā-
pārātikrame'nantaraprakārabahirbhāva vā pratijñāta pratibandhaniścayābhāvasādhaka eva
vyabhicāra iti | api ca, vyabhicāro nāma sāmānyena gṛhītāyā vyāpteniyataviṣayā-
pekṣayā vighātamātanoti, atha vyāptigrahaṇameva tanna bhavatīti vibhāvayati, atha
satyapi vyāptiprasa re'numānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati, ataevābādhita viṣayatvamapi liṅgalakṣaṇam
ākhyātamiti pakṣāḥ |
tatra prathamapakṣe sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ, anyatrāpi tadvalādeva sādhyapratyāśā, sā ca
niścitāpi khaṇḍitā kaciditi anyatrāpi śaṅkānivṛtteḥ, tata eva tadgrahaṇavaiyarthyāt |
dvitoye tu na viśeṣaścetane | yathā hi kumbhakāreṇa kāryasāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa
vyāptirgṛhītā vyabhicāreṇa durgṛhītā vyavasthāpyate tathā cetanyamātreṇāpi, tatrāpi
pratyakṣavyāpāre viśeṣābhāvāt |
tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyāmeva vyabhicāreṇānumānamapāsyata iti mahīyasīyam ayoga-
paramparā | kevalamatra pakṣe etadāpatitaṃ yadīdamatra sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ vyabhicarya na sthitaṃ tadā
sādhyaṃ sādhayatīti | etacca sādhyavidhuraṃ sarvārthasākṣātkāriṇo nānyaḥ kartuṃ śaktaḥ | sa hi
ya eva dharmī tathāvidhamadhyamadhiśayito na bhavati tameva vā vyabhicāragocaratayā anumāna-
bhājanīkaroti, sarvavipakṣānīkṣaṇe tu tanmadhya eva kadācideṣo'pi sthāditi śaṅkā'nivṛtteḥ |
tasmādukta eva nyāya āśrayaṇayogyo vyabhicāraśca vyāptidurgrahaṇameva sādhayatīti kārya-
mātravyāptiḥ prakṛtakā raga viśeṣeṇāsaṃbhavinyeva sādhuriti |
gṛhītāyāṃ vyāptau yadi vihatirāśvāsaviraho
graho nāsau vyāpte[52b] yadi ca na viśeṣo matimati |
abādhāpekṣāyāṃ na sakalavipakṣekṣaṇamṛte
nirātaṅkastasmāna khalu phalamātre grahavidhiḥ |
iti saṃgrahaḥ |
ki cādāya samastavastuviṣayāṃ vyāpti punaścenmatā
tattajjātiṣu bādhakakramavaśātsvavyāpya[tattat] sthitiḥ |
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokī vyākhyānam
tattajjātiṣu sādhakakramavaśādunnīyate kiṃ na sā
yenāyāsakaśaktisaṃśayapadaṃ santo viśantīdṛśam ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
aparigaṇito nāma vastuvyāpāraviṣayo'parigaṇitatamastvaviṣayaḥ | tatra ka
evamanātmīyakāryajātinikarasya pratyekaṃ vyabhicārān dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā svakāryaṃjātiṣveva
niyantuṃ hetumapāravyāpāra: pārayate ? tathā ca sati yasyaiva sākṣādanīkṣito vyabhicāraḥ
tadeva tasya gamakamāśaktam | tadā śaṅkāsaṃbhavānneti cet – na, kacidatīndriye tarhi
niścayamayaṃ kuryāt | yajjātīyoddeśena pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ sāmānya viṣayamavasthā[pi]taṃ tatra
kaḥ sandeha iti cet ? evaṃ tarhi parāparatadīyavyāpyajātiṣu tathaiva saṃśayapravṛttipratyanīka-
pramāṇavṛttyanusaraṇe āyātastṛtīyapādāpatito'rthaḥ | tasmānna kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā
kāryamātrasya vyāptiḥ pratyetuṃ śakyeti,
siddha yādṛgityādi
siddhāntaḥ |
athavā yaduktaṃ na śarīranirapekṣaprayatnavanmātreṇa kāryasya vyāptiḥ pratipattuṃ pāryate,
pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣepāt tādṛśasyetyādi, tadevopasaṃharati, -
siddhamiti
yāvṛkṣo'sau śarīrādiyogī adhiṣṭhātā ceti | śeṣaṃ subodham | tādṛśaśca pratyakṣabādhādi-
doṣaviṣaya ityākūtam | nanu śarīravatyapi cetanatvaṃ dṛṣṭamitaratrāpi saṃbhavati iti yathā
śarīriṇā vyāptaṃ kāryādi sidhyati, tathābhimatenāpi ityatrāpi prāguktanyāyāt saṃjñā-
mātrādavaśiṣyamānāt sādhanamanorathamunmathnannāha vastubhede kumbhādau prasiddhasya
kulālāderyo vācakaḥ śabdaśca tana iti tanmātrādabhidyamānasyābhimatasya pramāṇavyāpārā-
pekṣayā dūrīkṛtasya na yuktānumitiriti vyāptābhimatād vastuna iti prakṛtamarthāpanaṃ vā
kathamivetyāha,
pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśana iti |
ayamabhiprāyaḥ, yadi śabdamātrasāmyenābhidyamānasyānumānaṃ śabdasāmyenābhidya-
mānādapi pāṇḍumna: kiṃ na dhūmadhvajasyānumānam ? atha tatra viśiṣṭa kāryasvabhāvāpekṣamjñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
adhyakṣamanyavyāpti pratikṣipatīti nānumānamucyate, tathā cetanamātrapratikṣepeṇāpi
pratyakṣaṃ ki na tadanumānaṃ nirasyati ? etena yadā daśyamapi kāryāntaraṃ tiraskaroti
pratyakṣaṃ tadā keva kathā dṛkpathātiriktasya cetanamātrasyeti ? astu tāvad vyāpyā-
pekṣayā vibhāga eva, loke tathaiva pratīteḥ, anyathātiprasaṅgācca |
vyāpakāpekṣayā tu yadyeṣa niyamo na syāt ko doṣa ityāśaṅkhyā pūrvoktameveti
prasaṅgaṃ bhaṅgayantareṇa taruṇayati, anyathetyādi | valmīkasyeti valmīkajantorityarthaḥ |
tatkṛtiriti ghaṭādikṛtiḥ | [53a] ayamarthaḥ, yadi viśeṣeṇāpi vyāptimavasāya cetana-
mātraṃ sāmānyamanumātavyam, tadā kumbhādikaraṇasya kulāle niyatasya cetanamātra paryaṃ-
vasitatvāt ghaṭāderapi valmīkajantuḥ kartānumeya: syāt, yathāhi kumbhādeḥ kumbhakāreṇa
vyāptigrahaṇe caitanyamātreṇāviśeṣāt tasyāpyanumānamevaṃ valmīkaukaso'pi caitanyenānyā-
viśeṣāt kiṃ nānumānam ? yadā ca śarīriṇā vyāptigrahe śarīriṇo'pyanyasya pratikṣepaḥ,
tadā kā vārtātyanta visadṛśasyeti | na cātra bahutvenopayogaḥ, ekātmano'pi cetanyād
iti valmīkasyeti nirdeśaḥ | etena dhūmāderapi jāṭharāderanumānākṣepo vyaktaḥ | vyabhi-
cāracarcāyāṃ ca pūrvavat sarvamāvartanīyamiti ||
yaduktaṃ, prayatnavatā yadvaghāptaṃ sanniveśādi tanna siddhaṃ sindhubhūdharādau, yacca siddhaṃ
tantra vyāpta miti tatrai tatsyāt, nanu jātyuttaramidaṃ dharmabhedavikalpanāt, tato yathā
yatkṛtakaṃ tadanityaṃ ghaṭavaditi kṛte kaścidāha, yadi ghaṭagataṃ kṛtakatvaṃ hetustadasiddha śabde,
śabdagataṃ tvanitya saṃghāte ghaṭapaṭādāvabhāvādviruddham | atha sapakṣavad vipakṣetrapi nāstīti
matiḥ, tadā asādhāraṇamanaikāntikamiti | na ca tāvatā kṛtakatvaṃ tattvato'śaktameva
anityatvasādhane, tathedamapi | tathāhi yacca siddhaṃ tanna vyāptamityanena sapakṣāvṛttevirodhaḥ,
vipakṣādapi nivṛttipakṣe vā asādhāraṇatvamākṛṣṭamiti | atha prakṛtakāryānurodhād
adūṣaṇamevedamudghoṣyate ? tathā sati kṛtakatvāderapi asādhanatvaprasaṅgaḥ sūtrakāra
virodhaśca, kāryasamasaṃjñayā asya dūṣaṇasya tena pratijñānāt | yadāha,
kāryatvānyatvaleśena yatsādhyāsiddhicodanam |
tatkāryasamametattu tridhā vaktrabhisandhitaḥ ||
katiratyanteti mātṛkāsthaḥ pāṭhaḥ |
īśvaravādādhikāre vārtika saptaślokī vyākhyānam
iti upacāramātrakṛttvenānyatvasya leśa uktaḥ, vaktrabhiprāyeṇa traividhyaṃ ca darśita -
miti |
tadetadubhayamapyasāram, prathamapakṣasya tāvat pūrvameva pratikṣepāt | uktaṃ hi
vyāptisādhakapramāṇapuraskṛtasvarūpasyābhede bhidyamānā api saṃbandhino vidhūtabhedā
iva bhāsamānā na bādhakāḥ | tasya tu bhede abhedino'pi bhinnavadābhāsamānāḥ kārya-
tvādayo dharmā na tadvayāpakasya sādhakā iti | vyāptigrahaṇaprakramaśca dvividho darśitaḥ |
tatra yadi nāśena kṛtakatvasyeva viparyabādhakabalād buddhimatāpi kāryatvāderavinā-
bhāvagraha: syāt, tadā abhūtvā bhavanamātramiva sanniveśādimātramadhikṛtya pravṛttaṃ
pramāṇamiti kastatra dharmabhedena bhindānaḥ sādhanaṃ śobheteti yujyate jātyuttara miti |
yadi tu pratyakṣānupalambhavaśāt sanniveśādikamiva kṛtakatvamapi vyāptamava-
tadā śabde'pi sādhanatvaṃ kṛtakatvāde: kena nivāryeta, jātiviśeṣollekhenaiva
pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpārasya pari[53b] niṣṭhitatvāt ? anyathā dhūmagatā api kārya-
tvādayo jātiviśeṣānavacchedena dahanāvinābhāvinaḥ sidhyanto nāśakyaparihāramati-
prasaṅgamanupanīya svāsthyamāsādayeyuḥ | kāryāntarasya vyabhicāropakṣepo'pi kṣodiṣṭhaḥ
pratividhiḥ | tadā hi yatraiva sākṣād vyabhicārānupalambhaḥ tadeva sādhanaṃ jātamiti
kiyallāghavaṃ doṣabhārasya ?

yad yad bhāvyate tat tad bhāvanāprakarṣaparyante sphuṭābhaṃ saṃbhavati | yathā
kāmukasya kāminyākāraḥ | bhāvyante ca paramapuruṣārthinā kṣaṇikatve nairātmyādayo
vastudharmā iti | atredaṃ cintyate bhavatu bhāvanayā mānasī sphuṭābhatā, kevalaṃ bhūtābhūtārtha-
sādhāraṇatvād bhāvanodbhūta vai [56b] śadyasyāpi saṃvādaniyamānupapatteḥ kutaḥ prāmāṇya miti
kathaṃ pratyakṣatā yogijñānasyeti ?
athānumānavyavasthāpitavastubhāvanāyāstadvayabhicāraśaṅkāvirahāt tajjasyāpi

vidyuhanādikaṃ gṛhītvā bhāvanāprakarṣa paryantajātaṃ sthirataratadākāraṃ ca jñānaṃ bhaved yāvanna
viparītabhāvanābhiyogaparyaṃntaḥ | astaṃ gataśca tadviṣaya iti kathaṃ pramāṇopanītavastu-
gocaratve'pi saṃvādāśvāsaḥ ? anastaṅgame'pi vā tāvatkālamanalasya nāvasthāniyamaḥ |
samudrāderapyevam | mahīruhādīnāṃ cālpālpakālena vaisadṛśyaṃ dṛśyate | mahīdharādīnāṃ ca
dahanāśaniprabhṛtibhiḥ | bhāvanā tu yāmavasthāmabhiniviśya bhavati tadekāvasthāniyataḥ
sphuṭobhāva iti tadviṣayāpekṣayā bhrāntirākārabhedāditi na prāmāṇyaṃ na ca pratyakṣatā |
yadā ca hālika eva havyāśanamanumāya bhāvanayā sphuṭayet, tadā na tad yogijñānaṃ paramārtha -
viṣayatvābhāvāditi pratyakṣāntaraprasaṅgaḥ |

yat punarastaṃ gate'pi vastunyākārāntarabhāji vā sthirākāratayā bhāvanā,
yasya nirālambanatvamāpāditaṃ sarvasya tadapi vastubhāvanāpakṣe śobhate na vastudharmaṃ
bhāvanāpakṣe | vastudharmāṃśca kṣaṇikatvādayaḥ saṃsāraverāgyāt sphuṭībhāvabhājo bhāvayitu
mupakrāntāḥ | athaikatra pramāṇapariśuddhe'pi bhāvanājanitaveśadyasya vastuni visaṃvāda-
saṃdarśanādanyatrāpi ka āśvāsaḥ, pramāṇapariśuddhimantareṇāśvāsa he torapyasyābhāvāt,
tasyāśca saṃvādaniyatāvasāmarthyāt ? tanna, sthirāsthiraviṣayatvena viśeṣāt | asthiraṃ
hi vastu pradhvaṃsavikārābhyāṃ grasthata iti na saṃvādaḥ, [57a] vastudharmāstu

eva |
nanvetadapi na yuktam | na hi kṣaṇikatvādikaṃ nāma kiñcidasti vastu, satve vā

bhavanmate'pi kṣaṇikatvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikā eva bhāvarāśayo'parāmṛṣṭabhedāḥ bhedāntaratiraskāre-
ṇocyante | tathā ca sati kṣaṇikatvabhāvanetyapi kṣaṇikapadārthasārthabhāvanetyevārthaḥ | tāvatā
tānyeva vastūni bhāvyamānāni sphuṭībhavantīti sa eva doṣaḥ | athābhinnānyapi kṣaṇikatvā-
doni bhinnānīva tāvatpratibhānti ? tathāpyadhyavasāyād vastugatānyeva bhāvyanta iti na

mevākāro bhāvanāyāḥ |
tatkathaṃ vastutattvabhāvanāpakṣe'pi vastusaṃsparśaparihāra: ? parihāre cāvastvantara-
bhāvanaiva syānna dharmabhāvanā | satyam | yadyapi vastutattvabhāvanathāpi sāmānyenākṣiptaṃ vastu,
tathāpi na tasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ tattvamātratātparya paryavasānāt | tattvabhāvanaiva hi sphuṭībhavantī
saṃsārāpasāraṇasaraṇiḥ | na hi kāminīkalevaraṃ sākṣātkṛtaṃ rāgasaṃkocamācarati, kiṃ

nanu tatra tātparye'pi vastudharma: sphuṭībhavati na vastviti kā saṅgatiḥ, bhāvanayā dvayorapi

yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam
naiṣa doṣaḥ, dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭībhāvamaspṛśato'pi dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvadarśanāt |
kevalaṃ vastupratyāsatyanapekṣya na sphuṭasphuraṇamiti syāt | sphuṭībhāvo'pi tasya tadviṣaya-
sannidhau yatnamanapekṣya jhagiti tajjñāne tattadākārasphuraṇaṃ nāma, vastuprattyāsatyapekṣā tu
na kṣīyate, dharmatvādeva, priyatvādivat | tathā hi nimbarasādau tāvat priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ
sphuṭībhavadṛṣṭam | naca nimbādeḥ sa dharma iti tadbhāvanayā nimbādyapi svajanmadeśasthaṃ
rasanāprasaṅgi vā sphuṭaṃ sphuradasti yāvanna viparyayabhāvanābhiyogaprakarṣaḥ | na ca sphuṭībhūtaṃ
priyatvamapi taṭasthamupalabhyate nimbādyanubhavamanapekṣya kiṃ tu yadā yadā nimbādyanubhava:
tadā tadā jhagiti priyatvamanubhavaviṣayaḥ, na prāgivodvejakamanubhayaṃ vetyeṣa eva dharma-
sphuṭībhāvārthaḥ |
yathā hi kāminyādivastuni sphuṭobhūte'pi na yathā samayasiddhastattvasphuṭībhāvaḥ,
tathā tattvabhāvanayāpi na vastusphuṭībhāva ubhayo: parasparāvyabhicāre'pīti kīdṛśo
doṣa: ? atha na bāhyadharma: priyatvamasādhāraṇatvād bhāvanādheyatvācceti cet ? kasya
punarayaṃ dharmo'stu priyatvādiḥ pratyātmavedyatvenāpahnotumaśakyaḥ ? jñānasya [57b] cet ?
bāhyasya priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ jñānasya sphuṭībhavatīti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ ? utkṛṣṭamidaṃ nimbā-
diti bhāvanākāro'pi na tajjñānamutkṛṣṭamiti | athāpi jñānasyaiva priyatayā sphuṭībhāve
na jātu kaścidapriyamanubhavet | na hi bahiriva jñānamapi kādācitkasannidhānam |
jñānasyāpi kasyacideva priyatvavyaktiriti cet ? kikṛtaḥ punarayaṃ vibhāga: ? yadyabhyāsa-
kṛtaḥ, yatraivābhyāso bāhye tatraiva bhavatu | tadanapekṣāyāṃ kasyacidapi pratyāsattiviprakarṣā-
bhāvānmanomātramadhiṣṭhānībhūtamiti na kaścidviśeṣaḥ |
bā tu viśiṣṭajātinimbādikamabhyāsaviṣayīkṛtamiti nātiprasaṅgaḥ | jñāna-
mapi tarhi bhāvitanimbagocarameva pratyāsannamiti viśeṣaḥ | evaṃ tarhīdamāyātam, yadvastu
kenacid rūpeṇa bhāvyate tadvastu vihāya tatpratyāsannasya sphuṭībhāva iti kāminīṃ bhāva-
yatastatpratyāsannasya pitrādereva sphuṭībhāvaprasaṅgo na kāminyāḥ | atha viṣayasya viṣa-
yiṇā jñānena saha viśiṣṭeva kācitpratyāsattiḥ ? evamapi nimbe priyatayā abhyasyamāne
tajjñānaṃ priyatayā sphuratīti nimbādikaṃ prāgvadapriyameva bhavet | tato yathā sarpādāva-
priye parihārāṅgatayā tanniścayaḥ priya eva na sarpādistathedamapīti kṛtaṃ bhāvanayā |
atha bhāvanābalāt priyākārameva tadviṣayaṃ jñānamupajāyata iti kalpanā ? evaṃ
sati nimbarasaḥ priyo bhāvyata iti tadviṣayajñānameva priyākāraṃ bhāvyata ityāpannam |326
jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalī
sphuṭābhatāpi tasya tadviṣayopanidhau tadgrāhijñānasya jhagiti yatnamanapekṣya priyākāra-
sphuraṇam, na viṣayasyaivāsannihitasya sākṣādbhāvaḥ | evaṃ kṣoṇīdharādayo'pi kṣaṇino
bhāvyanta iti tadviṣayajñānameva kṣaṇikākāraṃ bhāvyata iti | tasyāpi sphuṭībhāvo
bhūdharādisannidhau tadgrāhakasya kṣaṇikākārodayo na bhūdharāderasannihitasyāpi sphuṭī-
bhāvaḥ | iyameva dharmaṃbhāvanā śabdārthaniṣṭheti na prastutavastukṣatiḥ |
vastutastu priyatvaṃ nāma sukhakaratvam | tatra yadviṣaye yasya priyatvabhāvanā
taccittasantānaṃ bhāvanāpariṣkṛtamupādānamupādāya sa viṣaya: sahakārī sukhamutpādayatīti
sthitau na sarvaṃ priyatvam | tatra prīṇakatvaṃ tu tasyaiva dharmaḥ, sarvaṃ ca pratīti na doṣaḥ |
sa cābhyāsādeva | evaṃ kṛpādiṣvapi mānaseṣu dharmeṣu yojyam | duḥkhinamuddharāmīti
duḥkhiparoddharaṇabhāvanāyāḥ sphuṭībhāvastadviṣayasannidhau jhagiti tat jñānaṃ tadanurūpā-
nuṣṭhānaprasavahetuḥ | evaṃ śucikapālabhāvānāyāmapi naṃrghuṇyasphuṭībhāvo nāma karpūropa-
sarpaṇe veditavyaḥ | na tu saṃbandhinaiva pratyāsannanetareṇa vā sahasphu[58a] rattā |

ityāha |
