rūpasya viśeṣasyābhāvāt | prayojanāpekṣayā hi bahulamekaprakārasaṃgrāhyasthāpi prakārabheda-
nirdeśa iṣyata eva, yathā saṃprayuktasaṃskāraskandhasaṃgṛhītayorapi vedanāsaṃjñayoḥ, vikalpa-
saṃgṛhītasyāpi kliṣṭamanojñānasya | tasmānnendriyayogijñānayorabhedapakṣe tāvaddoṣaḥ | tadeva
dharmirūpāpekṣayendriyajñānaṃ dharmāpekṣayā yogijñānaṃ, yathā dharmipratyakṣameva niṣedhāpekṣayā
nupalabdhi: |
bhedakapakṣe'pi na tāvat sthairyetarasphuraṇakṛtopālambhasaṃbhava: indriyajñānenāpi
vastu sarvātmanā gṛhṇatā truṭyadrūpasyaiva grahaṇāt | adhyavasāyo'pi pūrvaṃ durlabhaḥ sa
saṃprati bhāvanābalāvalambinā manasā āsāditapāṭavena ghaṭita iti viśeṣaḥ |
nanvindriyasyāpi taddaśāyāṃ niratiśayaviśeṣalābhād dūrasūkṣmādyanubhava ko nivārayati
bāhyayogivat, tiraścāmapi kutaścit karmākṣepānmātrayā tathopalabdheḥ ? vidyamānānāṃ
ca kṣaṇānāmavaśyaṃ vaisadṛśyamaṇīyo'pi saṃbhavi, anyathā sarvātmanā sādṛśye tattva-
prasaṅgāt | tat tathāvidhasūkṣmabhedāvadhāraṇadhūryeṇākṣavijñānenaiva sādhyasiddheranarthakaṃ
yogijñānam |
etena duḥkhānātmādisākṣātkāro vyākhyātaḥ | puruṣavapuṣā cendriyamantareṇa
bhavitumaśakyamiti yogijñānamanutpādanīyamastu | tadapyayuktam | na hi saṃbhāvanā-
mātropanītaṃ netrabalamavalambya saṃvyavahāriṇā prekṣeṇa pramāṇaparāyaṇo mārga: parihatu
śakyaḥ | tadabhyāsasahakārikameva vā tathāvidhendriyaśaktisādhanamityaparihāryeṇa yogijñānena
samānakakṣatāyāmapi indriyajñānasya na kaścid doṣaḥ | vaiyarthya[59a] mekasyeti cet ?
katareṇa punaḥ svakāraṇopanidhānadharmaṇoranayoḥ svavyāpāravaiyarthyabhayānnivartitavyam,
bojādiṣvivāntyakṣaṇaprāpteṣu |
aprāmāṇyamekasyāstviti cet ? bījādiṣvapyekasyākāraṇatvamastu | sarveṣāṃ
samānasāmarthyānāṃ katamadekamakāraṇamavasthāpayituṃ śakyamiti cet ? paricchedabalavato-
jñānayorapi kimekamapramāṇīkriyatām | parasparāpekṣayā mā bhūdubhayamapi pramāṇamiti cet ?
bījādiṣvapi naikamapi kāraṇatvamastviti samānam | gṛhītagrāhitvaṃ nāma nāstyeva | tarhi
doṣa iti cet –na, kālabhedena tasya svīkārāt | gṛhītagrahaṇaṃ hi taducyate, na gṛhyamāṇastha,
yathā kṛtasya karaṇasvīkāre'kārakatvam, na tu kriyamāṇakaraṇe bījādivadeva | tasmādabhinna-
kālapakṣe naiṣa doṣaḥ |

iti ? tasmād dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt kimivāniṣṭaṃ kimiva vā na doṣa ityubhayorapi nāvasaraḥ |
samasamayatayā tarhīndriyajñānānapekṣāyāṃ svātantryadoṣa uktaḥ kathaṃ parihartavyaḥ ? indriyāpekṣayaiva
parihariṣyata iti nottaram | tadā hi tadapīndriyajñānameva syāt tadvyāpārānuvidhānāt |
na yogijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit |
tadvaramekameva svīkṛtamiti na bhedapakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ | naivam tathā hi mā bhūdindriyā-
pekṣā | vīkṣaṇaṃ tu yathā svasāmarthyānurūpāṃ yogyadeśāvasthitimapekṣya svavijñānajanane
pravartate tathā manaindriyamapi pravartiṣyate, aprāpyakāritāyā ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇatvāt,
arthavattāyāśca manaso'pi tadānīmiṣṭatvāt | pṛthagjanasantānasya tu na tādṛśī śaktiḥ
yato netraśrotravanmano'pi tādṛṅmaryādayā yogyadeśasthamarthasahakāriṇamāsādya vedanam
utpādayediti nātiprasaṅgaḥ | taddaśāyāṃ tu śrutinayanayoriva manaso'pi kiyavareṇa
viṣayasannidhivyavastheti ka evaṃ pramātuṃ kṣama: ? kevalametāvaducyate, yāvattena śakyam
adhigantuṃ svākārārpaṇasahaṃ sahakāri vastu tāvaditarajanāsādhāraṇatruṭyadrūpatayā tasya
gocarībhavati | tathā ca sati vastvākāro vastukṛta eva na bhāvanājanita iti na
visaṃvādaśaṅkā |
nanu cakṣurādestāvadvarataragocarīkaraṇe dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ, manasastu nendriyātikrameṇa
sarvaviṣayasyeti cet –na, paracittajñānādīnāṃ saṃbhavāt | tadapi neṣṭamekeṣāmiti
cet ? adṛṣṭamātreṇa pratikṣepāyogāt | upāyābhāvāditi cet ? upāyābhāve'pi
nānupalambhamātrādanya upāya: | tasmād yadyevaṃ syāt tadā yogi [59b]nāmindriyamano-
jñānayorbhedapakṣe'pi na nirvāha ityupakṣepārthaḥ | nirvāhastvanyathā'pi darśita eva evaṃ
ca sati kālabhedapakṣe'pi na doṣaḥ, yadi [sā] prathamaṃ manojñānavṛttiḥ, yadi
cendriyapathātikrameṇa vṛttiḥ | indriyajñānaṃ tu tasya tadapekṣayā prāmāṇyavirahe'pi na
vyathayatītyalaṃ vistareṇa |

vartamānatāprasaṅgaḥ, yathā nirākāravāde vastusvarūpasyaiva sphuraṇāditi | yadyapi ca
vartamāne'pi jñānākārasyaiva sphuraṇaṃ tathāpi vartamānatayaivādhyavasāyastatra | evaṃ
dūrāsannādibhede'pi veditavyam | tatra yathādhyavasāyaprāptau niyamena saṃvādāt prāmāṇyam
anyadā viparyayaḥ yathā svapnakāminyādau | pratibhāsvargasādhanāgniṣṭomādivikalpe ca
bhāvinaḥ spaṣṭarūpasya pratibhāsābhāvādeva na cintā | na ca tatra prekṣavyāvahārikasya
prāptiniyamaniścayo'sti |
prastute'pi ko niścaya iti cet ? kasya punaratra niścayaścintyate, tasya tadanyasya
vā ? yadi tasya, tadā yathābhyāsāt parito nirastavibhramāśaṅka sādhanajñāne pṛthagjanasya
tathā yogino'pyatyantābhyāsād bhāvibhūtādipratibhāsa: kena vāryate ? athānyasya,
tadedamāyātam | yāvadanyasya na prāmāṇyabodhastāvanna pramāṇam | yāvacca na pramāṇaṃ
tāvannānyasya prāmāṇyabodho'bhrānta iti na kiñcitpramāṇaṃ syāt | tannābhiveśapāravaśyena
kiñcit | tasmādupāyaviśeṣa[60b] sacivabhāvanābhedasyāhatyāsphuraṇāt tādṛsiddhāveva
saṃśayo, na tu siddhe'pi nirālambanatvādidoṣairupadravaḥ śakyaḥ |

gṛhyate yaccādhyavasoyate te dve'nyanivṛttī na vastunī, svalakṣaṇāvagāhitve'bhilāpasaṃsagaṃyogya-
pratibhāsānupapatterityāha, tadapyasaṃbaddham | tathā hi, yathā tathā vā bauddhasiddhāntagandhena
vyavahāraḥ, kāminyākāravikalpabhāvanavat kṣaṇikākārasyāpi paryante viśadopādeyakṣaṇa-
prasavastu dunivāraḥ | yadi punarīdṛgapohasthitiḥ kṣaṇika vikalpaikatalpaśāyinī na kāminyādi-
vikalpamanvetītyupapādayiṣyasi tathaiva grahīṣyāmaḥ | na cādhyavaseyamavastunivṛttimātraṃ vā |
dharmottare'pi hi mate svalakṣaṇamadhyavaseyamiti sthitiḥ |
nanu vahniḥ pratoto mayetyadhyavasāyākāraḥ | tatra ca svalakṣaṇasphuraṇamiti
sāhasam, vikalpādhyavasāyayorekārthatvāt | satyam, na tu tatra sphuratīti tāvatā
svalakṣaṇamadhyavasitamucyate | asphuraṇe tarhyabodhāt kathamavasāya: ? sphuraṇe'pi prati-
bhāsa evāsau, kathamadhyavasāyaḥ ? na ca pratibhāsādhyavasāyāvadhyekārthau | pratibhāso
hi sākṣāt sphuraṇamasphuraṇe'pi pravṛttiviṣayīkaraṇamekavyāvṛtyullekhasāmarthyādadhyavasāyo
bhāṣyamataḥ | ato yadanurūpamanuṣṭhānaṃ tadadhyavaseyam pratibhāsamānarūpānanupraviṣṭameva |

pratyālambanabhāva
indriyavyāpāravirahe ca samastā [6la] parakāraṇasannidhāvasannidhīyamānasattākaṃ
tatpratibaddhaṃ siddhamiti kathamindriyānapekṣyasyārthasya svavijñānaṃ
iti cet ? etadapi paracittajñānasaṃbhavena prativyūḍham | iṣṭāśca paracittavedinaścārvāka -
mīmāṃsakavyatiriktaiḥ | cārvākāderapi sandehānnāparā gatiḥ | sandehe ca vipakṣādekānta-
vyāvṛtterayogaḥ | nanu jñāna kāryasyendriyāpekṣā niyamādeva nānyatra sandeho dahanāpekṣa-
dhūmavat | yadyevaṃ rūpajñānasya vīkṣaṇāpekṣaṇe yādṛśī sāmagrī sā na saṃcaraṇaviśeṣasya
caraṇāpekṣaṇe kalayāpi hīyate tat kathaṃ na dhūmadṛṣṭāntaścaraṇavirahiṇāmuragādīnāṃ
gamananiṣedhāya prabhurabhūt ? kathaṃ vā karādivyāpārasaṅga sāvegamantrodgāraparamparā-
sādhyamekeṣāṃ viṣaśamanādikāryaṃ samādhimātrādanyasya ? na caivaṃ dhūmo'pi kacidindhane
dahanānapekṣodayo dṛṣṭo yato'trāpi tathā śaṅkayeta |
tasmād bahirbhuvo bhāvā yathā hetuphalabhāvenopalambhabhāja: te tathaiva niyata-
vṛttayaḥ | cittasantānasya tu vicitrakarmābhisaṃskārasāmarthyād vicitra eva vivartaḥ |
atastadāśrayakāryamekatra yāvadapekṣaṃ tāvadapekṣamanyatrāpīti na niyantuṃ śakyam | tat
kathaṃ paracittavedanāderabhāva eva ? yadi ca dhūmavadanalamanapekṣya nendriyaṃ buddhiḥ tadā
svaviṣaye'pyutkarṣaghoṣaṇāvīkṣaṇādīnāṃ dīnaiva syāt | tathā hi yāvaddeśaṃ dahanendhanādi-jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
dhūmādisādhanamupalabdhaṃ na tāvaddeśātikrame samartham | evaṃ yāvaddeśe'smākaṃ viṣaye
ndriyādivedanamutpāditavat kathaṃ tadatikrame gṛdhrādīnāmutpādayet ? utpādane vā nendhana-
dahanādikakṣāṃ kṣamate cittasantānāśrayā sāmagrī | nāpi dhūmakakṣāṃ buddhiḥ |
ataḥ sahakāriṇo'tivyavadhānavaduvaikalye'pi ki na kutaścit viśeṣāt
saṃbhāvyate ? jātikṛto'sau vibhāgaḥ, na cittasantānāśrayāditi cet na, jātirapi
hi vicitrakarmādhipatyādeva vicitrasvarūpopasaṃhārasvabhāvā, karma ca na cittādanyaditi
na cittāśrayatvaparihāraḥ | athendriyasya prādhyakāritayā sarvaiva vijñānajananasāmagrī
sādhāraṇadeśetyucyate | tathāpi kasmāt punastāvad dūradeśasthitimati kacillocana-
ruḍhāṃśaśleṣa: kacidavagiva viśrāma iti kimatra vaktavyaṃ karmādhipatyādanyatra ? tasmāt
tadāśrayasya cittasantānasya citraiva śaktiḥ |
nahi bahirapi śakyamevam | anyathā sadṛśapradeśasthāyinoḥ pradīpayoralpakasya
kasyacid dūrasāriṇī kiraṇasaṃhatiritarasya punarkhācīnacāriṇī syāt | atha mantra-
prabhāvādevamapi syāt, sarīsṛpadṛśā ca māndyamādadhātīti cet ? sa tarhi citta-

vyavasthitatvāditi ||

sukhaṃ na tadanyasyeti cet ? arthasya dharma: sādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ jñānasya tataḥ
tadātmaniyataṃ sukhādi na parasādhāraṇamanugrahādirūpatveneti yuktam | bāhyarūpaṃ tu svīkriya-
māṇaṃ sādhāraṇameva tatkāryatve'pi hyanugrahasya, sukhasaṃvidupādeyakṣaṇāntararūpatvāt | tadvadeva
sādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ ceti |
evaṃ na caitrajanitaṃ maitrasya tatputratvaṃ nāma kiñcid gauratvamiva yat sādhāraṇaṃ
syāt, api tu tajjanitatvamevāsya tatputratvaṃ vyavahrayate | sa ca jananavyāpāraścaitrasya
nānyasādhāraṇaḥ | tathā tannimitto'pi vyapadeśaḥ, tajjanitavyapadeśavat | gauratvaṃ tu tatkṛtamapi
na tatkṛtameva guṇāntaratvāditi sādhāraṇaṃ yuktam | na hyasau pitureva gauraḥ kiṃ tu parasyāpi |
evaṃ na jñānakṛtatvamevārthasya vyaktatvaṃ vyavahitādya viśiṣṭarūpasya, kiṃ tu tadatiśāyinaḥ
prakāśarūpasyotpattirityabhyupagama: | anyathā na vyakta ukto viṣayaḥ syāt | tathā vyavahāra -
mātraṃ tu tannimittaṃ syāt, yathā gauratvameva tajjanyatāmātreṇa vyavaharataḥ, sautrāntikasya vā
tajjanakatvena | yathā ca tasya janakajñānāntarasya viṣayatāprasaṅgaḥ, tathāsyāpi janyajñānasyeti
jñānārthayorhetuphalabhāvasamayātikramamātramatiricyate | sādhāraṇatvaparihārastūbhayorapi | na
tu vyaktirūpārthotpattinirvāha ito'sya siddhaḥ |
prakāśotpādane sarva prati prākāśyasaṃbhavaḥ |
• utpādanāprakāśatvasthitau naikamapi prati ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ |

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
bhedābhedavikalpo'pi na prakāśasya bādhakaḥ |
na vā yathoktasādhyena vyāpteriti kimarthaṃkaḥ ||
pareṇa parasaṃvitti yo'bhimanyeta taṃ prati |
śeṣaṃ syādapi doṣāya brūmaḥ svapne'pi na tvidam ||
ekānekatvavirahāt niḥsvabhāvamidaṃ jaḍam |
yathā tathā na kiñcittaṃ sattaikasya kathaṃ tataḥ ||
prakāśamānaṃ nīlādi jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā |
iti prakaraṇe'smābhirbuddhive heturucyate ||
tatraikānekaviraho yadi dharmāntarārpakaḥ |
kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tāvatāpi nīlāderjaḍatā na hi ||
sattāyāṃ nanu siddhāyāṃ jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā |
asatturaṅgaśṛṅgādi na hi tattve'numīyate ||
tathāpya prastutamidaṃ sattācintāviyogataḥ |
siddhāyāmeva sattāyāṃ viśeṣaścintyate yataḥ ||
sattāyāṃ saṃśaye'pyasmāt sacced vijñānameva tat |
tataścādūṣaṇākhyātirasattāsiddhibādhayoḥ ||
prasiddhimātrarūpeṇa dharmitvānnāpyanāśrayaḥ |
anyathā niḥsvabhāvatvahetorapyāśrayaḥ katham ||
tasminna bhāvamātraṃ cet jñānatāmātramatra ca |
bāhyavastutvasiddhistu dvayorapi virodhinī ||
vastutopādhibodhatvaṃ sādhyamatra tvayeti cet |
bodhatvamātra prastāve viśeṣa: kuta īdṛśaḥ ||
jñānatvaṃ vastutāvyāptaṃ tadabhāve bhavenna cet |
viruddhāvyabhicāraḥ ka doṣo yadvāstu vastutā ||
advaitabinduprakaraṇam
kiṃ ca prakāśamātrātmavyatiriktānyathāthavā |
sattā niṣeddhayābhimatā niḥsvabhāvatvahetunā ||
niṣedhe vyatiriktāyā na prakāśātmavāraṇam |
asyaiva vāraṇe kena vāraṇādhyakṣabhāsinaḥ ||
anumānaṃ pramāṇatvād bādhakaṃ yadi kasyacit |
pratyakṣamapi tadbhāvāt sādhakaṃ kiṃ na kasyacit ||
avaśyamante'dhyakṣasya prāmāṇyamanumāśrayet |
prakāśamātrarūpe ca nānumāpekṣamakṣajam ||
athāyamanumānasya viṣayo'kṣadhiyo'paraḥ |
prakāśarūpe'dhyakṣatvādanumāvasaraḥ kutaḥ ||
atha pratyakṣasiddhaṃ yanna tasyeva nirākriyā |
vyāvṛttibhedaḥ kaścātra vicārāsahatā yadi ||
vijñānasyaiva dharmo'stu śaśaśṛṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ |
arthaśaktiviyoge vā dharmo'stu dhiya eva saḥ ||
arthaśaktiviyogaśca vicārāsahtā ca sā |
jñānasyaiva na bāhyasyetyaya~te kimataḥ param ||
prakāśasyaiva cinteyaṃ tadgandho'pi bahinaṃ hi |
tannāgaśṛṅgasāmye'sya siddhe ki na kṛtārthatā ||
bahivaṃdavabhāseṣu prajñaptā rūparāśitā |
saṃskārādvedanāsaṃjñe [71b] abhinne kiṃ na bhedi te ||
mūlamevāprakāśasya duḥsthaṃ sattāvyavasthiteḥ |
prakāśarūpasya sato dharmāntaramabādhakam ||
prakāśasyāpi taddoṣād yadi sattā davīyasī |
aprakāśo'pyasattāyāḥ kimanyat sādhayiṣyati ||
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalau
asattaivāprakāśasya prakāśasya tu nātmanā |
tenaivāsattvamityuktaṃ kalpite na tu yujyate ||
prakāśamānasya punaḥ prakāśādeva satyatā |
abhāvo'vasitenaiva keśasyāpi jaḍātmanā ||
prakāśasaṃmatasyāpi nīlāderata eva hi |
satyamarthakriyaivoktā tāṃ vinā na bhidā dvayoḥ ||
kriyāmātrānubandhācca vijñānasyāpyanityatā |
kriyā'bhāvo yadā tvasmin sattā mukhyaiva bhāsanāt ||
na kṣaṇitvaṃ tadā tasya sattvaṃ ca vyabhicāyaṃtaḥ |
sattvamarthakriyārūpaṃ sādhanaṃ tanna duṣyati ||
na vā tasyāpyanityatvaṃ parihṛtya daśāntaram |
tatkṣaṇasyaiva saṃvitteranyathā na bhidā kacit ||
kāryakāraṇabhāvo'yamāyātastahiṃ cennanu |
sāṃvṛtasyāniṣedho'tra kṣaṇitāpyasya sāṃvṛtī ||
tattvato nityarūpaṃ cet saṃvṛtāvapi yanna sat |
anityapratiṣedhācet tathāpyasthāgatiḥ kutaḥ ||
bhāvaṃ kañcit puraskṛtya bhedābhedāvudīrayet |
deśakālādibhedena svavinmātre tu kaḥ kramaḥ ||
svarūpaṃ buddhiraparairna yauti na bhinatti ca |
svaparapravibhāgo hi dhiyo yācitamaṇḍanam ||
anyasyāvācyatā nāma svabhāvabhāvaśaṃsinī |
tadeva rūpaṃ tattvasya taccādvaite pratiṣṭhitam ||
paraṃ hi vidvan niyataṃ niyataṃ pratipadyate |
anyathā vittimātreṇa na pravṛttinivartane |
advaitabinduprakaraṇam
prathamaṃ grāhakākāro bhinatti grāhyamātmanaḥ |
rūpana tathā grāhyāntarādapi ||
advaitamevetarathā tadabhāve bhidāṃ dyati |
bhedābhedau tato dvaite niyato nādvaye tathā ||
yāvacca svapnabodhāya kālabhedaṃ parāmṛśet |
dhīvikalpāntareṇeyaṃ kṣayeṇa grasyate'nyavat ||
tasmānna nityatā nāma tattvato na ca saṃvṛtiḥ |
kṣaṇitātattvayoge'pi gṛhyatāmanumānavat ||
citraikavyavahāro'pi bhedāpohaparo mataḥ |
ekānekaviyukto hi prakāśaḥ kevalo'tra san ||
sarvaṃśaktiviyuktena prakāśana satāpi kim |
śakyabhāvānna kāryaṃ syāt svarūpaṃ tu ke gacchatu ||
prakāśasyāpi rūpaṃ cet vicāreṇa na labhyate |
vicāramanumāṃ vidmona sā pratyakṣabādhanī ||
guñjānala viparyāsau bādhyate'kṣakṛto'pi cet |
pararūpe bhramānnākṣaṃ svarūpe bhrāntatā kutaḥ ||
' pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ ced vicārāvasaro hṛtaḥ |
bruvatā niyataṃ kiñcit sādhyaṃ vā bādhyameva vā ||
tatrāyukti bruvāṇasya ślāghā sadasi kodṛśī |
nānumāyāḥ parā yukti: ki siddhaṃ tadanādare ||
svīkṛtā tena setyasmāt tanmatyā bodhanaṃ yadi |
abādhane'syāḥ svīkārāttaddhiyā[72a]bodhanaṃ katham ||
sādhyaṃ na kiñciditi cet bādhāyā api sādhyatā |
sāpi neti vaco vyarthaṃ praśnamātre'pi kiṃ phalam ||

rūpamiti na tat tasya viplavopanītam yena tadvedanaṃ bhrāntiḥ syāt | nīlaṃ tu rūpāntaratvāt
viplavopanītamapi syāditi syāttadvedanaṃ bhrāntiḥ | tato'sti nīlādī bādhakasyāvatāro na
prakāśe | kalpitālīkayostu niṣedho boddhavyaḥ sarvatreti ||
atra cintyate | ko'yaṃ prakāśo nāma nīlādibhyo vyatiriktaḥ, avyatireke
bādhābhayanivṛtteḥ ? na ca vyatirikta kiñcit pramāṇamasti | na tāvat pratyakṣam, prakāśa-
mānarūpānnīlādaparasyopalambhāsaṃbhavāt | na cānumānam, kadācidapi pratyakṣatāmananubhavataḥ
kenacit saṃbandhagrahaṇānupapatteḥ |
kiṃ ca,
prakāśa ātmasantāne'numānena pratīyate |
parokṣaviṣayeṇeti kā dhikkṛtirataḥ param ||
vyaktamidaṃ śabarasvāmidarśanaṃ śaraṇīkṛtamiti kimatra vaktavyam ? tadayaṃ dṛśyātmā
kumbhādibhyo vyatirekeṇānupalabhyamānaḥ sāmānyādivanna sadvyavahāragocarībhavitumarhati |
anyathā teṣāmapyaniṣedhaḥ,
nityatvāṅgīkṛtestaccet kramādivirahādasat |
na pramāvyāpakābhāvo dṛśyādṛṣṭeranādare ||
kathaṃ vā viṣāṇaguṇakarmādeniṣedha iti yatkiñcidetat | atha nīle bodharūpe
pratīyamāne nīlabodhātmanoḥ pratītiraśakyāpahnaveti na siddhānupalabdhiriti cet ? tarhi
gavi śābaleye pratīyamāne ubhayātmapratītyā pratyavatiṣṭhamānaḥ kathaṃ niṣedhyaḥ ? pṛthakpratītya

bhāvastu sādhāraṇaḥ | avidyāvaśāt prakāśanīlayorapṛthakkathana miti cet ? guṇadravyayorapyevaṃ
bhaviṣyati | yadi samavāyaniṣedhe nirbaṃndhaḥ, kimavidyāvaśāt pṛthagadarśanamathābhāvādeveti

kariśatasya vā,
tasmāt,

na santi sāmānyaguṇādayo yathā
tathā
sitādibhedeṣu niraṃśabhāsiṣu |
prakāśāntaramapyasattataḥ

deśasyāpi bhidā yadi svatanuvad bhidyeta bhāso dvayo-

bhedastanniścayaśca |
deśe vā bhidirūpameva na paraṃ rūpaṃ na deśo'paraḥ |
nanu vātātapayordeśābhede'pi svabhāvabheda iti cetu-na, tayoravayavirūpatayā
utpatteḥ, ekaghanākārayoḥ sapratighayorantho'nyadeśaniveśa: | paramāṇunikarastu vyatikaramā-
sādayati | tathā ca sati,
bhinnātmā marudātapāṇunicayo bhinnapradeśo na kim ||
tato yathā svabhāvabhedastathā deśabhedo'pīti na deśo nāmānyaḥ svarūpāt | tatastadabhede
svarūpābheda eva prakāśasthāpi |
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
tadvad yadyaṇusaṃhaterupagamo doṣo'pi tadvad bhavet
sthūle vā pratighe'pi deśabhidayā doṣastathaiva sthitaḥ |
kiṃ ca vyāptirihānyathāpyuparatā khaṇḍe'nyathā bhāsana-
prāptestadvaśataḥ sitādini tato yāvat prakāśasthitiḥ ||
yāvaddeśo hi nīlādyākārastāvad vyāptivirahe khaṇḍapratibhāsanaprasaṅgo nīlādau
tadvaśataḥ pṛthagiṣṭaprakāśavaśāt | tato yāvat prakāśanaṃ sitādestāvattasya prakāśākhyasya
sthityā bhāvyam | tatastāvaddeśavyāpinastasyāpi nīlasyevāvayaviparamāṇurūpacintāyāṃ
punaḥ sādhāraṇadoṣānna mukti: | tasmānna nīlādiniṣedhe kasyacit sthitirbhedasyaivābhāvāt
pratibhāsabhedābhāvāditi ||
atha kṣaṇayorabhedabhāsane'pi yathā bhedasiddhirbādhikāt, evamihāpi | yathā hi
kāryaviśeṣasya bhāvābhāvāvanyathānupapadyamānī tayorbhedasādhanau tathā bādhakasya bhedena vṛttiḥ
prakāśanīlayorapi | tato bādhyānnīlādabādhya: prakāśo bhinna eveti cet ? ucyate,
abādhyatā nāma paryadāsaprasajyabhedena dvidhā | paryudāso'pi prakṛtavyaktiviṣayaḥ aspṛśyādi-
vadbādhāntaramevopanayediti, abrāhmaṇakṣatriyavajjātiparyudāsāt |
abādhā nāmeyaṃ pramitibalasiddhiyadi matā
pramiyokāpi svavidi bhidurāyāṃ prabhavati |
abhāvo bādhāyāḥ punarasati sādhāraṇatayā
pade saṃdehasya prathayatu kathaṃ bhedamamutaḥ ||
prasajyapratiṣedhapakṣe hi bādhāsphuraṇamātramabādhārtha: | [73b] tacca sandigdha-
sattāke'satyapi samānam kathaṃ tato nīlādebhinnavasturūpatāṃ prakāśasya sādhayet ?
nīlādibādhyamabādhyastu prakāśa iti bhinnarūpasiddhau kaḥ sandeha iti cet ? naivam,
abādhāyā bādhakāsphuraṇamātratvāt, sattāsandehe bādhitādapi nīlādbhinnarūpasiddherayogāt |
ataeva pade sandehasyetyuktam |
kṣaṇabhaṅge tu bādhakāntarabalādaśakyastatparihāraḥ | naitādṛśāsārasādhanapratyāśā |
na ca tadvadatrāpi śakyamabhidhātum | tatra hi kadācinmadhūdakāharaṇādivat sthūlakālā-
pekṣayādhyakṣeṇa vyavahṛto'rthakipāśaktikramaḥ kadācidaśakyo'pi kṣaṇāpekṣayā sāmarthyā-

yātaḥ svabhāvabhedaṃ vedayet | sakalakriyākṣayiṇi kṣaṇe'bhāvaprasaṅgāt, kṛtasya kartuṃ na
śakyatvāt |
so'yaṃ kāryakramo na kāraṇakramamatikramituṃ kramata iti yuktam | na ca tatheha
prakāśamātrasādhyaṃ kiñcit siddhamadhyakṣataḥ, sāmarthyāyātaṃ veti | na cāpoddhāreṇa kārya -
bhedavyavasthāpito'pyātmabheda: sakṛdabhedabhāsini tāttviko bhavitumarhati vikalpamātra-
niveśino'nyatra, pradīpe tamaḥkṣayāvakāśapiñjaraṇopayogiprakāśapiśaṅgarūpavat | abhinnā-

rūpapratibhāsasya sakṛdeva paryavasāne sarvasya trikālālokaprasaṅgāt | na caivamadhyakṣa-
vyavahāryo'pi kāryabhedo bhāvābhāvadaśābhyāṃ kāraṇabhedāya prabhavet | ekīkṛtya
grahaṇe hi ya evaikakṣaṇe bhāvo'bhāvo vā kāryasya sa eva kṣaṇāntare'pi, vivekā-
bhāvāt |

evābhedena sphuṭataro'nubhūyate | tathāpi bhedakalpane kimaparāddhamupādhisahasreṇa ? na
cānupalabdheranyad vārakaṃ nāmetyuktaprāyam | tadiyamabādhā dṛśyānupalabdhisaṃbhave prati-
jñāyamānā svayameva viśīryate nottarāntaramapekṣata iti |
kiṃ ca bādhātra nātreti pṛthagbhāse dvayorbhavet |
anirbhāse tadaṅgasya tatrāsiddhisthitaḥ kutaḥ ||
siddho'pi tatra hetuśceśa samartha: prakalpate |
nūnaṃ na sādhyasaṃbaddho nākāre'pi tataḥ kṣamaḥ ||
svabhāvaṃ kāraṇaṃ vārtho'vyabhicāreṇa sādhayan |
kasyacid vādabādhāyāṃ svabhāvānna nivartate ||
nanu prakāśo nīlādau pratibhātyeva dehinaḥ |
tanmātre bādhakābhāvaḥ khyāyamānaḥ kṣamo na kim ||
nīlasvabhāvāśiduraprakāśakathanena kim |
na hi tasyaiva bādhāyā virahaṃ vaktumudyamaḥ ||372
jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalauṃ
nīlasya [syāt ] prakāśa [74a][ścetprakāśa:] kimataḥ param |
parato'pi bhavannasya prakāśaḥ śakyavāraṇaḥ ||
nānyato'pi prakāśo'sya prakāśo'syānya eva cet |
na tannīlaṃ prakāśyeta prakāśe'nyasya tasya kim ||
saṃbandhasya ca bādhyatvāttasyeti na samanvayaḥ |
ṣaṣṭhyā lābhe'pi kathamapyaśakyo rūpasaṃkaraḥ ||
yataḥ kuto'pi vā tasmāt prakāśo'syānapahnavaḥ |
tadabādhe ca na phalaṃ na tanmātraṃ ca kiñcana ||
pratyāśayā tvabhimataṃ prasiddhamabhidhīyatām |
āśrayāsiddhinirdhūtā hetavo'pyata eva ca ||
abādhyatvaprasiddhārthāḥ saṃkalpakalite'tha cet |
tasyāmarthasamānatvād vidhisiddhau na sādhutā ||
abādhayaiva sattvaṃ cet sattve hetustataśca sā |
iti cakrakamāyātaṃ māyāmetāmapohati ||
athāpyabādhā bādhāyāḥ sphuraṇe satyapodyate |
tadabhāve tu siddhaiva saṃdehapadamīdṛśī ||
va[rga]dharmastvāśrīyamāṇo na cakrakamatikrāmati |
āśrayo'pyastu hetustu kathyatāṃ bādhabādhanaḥ |
svayaṃvedanamevātha pṛthag nāstīti darśitam ||
na ca svavittirityeva yuktaḥ saṃpratyayo'pi vaḥ |
svavittāvapi nīlāderyadā bādhābhidhāvati ||
svasaṃvittirna nīlasya yadi kiṃ na prakāśate |
prakāśyantāṃ pareṇeti na śakyamidamīdṛśam ||
pareṇa parasaṃvido'nyatra vistareṇa nirastatvāt | asattvānna paramiti cet ?

rūpatvāttasya | kalpitatādātmyānna doṣa iti cet ? bālapratāraṇametat | pratibhāsādeva
hi tādātmyakalpanam, tatkṛtaśca pratibhāsa iti vyaktamitaretarāśrayatvam |
na pratibhāsanāt kalpanam api tu pratibhāsāvasāyāditi cet ? so'pi
pratibhāsāvasāya: pratibhāsāditi cakrakramastu, tādātmyakalpanātaḥ pratibhāsastatastadava-
sāyastatastatkalpa [namiti | tatkalpa] namapi na tādātmyakalpanātaḥ kiṃ tu kalpanā-
viṣayīkṛtaṃ yattādātmyaṃ tata iti cet na, tasya kalpanātaḥ prāgabhāvāt anyathā
kalpitatvānupapatteḥ | na ca kapitaṃ kvacidarthakriyāyāmupayujyamānamupalabdham, tathātve
satyatāyā eva prasakteḥ |
etenālī katādātmyakīrtanamapi pratyuktam kacidupayoge'līkatvasyāpyanupapatteḥ |
anyathā nāmamātrakripāyāṃ niṣedhānibaṃndhāt | kacidupayoginaḥ prakāśamānasyāpi
bādhanādalīkatvamaviruddhamiti cet ? prakāśasya na [tarhi ] bādhitumaśakyatvāt kacid
upayogamapi yadi na bādhate bādhakaṃ kimavaśyaṃ bādhakamabhidheyamiti kuto'līkatādātmyasya ?
atha sāmarthyādarthaśakti bādhate na sākṣāt ? bhavatu kimatra nirbandhena śaktibādhāyāḥ
siddhatvānnālīkamupayogi tādātmyamiti sthitam |
yadapyucyate | vijñānameva prakāśarūpatvāt prakāśamā [74b] namanādibhrānti -
vāsanopaplavatvād bhrāntamalokairnīlādibhirākāraiḥ prakhyāti svapnādivaditi, tadapi etena
prativyūḍham |
nīlādivyatiriktasya vijñānanāmno'nupalabdheḥ prakriyāghoṣaṇāmātrametat | sādhya -
śūnyaḥ svapnadṛṣṭāntaśca | api caivamalīkatayā kārakaśakterabhāvānnīlādiriti itthaṃbhūta-
vivakṣāyāmapi sahaprakhyānamātramartha iti vyaktamuktastatprakāśyatāvirahaḥ |
tat kathaṃ
svasaṃvedanātikrama: ? athāvidyāvāsanāvaśāt tathā khyātīti tatprakāśyataiva bhaviṣyatīti
cet ? evaṃ satyavidyāhetureva syānna prakāśikā | prakāśarūpasya tu tasya tasyāḥ sakāśā-
dudayaḥ, pradīpasyeva svahetoriti kutaḥ svaprakāśanāśa: ?
evamapi paraprakāśyatāvyavasthāyāṃ cānubhavasyāpi prasaṅga iti na kiṃcit
svaprakāśaṃ nāma | tathāpyasaṃbhavādeva svasaṃvedanānna kacit sattāsiddhiḥ | tannāyaṃ nyāyaḥ,
prakāśarūpajanakāpekṣayā kṣaya: svasaṃvitteriti evaṃ nīlāderapīti siddhā svasaṃvittiḥ |
athānīla[syālī]katvānna kāryatā tataḥ prakāśanamātramavidyayā prakāśena vā anubhavasya374

tu vastutvāt samanantarapratyayena jananamevocyata iti cet ? tadapi yatkiñcit | anubhavo'pi

kāryatāparipanthina iti ||
api ca, nīlamalīkamastu na vā, kāryatā tu kathaṃ vāryate ? apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi
svabhāvaniṣpattau bhāvaḥ kārya uktaḥ |
kādācitkatayā siddhā nīlasyāsya sahetutā |
nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vā hetoranyānavekṣaṇāt' ||
evaṃ deśādyaniyamo'pyupalakṣaṇīyaḥ | na cānyasyāpi kāryatāvyavahāranibandhanam
anyadasti deśakālapratiniyamasiddhāṃ parāyattatāmavadhūya | anyathā cānubhavasthāpi mā bhūt |
tadayaṃ śraddhāmātraviṣayasya tādṛśādeva janmajalpanaṃ dṛṣṭāt kutaścidākārāntarasya dṛṣṭānutpatti
pratikṣipatīti kimatra brūma: ? etenābhūtvābhāve'pi śaktyabhāvānna kāryatvamiti nirastam,
uktakrameṇa śaktivyavasthānāt | śraddhāviṣayasya tu cintyatāmadarśanāt | mā bhūt śaktiḥ,
parāpekṣodayatayā kāryatvaṃ tu kiṃ nivartate, atadvayāvṛtteranapāyāt ?
atha vastudharmaḥ kāryatvam, na ca śaktimantareṇa vastutvam | tarhi śaktirapyastu,
tadvyāptavastudharmakāryatvasya darśanāt | śaktyabhāvāt tadeva nāstīti cet —na, asiddha-
tvāt | kāryatve tu na sandehaḥ kāryāntaravat | tasmād yadi śaktikāryatvayoḥ pratibandhaḥ
śaktiranumīyamānā kacidastu nānūhamātreṇa pratikṣepa: | pratibandhābhāve tu siddhaṃ kārya-
tvam | ataḥ kathamucyate nīlasyākāryatvāt [75a] prakāśamātra hetubhiḥ yato na
svasaṃvedanamiti |
kiṃ ca prakāśanamātraṃ kasyacit kenacidityapratītopādānāntarasaṃbhave pūrvāparakṣaṇā-
nāmabhedādhyavasāyād ghaṭādivadālokena syādapi vaktum alīkābhimate tu kīdṛśī
durgṛhītiriyam ? apūrvotpattistu na virudhyate kevalaṃ nīlatayeva prakāśatayāpīti | mā bhūd
vā sarvathā kāryatvam, tadāpi parāpekṣāniyame paraprakāśyatāśaṅkāpi syāt | sarvathā
nirapekṣatve niḥsaṃśayaḥ svayaṃ vedanābhāvaḥ sarvākārāṇām | tatra ca bādhasandarśane'nyatrāpi

kathamabādhasiddhaye prabhavet ?
vijñānasya tadeva rūpamiti cennīlātmanastanna kim |
yathā hi prakāśasya prakāśa eva rūpam na tu tasya viplavopanītamityucyate, tathā
nīlasyāpi nīlataiva rūpaṃ na tat tasya viplavopanītamityucyamānamapi na vaktraṃ vakrīkaroti

na nīlasthitiḥ, nīlamantareṇāpi na prakāśasthitiḥ | pīte'stīti cet ? astu, na tu
nīladharmaḥ | prakāśaśabdasāmyācet ? tarhi pītadharmaṃprakāśāpekṣayā prakāśavinākṛtasyāpi
• nīlasya sthitirapahnavasya viṣayaḥ |

tatastasya tadeva rūpamiti neyaṃ prakāśaikaniyatā kalpanā,

nīlotpalaṃ ca nidarśanaṃ smārayāmaḥ, vastrodakasya nidarśayitumaśakyatvāt | sthitipracyuti-
lakṣaṇayoriva viruddhayodhaṃrmayoruddiṣṭādhārayoranupalabdhereveti bhavanta evātra pramāṇam |
tadalamabhiniveśavaśatayā | tasya tadeva rūpamiti śraddheyasya,
saṅkalpaikaniveśino yadi tathā nirbhāsinaḥ kiṃ na tat ||
satyatvaṃ nīlasya, kevalaṃ svarūpanirbhāsa evāsya sattāsiddhāvadhiko'parādhaḥ |
ki cāpūrvo'yamupāyastasya tadeva tattvamiti bādhāvidhūtaye | bādhyamapi hi pradhāna-
sāmānyādi,
yad yena rūpeṇa vikalpitaṃ vā vibhāti vā tasya tadeva tattvaṃ
pramāṇatastattu sadanyathā vā bādhāvakāśo dvitaye'pi tasmāt |
nīle prakāśe vā | yadi paramasiddhayādidoṣasya vibhāgena vṛttau vibhāgaḥ, na tu tadeva
tattvamiti kṛtvā | kiṃ ca,
āropitaṃ kalpitameva bādhyaṃ prakāśabhṛd bādhyamalīkamāhuḥ
tattvaṃ tataḥ kalpitaniṣṭhameva mā vāstu dṛśyaikagataṃ kathaṃ syāt 11.jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
āropitatvaṃ jalavat kalpita eva vyavahriyate kevalaṃ bādhye | prakāśamānaṃ tu
bādhitamalīkamapi vyapadiśanti, dvicandravat | tato yadi dṛśyamapyāropitamiti
vakta[75b]vyam, ucyatām | dṛśyamevāropitamiti tu kuta etat ? tasmānna kalpitamāropa-
parihāreṇa vyavasthitaṃ pramāṇasiddhādanyatra | ataḥ pramāṇena siddhirbādhā vā nirūpaṇamarhati |
na tu tasya tadeva tattvamityeva bādhoddhūtiḥ siddhirvā |
tadayamapi vibhāgaḥ kriyamāṇo nīlādayaḥ saṃvṛtisantaḥ pratīyamānatve'pi bādhya-
mānatvāt | nīlādipratibhāsaṃ tu prakāśaśarīraṃ vijñānaṃ paramārthasat, bādhakāyogāt,
pramāṇasiddhaśaktiyogācceti hastasamāracita eva pratibhāti | nīlavyatirikte hi prakāśe
nīlavad vyāpakānupalambhasya pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro nānicchāmātreṇa nivarteta ityādyuktam |
bādhā ca prakāśābhimatasyāprakāśāt kīdṛśī paretyapi | tathā śaktirapyākāragocaraiva
ityanantaram |
vyatirekaścāyaṃ kṛtakānityatvavat kalpanāmātropanītaḥ pratibhāti, na sākṣāntri-
rbhāsī | yamalakavat, dvicandravad vā | bhinne ca pratibhāsamāne dharmiṇi śakyamadhigantumatra
dharmo'yaṃ saṃbhavī, na saṃbhavī cātreti | viśeṣato vyāpakānupalambhasya viparyayeṇa vastudharmasyai-
vopaneyatvāt | sarvaśca bhedasādhano vyavahārasādhana eva, viruddhadharmasaṃsargamantareṇa kacidapi
bhedāsiddheḥ | anyathā na kacidabhedo nāma viruddhau ca dharmona kalpanāmātreṇa bhintaḥ |
pramāṇataśca bhinnādhikaraṇāveva pratyetavyau, nirādhārayoḥ bhinnādhārayorvā pratītau na
[pramāṇā] pramāṇayoranyataravyāpāro virodhasiddhirvā | bhinnadharmiṇośca tayoḥ siddhau ko'paro
dharmabhedasādhanavyavasāya: ?
ataeva vyavahārasiddhirmukhaṃ pratīti nirṇayaḥ | tatra dharmabhedasiddhiḥ kacid deśabhedena
golakavat, kacit kālabhedena | yadadhikāreṇocyate, ata eva tayoravasthayoḥ vastubhedo
niśceya iti | na hi tatrāpīyaṃ kuśūlāvasthā, iyaṃ kṣetrāvasthā ceti | kālabhedenānupadarśane
karaṇākaraṇābhyāṃ bhedaḥ śakyadarśanaḥ |
tāvatā ca bhedasiddhiravasiteti kriyākriyopanyāso vyavahārasādhana eva | yatra
tu na deśakālābhyāṃ bhedollekhaḥ, tatra pratibhāsabheda eva śaraṇamindriyabhedo vā |
pānakasya rūparasādivat, cārvākasya svābhyupagama iva buddhiśarīrayoḥ | sa hi śailādi-
vikalpaṃ karacaraṇādyākārāccharīrādvisadṛśamanudāharaṇe kenākāreṇa śailādivikalpatāṃ
sākārasiddhiśāstram
sphuṭayet ? yatra tu pratibhāsabhedagandho'pi nāsti kalpanākārādanyastatra nīlotpalādi-
vadabheda eva tāttvikaḥ |
abhinnavedanasyaikye yantaivaṃ taddhi bhedavat |
sidhyedasādhanatvasya bhedābhedau kimāśrayau ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
tasmād bādhābādhalakṣaṇaviruddhadharmādhyāso dharmiṇa: pratibhāsabhedamantareṇa na
bhedavyavahārāya prabhavati | kevalaṃ bheda [76a] sādhanaṃ sattāsādhanarūpatvānna trayīṃ doṣa-
jātimatipatati | yadapyucyate, yadyena rūpeṇa naikaṃ nānekaṃ, na tat tena sat | tad
yathā duḥkhaṃ sukharūpeṇa | naikaṃ nānekaṃ ca vijñānaṃ nīlādirūpeṇeti vyāpakānupalabdhiriti,
tadapi hṛdayaparitoṣamātrametenaiva nirastam | tathāhi na vijñāyate na vijānātīti vā
vyāpāra nibandhanaṃ vijñānatvamiṣṭamanyatra niṣedhāt, kiṃ tu svaprakāśatāsvabhāvam | sa
ca prakāśastenātmanā asanniti na tādātmyaniṣedhamātramabhimatam, kiṃ tu svenātmanā
sanneveti |
anena tadvad doṣānavatārādityapyākṣiptam | anyathā na vyatirekasiddhirbandhyā-
sute'pi vyavacchedamātreṇa prasaṅgāt | tataśca bādhābādhābhyāmeva bhedasiddhirityasmānna
kaścidatirikto'rtha upātta iti tenaiva gatametat | tathāpi kiñciducyate | ihākāra-
vyatiriktaprakāśasādhanaprakaraṇe'pratibhāsamāna eva vā prakāśo'numānena sādhayitavyaḥ,
pratibhāsamāna eva vā ākārād vyatirikto vidhātavyaḥ, ubhayathāpi tu vidhisādhanā-
dhikāre kaḥ prastāvo vyāpakānulambhasya ? tadāhitena rūpeṇa sattve'pi svarūpeṇa yadi
asattvaśaṅkāyāḥ na nivṛttiḥ śṛṅgasyeva kuto bhedasiddhiḥ ?
atha tayorabhāvo bhāvāntarasvabhāva evābhimataḥ tadā svabhāvahetureva prayoktavyaḥ,
vidhiviṣayatvād vivādasya | yadā tu tadabhāve'pi tat syāditi saṃśayīta kaścit
tanmātre yukto vyāpakānupalambhaḥ | na caikānekaviyoge'pi sattvaśaṃkāyāḥ prastāvaḥ| na
ca viparyaya vivakṣāyāṃ kṣemaḥ | tadā hi yad yena rūpeṇa sat tat tena ekamanekaṃ veti
darśanīyam | na cātra dṛṣṭāntaḥ pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro vā śakyanirvāhaḥ | na hi prakāśamātraṃ
kacit siddhamanyasya cāsattvāditi kuto dṛṣṭāntaḥ, ka pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro vā, anya-
sādhanābhāvāt, tatsādhanatve vā anavasthāprasaṅgāt ?

jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
prakāśaśca prakāśarūpeṇa sanniti pakṣadharmopasaṃhārakāle [vā] nāprakṛtopālambha-
parihāraḥ | na hi svarūpeṇaikānekatve vivādaḥ | kiṃ tvākāreṇa saha bhedābhede | ekā-
nekatvavivādino vā sattvasiddhiriti kutaḥ ? śaktyabhāvādeva tarhi nīlādirasannekā -
nekatve'pīti kiṃ tadupanyāsaprayāsena tadabhāve'pi prasajyaśaktyā sattvavyavasthāpanāt ?
anyathā tatsaṃśaye ca kathamavasthāpayet ? sā ca cintayiṣyate |
atha tenaikānekabhāva iti svarūpeṇa ekānekabhāvaḥ, tatastenaiva sattvamityabhi-
matam ? tadāpi kiṃ punarasya tatsvarūpaṃ yenaikānekatāyoga iti praśne yadīdameva tarjanī-
nirdeśayogyamiti ucyate, tadā nolametaditi na tenaikānekaṃ vijñānamiti plavata etat |
athānyat ? tanna siddham | siddhau vā kimanena ? sa caupālambhasta[76b]davasthaḥ |
bhinnasya hi siddhāveva vivādaḥ, na tu tasmin siddhe'pi kiṃ pararūpeṇāpi tasya sattvam
iti prastāvaḥ |
atha siddha evāyaṃ prakāśo dharmī, tasya nīlādirūpeṇāsattvasiddhau sāmarthyalabdho
bhedaḥ, tāvatā ca siddhamabhimatamato na vidheranurodha iti vyāpakānupalambha eva prakṛtopa-
yogīti cet ? mahatīyaṃ vedagdhī, kevalamavidyāpi nīlādinā asan prakāśo yadi
svenāpi rūpeṇa tathā, tadā kā bhedasiddhi: ? nanu tasyāsattvāśaṃkā nāstyeva, svasaṃvedana-
pratyakṣa siddhatvāt, svabhāve bhrāntyabhāvāt | bhede eva hi vivādaḥ | tādṛśī tahi siddhiḥ
nīlasyāpi kathaṃ bādhā ? prakāśasya prakāśa eva rūpamityādāvuktameva | śakyaṃ ca
nīlaprakāśasya nīlaprakāśa eva rūpamityādi vaktum | tato bhedādhikṣepe'pi yadi
svānubhavo bādhakamanavakāśīkurvan prakāśasattāṃ sādhayet tathāpi kimanena ? tathā
aśaktāvapi kimanena, nīlavattatrāpi hastakatyāgāvarjanāt bhedāsiddheḥ ?
atha parasya paramārthasattvena siddhaḥ prakāśo bheda eva vivādastataḥ sanneva prakāśo
na nīlātmaneti sādhyasiddhiḥ | sarvopāyaparikṣīṇanyāyaparyavāsanā tarhi vaidagdhī |
tadetadātmavādino ghaṭanairātmyasiddhinyāyena helāmarhati | kiṃ cāsmin sādhane'bhedāva-
bhāsinoranubhavākārayorbhedaḥ pratijñārthaḥ tadrūpeṇa ekānekaviraho hetuḥ | na cāsya yathokta-
sādhyenānvayo dṛṣṭānte darśayituṃ śakyaḥ | tatrāpi duḥkhādyākā ravyatirekiṇa: prakāśasya
asiddheḥ | siddhāvapi yathā śātamaśāteneti na vaktavyam | yathā duḥkhānubhavo duḥkhā-
dyākāraṇeti yuktam |

sākārasiddhiśāstram
anyathā hyāṃkārāntaraparigṛhītaprakāśasyākārāntareṇāsattvakhyāpane tadapekṣayaiva
bhedaḥ syāt | tataśca sādhyakāle nīlākārasya pītānubhavād bhedaḥ sidhyet | tato yadi
svaprakāśāpekṣo bhedo dṛṣṭānte nopadarśayituṃ śakyaḥ sādhyo'pi kathaṃ bhaviṣyati, anvayasya
evābhāvāt ?
yad yena naikāneka miti sāmānyenānvayo'trokta iti cet ? tadasat | yataḥ,
anukto'pīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhya ātmārthavanmataḥ |
tadetadapi cakṣurādipārārthyasādhanādinā samānam | athavā yad yena naikānekam
ityatra yadabhinnābhāsi yenāvabhāsineti vivakṣitam, atha sāmānyeneti vikalpya,
viśeṣe'nugamābhāvaḥ sāmānye siddhasādhanam |
sukhaduḥkhayoriva nīlapītānubhavayoraparaspararūpatayā tenātmanāsattvākṛṣṭabhedasiddheḥ,
abhedagrāhiṇastu pratyakṣasyobhayatrāpi na kṣatiḥ | śeṣamasmad bṛhadīśvaravādavat | api ca yadā
prakāśaśca naikāneko nīlādineti pakṣe hetorupanayaḥ, tatra ko'yaṃ prakāśo nāma, prakāśanam,
prakāśata iti vā ? athārthāntarameva kiñcit prakāśaśabdābhidheyaṃ prakāśayatītyādivyāpārā-
pekṣayā vyavasthitenirasta [77a]tvāt ?
prathamapakṣe prakāśamānānāṃ nolapītādīnāṃ prakāśo nāma dharmamātrametat,
bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇa bhinnavadābhāsamānamapi kalpanābuddhī na dharmirūpavighaṭane taṭastham
āsituṃ śaktam, tat kutastattvatto bhedasiddhiḥ ? na hi dharmirūpamuddhaya dharmāṇāṃ kacidapi
sattvamasti guṇakarmādivat | kartṛsādhanapakṣe tu nīlādireva prakāśata iti tasyaiva tena rūpeṇa
śūnyateti pūrvavat |
arthāntarapakṣe ca yadi prakāśata iti sānvayapadaṃ, tadā nīlādivyatiriktasya tasya
dṛśyānupalabdhibādhitasya tenātmanāsatve'pi na sādhyasiddhi: | niranvayanāśapakṣe'pi na
pramāṇasiddhiḥ, tatra ca vyavacchedamātrayoḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvāśrayādāśrayāsiddhiparihāre'pi na
prakṛtopayogaḥ | athāyameva pratividitaḥ prakāśo dharmī | nanu pratividita iti pratibhāsamānaḥ
saca nīla eva, na tadvyatiriktaḥ kaścit |
nanu tadvyatiriktasādhanāyeva yatna eṣaḥ kathaṃ prathamatastatprārthanamiti cet ?
kimapi sādhyamastu bhavataḥ, sādhanādhārastu niṣṭhitasvarūpo darśanīyo yadi prakāśo nāma380

pratihatam ? ataeva yathā tasya sādhyārtho yatnastathā parasyāpi sādhyārthina eva

sākārasiddhiśāstram
atha vyāpakānupalambhastasya tatrāvatārayitumaśaktiḥ ? evaṃ tarhi duḥkhamapi
prakāśātmaiveti na kadācit prahīyeta | api caivamavayavyādeḥ pratyujjīvanaprasaṅgāt
sarvamāditaḥ prabhṛti śīrṇam | tasmānna kacidabhedapratibhāse bhedasiddhiḥ | ataeva sarvo
bhedaheturvyavahārasādhana ityuktam |
ye'pyāhu: dvaitābhāso dharmī bhrāntatvāt satyasaṅgato'vaśyaṃ taimirikacandrabimba-
dvayanirbhāso yathādṛṣṭa iti teṣāmapyasatprakāśo bhrāntirabhimatetyeṣā pratyāśā |
sāca nityasyeta eva [nirastā] | evaṃ māyākhyātirasatyetyādyapi nirastam | na ca
māyākāro nāma svaprakāśākāra vyatiriktaḥ siddhaḥ | jñānāntarabhavaṃ ca jñānāntaramiṣṭam
iti |

nānātvādeva cānyonyavedanaṃ tāsu neṣyate ||

anyonyavedanāpavādaḥ | sa cāpracyutaḥ prastute'pīti na viśeṣaḥ | nanu sāhityapratibhāse
vyavasthāpye kimekasaṃvidāveśena, sādhyavirodhinā tamantareṇāpi kṣaterabhāvāt ? nanu
sāhityamityapi sahacāramātraṃ tadde śakālopaniyate lakṣaṇaṃ khyātam | pratibhāsaśca teṣāṃ
svasvarūpa sākṣātkaraṇamiti nānyonyavedanamupapāditam santamasamagrasannihitāneka-
puruṣavat | tataḥ parasparasaṃvidāveśa eva parasparavedanavyavahāropayogī kimatra sāhitya-
mātreṇa ? atha sarveṣāṃ sarvatra pratibhāsa eva sāhityapratibhāsaśabdenābhimataḥ, tadā
sāhityapratibhāse'pi sādhye viruddhaḥ sarvatrakasaṃvidāveśa iti riktā vācoyukti: |
tadarthatve hi sahāya evāyam |
ekasaṃvidi nānyonyadhvaniścet tadapahnave |
pratītireva nānyonyamarthaṃdoṣo'tra duḥsahaḥ ||
sākārasiddhiśāstram
mā bhūd vā sāhāyyaṃ sāhityapratibhāsasya tu parasparapratibhāsārthatve [90a]
abhinnopādvanatve'pi bhedāniṣedhāt, na hi svasaṃvitparasaṃvidamāviśatītyatra dūṣaṇe
kimuttarīkṛtamiti na vidyaḥ, paryāyamātraghoṣaṇe viśeṣāpoṣaṇāt ||
api ca,
ekopādānabhāve'pi na hi tāḥ sahitā api |
āviśanti mitho vittimanyathā bheda eva kaḥ ||
svavidekanimagnāstā na spṛśantyanyasaṃvidam |
sākṣātkurvanti cānyonyaṃ kimapyetanmahādbhutam ||
upādānābhedād vyatiparicayaśced varamataḥ
svabhāvasyābhedo bhavatu na tu bhinne'pyanubhavaḥ |
tathaikā sāmagrī yadi niyatavastugrahasahaṃ
sṛjeccetastat kiṃ bhayamubhayathā lakṣaṇahateḥ ||
evaṃ hi satyutpattisārūpyābhyāṃ yad grāhyalakṣaṇaṃ tasya dūṣaṇād bhītirna kācid,
bahirarthaṃvādino'nyathaiva grāhyagrāhakabhāvasya sulabhatvāt | tatropādānābhedāt parasparamanubhavaḥ
sarveṣāmanubhavasvabhāvatvāt | ekasāmagrījanyatve tu jaḍānubhavayoḥ pratiniyataṃ vedyatvaṃ vedakatvaṃ
ca syāt | tatpratibandhācca nātiprasaṅgaḥ | atha jaḍasyāpi tadānīṃ sphuraṇāt kutaḥ prati-
niyama: ? jaḍopādānatvādeva grāhyaṃ, tadanyad grāhakamiti | indriyeṇātivyāptiriti cet -
na, sāmagrīsāmarthyādeva nīlasyaiva vedyatvenotpatteḥ |
sahabhāvitayānyonyamupakāraviyogitā |
tādātmyavyativṛttiśca yuvayorubhayorapi ||
atha prakāśotpatteḥ sādhāraṇatvadoṣa iti cet ? vedyatvenotpattirna prakāśatvena |
kimidaṃ vedyatvamiti cet ? svasaṃviditayoḥ kimidaṃ parasparavedanamiti samānam | atha na
vedyatvaṃ prakāśotpatteranyaditi cet ? tathāpi sādhāraṇatvaṃ sāmagrībalādeva parihariṣyate |
athaikarūpatvād vastuno nīlatvavat prakāśenāprakāśenāpi nanvasādhāraṇena abhūtvā sthātuma-
śakyam | śakyameva sāmagrībalāditi tūṣṇīkāmāsyatām |jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalo
atha pramāṇavyāhato'yamarthaṃ iti ka sāmagrayāḥ śaktirupanīyatām ? yasta
tadavatāramapi nāpekṣate svarūpanirūpaṇe svayameva parigalati, tatra kathamupādānābhedanirdeśa: ?
na hi dvayoḥ prakāśayorutpannayo rekenānyaḥ prakāśyate, ekasyānya: pratibhāti, ekasmin veti
kācidarthasaṅgatiḥ | yathā hi pradīpasya svaprakāśaḥ kathañcid vidito jñāne tadanusāreṇānu-
gamyate, tathā na pradīpānāmanyonyaprakāśatāpi kācidupalabdhā, tato yathā dīpena dīpāntaraṃ
prakāśitamiti viplavastathā jñānena jñānāntaramiti | tat kasminnarthe ekopādānamuttaramastu ?
etena svasya vedanamityayogavyacchedasyāpi nāpahnava evātivyāptiparihāraścet sulabha
ityapi nirastam, paravedanārthasyaivāpratiṣṭhānāt |
paraprakāśo'pi dṛṣṭa iti cet ? so'pyaprakāśopādānasya prakāśakṣaṇāntarajanana-
dvāreṇetyanavasara eva jñānadīpādiṣu | yastu tatrāpi sahabhāvinamālokaṃ paṭasya prakāśaka -
micchati so'pi na lokādhyavasāyamātreṇa tattvavyavastheti idamasyeti vyavasthā[90b]-
nibandhanānumāne yadi tajjñānajananamāśrayet tat tarhi jñānena sahabhuvārthasya prakāśana svīkāre
nāstīti duḥsthā vyavasthā athehāpi pṛṣṭhajavikalpajñānāpekṣayā sāmyam ? tahīṃdameva
grāhakaṃ na pūrvakam | idantvabhinnakālamiti sautrāntikamatāvatāraḥ |.
atha nālokasya jñāna janane'pi tāvatā prakāśakatvam, jñānamapi sahabhāvyeva, kiṃtu
sāmagrītaḥ sahotpattimātreṇa, tarhi tadātanendriyāṇyapi prakāśakāni prasajyeran, teṣāma-
prakāśarūpatvāditi cet ? prakāśo'pi prakāśa evāstu, prakāśakastu katham ? na hi pītasya
sahabhāvamātreṇa nolaṃ pītakaṃ bhavitumarhati | tasmānnākiñcitkaraṃ kasyacit saṃbandhapaddhati -
madhyāste | kāraṇopakāradvāreṇa tu pradīpo'prakāśasvabhāve ghaṭādau dṛṣṭaḥ tadvyavahārabhāk,
tatastajjñānasya jñānāntaraṃ prakāśamiti gamyamānaikopādānabhāve na ṣaṣṭhīṃ prayuñjīta nāma |
na punaradhyakṣatāpekṣayā, caitrasya maitra: sundara ityatra yathā gamyamānasaudaryatāpekṣayā,
na tu
saundaryāpekṣayādhyakṣatā, saundaryayorekātmaniṣṭhatvāt |
naivaṃ kaścit prayuṃkta iti cet ? yadi paribhāvakaḥ syāt tadapi kathaṃ prayuñjīta,
samānatvāt nyāyasya ? tadasyāndhadugdhanyāyena grahaṇe gatametad grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇavaidhurya-
dvāreṇādvayasādhanaṃ nyāyanāyakasya | na cāyaṃ nyāyaḥ tat kimanena vārtikakāradveṣāt
śubhaguptajuṣṭaloṭanena ? anekapradīpavadeva tarhi saṃvidaḥ sahitāḥ pratibhānti bhinnāśceti
vedanenāpi ko'rtha iti cet —na, vyatiriktapratipatryapekṣayā hi sahitāḥ prakāśanta iti
vyavahāraḥ | nanu tadabhāve'pi sahitānāṃ prakāśanaṃ na kṣīṇam | evametat | na tu
sākārasiddhiśāstram
eko'pyanyasya prakāśa ityasti | svasvaprakāśarūpatā punarayoghaṭīpihitānāmadhyastīti na
prastutasiddhiḥ | tasmādanyonya saṃvidantarbhāva evānyonyavedanavyavahārasiddhiḥ | na hyekadīpa -
prabhavā api parasparaprakāśino dīpā iti vārtāpyasti ||
bhinnā evāṇavastatra jīvaṃ cet sutarāṃ priyam |
kāpyadṛṣṭestathā hetorasādhāraṇatā sphuṭam ||
api ca,
svaprakāśo yathā dīpo dṛṣṭo'nekastathā yadi |
bījābhedānmitho bhāsastatra dṛśyeta sādhvidam ||
tadayamekasāmagrīsaṃbhavo'vyabhicāradvāreṇa kacidekadarśane'nyānumānāya prabhavet,
nānyādhyakṣatvāya, rasarūpādivat | evamekopādānatāpi sajāyīyatāmadhikāṃ prasādhayet,
na svabhāvasaṅkarasādhyamanyaprakāśam | anyathā kacidekamanyasya jaḍamityapi syāditi |
etenābhinnopādānatvameva parasparapratibhāsa ityapi kalpanamapāstam, ekopādānānāṃ
jaḍānāmapi parasparajaḍatvaprasaṅgāt | ātmātmarūpeṇa hi teṣāmapi jaḍatvam, evaṃ
prakāśatvamapi ||
na [9la] rūpajananadvārā yathā vastumati sthitiḥ |
ekopādānabhāvena tathāstu paribhāṣayā ||
yathā hi, sautrāntikasya sarūpajananameva grāhyatvaṃ na tu tasyāpi sphuraṇam,
evamekapratibhāsa evānyapratibhāsaḥ syānna citrapratītiḥ | kiṃ ca, ekopādānatvamapi
śuddhāvadheyametat svapnajāgradavasthayościtrākārasyaiva hetutvāvadhāraṇāt | vyākula-
kāle'pi vikalpasyāne kākā ravivartatvāt, ekavastuvikalpane'pi pradeśabhedenākārasya
citratvāt | puñjāt puñjotpattau cānyatamasyaiva sāmarthyakalpane ca kacidanekasya janakatvaṃ
bhāvābhāvānukāraṃ samānam | vicchinnanīlākārādapi nīlākārodayadarśanāditi
nottaramacitrāt citrotpattivādinaḥ | aśakyasaṃkhyānatvāñcca na nyūnādhikabhāvaḥ | kiṃ
ca vaṭavat,
nyūnādhikatve'pi bhavet kiñcidekamanekakṛt |
na tvekabhāvo nyūnasya bhāve vā citramadvayam ||jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalo
tajjñānaṃ tadvadanyadapi gāḍhasvāpādyavasthānantaraṃ cālayavijñānāt pradeśabhedena
citrādeva citrāntaropattiḥ | astu vā saṃmūcchitākārādekasmāt kadācit kutracit
citrasya krameṇākrameṇa vā bhāvaḥ | yadā tāvat jāgarānantaraṃ yāvatkālamanavaruddho
middhādibhistāvat prathamakṣaṇabhuvo vihāya nāpareṣāṃ parasparamaṃnubhavaḥ syāt, upādāna-
bhedāt | paramparayā tadekaprabodhāditi cet ? yathā yathā tarhi vyavadhānaṃ, tathā tathā
mandatātāratamyādanyo'nyaprakāśapraṇāśaḥ
kiyatāpyantareṇa syāt | citraprakāśā-
vināśaśca jāgarādibhiranekaṃ dinamanubhūyate, nāpi mandatātāratamyam | naivaṃ jñānākāre
śakyamiti cet ? ekākārasaṃvedanena bhinnasya saṃvedanamityapi kathaṃ śakyaṃ yadi nāmo-
pādānābhedaḥ, svagatasyaiva bhedābhedasya prayojakatvāt ? na ca prasaṅge tattvameva, viparyaya-
paryavasāyitvāt |
ki ca,
upādānena saṃbandhādupādeyasya ced grahaḥ |
upādānasya kiṃ neti saṃbandho na prayojakaḥ ||
svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭo hi parasparasya bodhaḥ, tāṃ ca sīmānamatikramya sannikarṣaḥ sva-
prabhāvamādarśayati sa copādānenaiva sārdhaṃ mukhya iti ekasāmagrayadhīnānumānavaddhetupratīti-
dvāraka eva sahabhuvo bhinnasyānubhava: syāt | atītatvānneti cet ? svabhāvakālaviprakaṣayorna
kaścid viśeṣaḥ| athopādānasya dvayamapyetat sahabhuvastu svabhāvaviprakarṣamātram | atra
tarhi sannikṛṣṭatvamapi nikṛṣṭam | upādāne tu prauḍhamiti godhāśaśanyāyaḥ | sannikarṣabalāñca
grahaṇasthitiḥ | athātītasphuraṇe vartamānatvameva syāt, kathamatītatvam ? tato nātīta-
sphūtiḥ | yadīdṛśī tattvadṛṣṭiḥ parasyātmabhūtayā saṃvidā [91b] saṃvedyamānaṃ paraṃ svarūpameva
syāt kathaṃ paravittiḥ ?
tatrānunmīlitākṣasya sannikarṣaghoṣaṇamanyatrāpyastu | yogivad vātītagrahaṇamapi
syāt | evaṃ prabandhapravṛttau pūrvapūrvasarvakṣaṇavīkṣaṇaprasaṅgo yāvadekamupādānamanavadhirvā |
yathā vyavadhitāratamyaṃ tathā sannikarṣaprauḍhitāratamyamiti | evaṃ svopādeyasyāpi prati-
bhāsaprasaṅge sarvaṃ tadvat | api ca yadi citrapratibhāsasya bheda eva tadā nīlapītavannīla-
khaṇḍayorapīti paramāṇuparyantadarśanāt na kiñcidekaṃ saṃviditamasti yasyānyade kopādānaṃ
syādityapratirodhamāndhyamaśeṣasya jagataḥ | na vā kiñcidityetatparyavasāno'yaṃ vādaḥ |
sākārasiddhiśāstram
tad yadīdameva vivakṣitaṃ kimanena phalguvalgitena ? ṛjunā krameṇānekatvamapi bhāvānāṃ
nāstītyetadevocyatām | ākārāṇāmavastutva miṣṭameveti cet ? tathāpi kimanena
dhyāyamasahamānena ?
api ca,
ākārāṇamavastutvānnai kopādānasaṃbhavaḥ |
prakāśamātrasya punarbhedābhāve'pi na kṣatiḥ ||
iti siddhāntaviplavaḥ | tadayamācāryanirapekṣamākhyāyamāno'pyupādānābhedaḥ svabhāvabheda-
manākṣipannaiṣāmākārāṇāṃ parasparānubhavavibhāvanāya prabhavati |
athāpi bheda iṣyeta na mṛṣyeta mitha: prathām |
mitha: prathāyāḥ kṣāntī tu grāhya grāhakatā parā ||
tasmāt,
tat ko'tra paramārtha : ? tathā hi,
dṛśyate tāvadevaṃ cet dṛśyatāṃ kiṃ tvabhedataḥ |
bījasya svātmano veti vicāramidamarhati ||
ekatve citratā'bhāvo nānātve sutarāmayam |
naikatvaṃ nāpi nānātvaṃ buddhīnāmupapattimat ||
ākārā yadi rūpameva manasaścitrāḥ kathaṃ kiṃ nu vā
cetaścitramanekameva yadi tat kunaikyamāsthīyatām |
aṇvākāradharā ca dhīra viṣayo nāpi kṣamā saṃhato
bhāsante ca parasparavyatikaraṃ ko'pyeṣa māyāvidhiḥ ||
idaṃ vastubalāyātaṃ yadvadanti vipaścitaḥ |
yathā yathārthāścintyante viśīryante tathā tathā ||
[pra. vā. 2. 209]
bhāvā yena nirūpyante tadrūpaṃ nāsti tattvataḥ |
yasmādekamakaṃ ca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate ||426
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalo
nāṅgāni dhārayantyete vicāraviṣadūṣitāḥ |
varaṃ hyapekṣitā bhāvāḥ kṛtvā gajanimīlanam ||
iti | svapnamāyāmarīcigandharvanagarapratibhāsavat sarvadharmaṃśūnyataiva nyāyaprāpteti para
mārtha: | nanu bhagavantamadhikṛtya prakrānto vicāraḥ, tat kimīdānīṃ buddho'pi bhagavān
māyopamaḥ svapnopama iti cet ? kasya punaratropālambhaḥ svayameva bhagavatā tathā prathanāt,
sollāsaṃ tadvayāhṛteścāryairudyotanāt, tathatayā ca tathāgatapṛthagjanayoraviśeṣasvīkārādāgamo-
pagītagāmbhīryaudāryaviśeṣādanyatra ? nanu vyāpakānupalabdhibādhitatvāt lakṣaṇādyākārāṇāma-
līkatvāt kaudāryamasatkhyātiprasaṅgaśca ? asatapratibhāsijñānasvabhāvatvena bhrāntatvāt ka
gāmbhīryam ? tadayuktam,
atasmiṃstadgraho bhrāntirbhrāntiranyā [92a] nirākṛtā |
alīkaṃ cānalīkena rūpeṇa na sa paśyati ||
yathā sthitā dharmayaṃ tathā jñānāt tathāgataḥ |
vyavasthāmātrato'pyasya bījābhāvād bhramo na hi ||
yataḥ pravṛttivyāvṛttī vikalpād vāsanābhuvaḥ |
tayoḥ samūlamunmūlānnivikārapadasthitiḥ ||
asatkhyātirmate cātra nāniṣṭābhāsateha yat |
asattattvena tatsarvaṃ na cāstyanyadabādhitam ||
pūrvaṃ vistareṇa nirastatvāt |
athāpi dharmottaramārgasaṅgā-
danaṅgamaṅgīkṛtametadeva |
dakādikākāra viviktamantaḥ
parisphuradduḥkhasukhādi cetaḥ ||
nātra kila bādhakāvatāro deśavitānībhāvāditi | tadapi viplutam | yataḥ,
antaḥ sātādiviṣayaṃ bahiḥ śītādigocaram |
vedanaṃ tattadākāraṃ bādhakagrastameva ca ||
sākārasiddhiśāstram
vyaktiviśeṣameva hi jñānasyākāraṃ vidmaḥ | deśavitānābhāvaśca deśasyālpatvaṃ
vā syādabhāva eva vā ? tatra paramāṇuparimāṇe'pi deśe prasaṅgī doṣaḥ kiyatyalpe prati-
nyeteti na prathamaḥ pakṣa: | dvitīyastu asaṃbhavī saṃbhavinaḥ, saṃbhavinā hi niyamena
kacid bhāvyam | kacidapyabhāve'bhāva eva vibhāvito bhavati | saṃvedyante cāsukha-
saumanasyādayo dehāntastadvahirdeśavyavacchedena sphurantaḥ | anyathā prakāśavannīlādibhiḥ
abhede tadvadeva doṣaḥ |
tatra ca kāye kiyantamabhivyāpya deśamāsata iti kimanena ? kā vā sadeśatā,
rūpe'pi svarūpātirekiṇo deśasaṃjñitasya kacidanupalabdhe: ? nāpyādhāra eva deśo,
vātātapayorapyadeśatāprasakteḥ | na ca tadapekṣayā bādhaka pravṛttiḥ, kiṃ tu svarūpāpekṣayā |
svarūpaṃ ca niraṅgamapi kalpanābuddhau yathā vyatiriktairiva dharmāntaraiḥ parikaritamābhāti,
tathā ihedamiti kālākāravimarśapratyanīkapratyayakalpito nabhogatipratidvandvīva deśo
na nāma vyavahāramavatarati | na ceyaṃ gatirantaḥ sukhasaumanasyādivedane duravartinī
sparśāntavadityuktaprāyam | atha yathā nīlādau viśadatarordhvādharādibhāgatvaṃ vitastiḥ
hastahastipuruṣādiparimāṇaparicchedyatvaṃ copalabhyate, na tathā sukhādiṣviti matiḥ, tataḥ
ki deśavattāmātraparijñāne ? evaṃ hyasparśanendriyagandharasadhvaniprabhṛtīnāmapyadeśatāprasaṅgaḥ |
na ca parokṣe vahnayādāvapi pratiniyatadeśatādi śakyam |
atha yatra phale gandharasasaṃbhavastāvati vartamānau niyatadeśāvūhituṃ śakyau, para-
pūrvādibhāgena ca grahaṇakāle cendriyaśeṣaparimāṇeneti cet ? sukhādyapi dehāntargaṃtā-
[bhogā]ddeśaparimāṇena kiṃ na śakyaṃ pratipattum ? avyāptistu phale gandharasayorupalabdhā |
bhoktuniyata deśopalambha iti cet ? so'pi sthūlagrāhī nāṇuśa: pratiniyamena deśamava-
sātuṃ śaktaḥ | tasmādatra tāvad vartate kiyantamapi deśamabhi [92b] vyāpyeti samānam |
evaṃ grahaṇakāle'pīndriyadeśaparimityasya pratiniyamaniścaya eva | sukhāderapi vā sa eva
nyāyo darśanaśravaṇajanitasyāpi | apriyāvalokana taptaṃ hi locanameva priyadarśane śītalī-
bhavadanubhūyate | kharāṃśutaptasya taḍāgāvagāhane tu vyaktaḥ parimāṇaviśeṣa ūrdhvādhara-
bhāgo vā | anyadeśodayasya tatrāropakalpane'pi sa eva deśa: syāt | parimāṇaniyamo
bhūmiṣu bhūbhujāmucitaḥ | idameva ca nṛsukhaṃ yacchābdaṃ saṃvedanamiti na bhinnasiddhiḥ,
spaṣṭapratibhāsād vā | saumanasyasya tu mānasatvādaspaṣṭapratibhāse'pi tadanusāreṇa428
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau
saṃbhavina ihaiva kacid deśa iti sāmānyena siddherapratibandhāt | nāpi nirbandha:
tatropayogī, sādhyasyāpi vikalpakatvaprasaṅgāt |
kiṃ ca parimāṇaniyamānavadhāraṇe yadi deśavattāniṣedhaḥ kacit kālavattā
tu sarvasya mā bhūt kṣaṇasya parimāṇenāvadhārayitumaśakyatvāt | kevalaṃ pūrvaṃ nāsīt
pañcāñca na bhavatīti pratiniyatakālatāmupasthāpayati sthavīyasī buddhiḥ | ihāpi na
bahirdehādihaiva tu saumanasyādīti niścayaḥ sthita eva | kiṃ ca, kālayogastāvadiṣṭa
eva saumanasyādeḥ, anyathā kadāpyabhavataḥ sādhvī bādhakayuktiḥ, sa eva ca deśavattā-
mupanayati, kacidabhavataḥ kadācid bhāvayogāt | yatraiva cāsti sa eva deśaḥ, satu
sthūlaḥ sūkṣmo veti kimanena ? kāle tu prayojanāntarāpekṣayā niyamasthāpanamiti ||
yathā niyatakālatā niyatadeśataivaṃ sphuṭā,
pradeśaniyamastvasāvaṇutayādhimātreṇa vā |
dvidhāpi tu na bādhakavyuparatiḥ sukhāṃdāvato
nirākṛtagirā kṛtaṃ kimu viśeṣaparākṛteḥ ||
tadevaṃ sattāmātrānubandhinī kālavatteva deśavattā na kacid vyāpakānupalambha-
saṃbhavaṃ bhayamanavakāśayituṃ śaknoti maivaṃ vā svayamapi sattāvyavahārasiddhiḥ kathaṃ
sukhādau ?
ekāneka vivekāsiddhiyaṃdvadasya bhavato'pi na siddhiḥ |
eketarayoranyatarasya svavido mita iva dhāma nirasya ||
yathā hi, nīlasyeva puro'vasthitākārasya sukhāderapratibhāsanāt ekānekarūpa-
vyatirekaḥ pratipattumaśakyaḥ, tathā tata eva tayoranyatarasaṃbhavo'pi puraḥsphuratyevedamekamanekaṃ
veti nirūpaṇopalabdheḥ| parokṣe'pi darśanānusāreṇa tathā vyavasthāyām apuraḥsphuratyapi
rūpe puraḥsphuradvapānusāreṇa deśapratiniyamāttigmabhaṅgajāgnikaṇikādivattayorabhāvo'pi
vyavasthāpyatām |
satā avaśyamekadhā bhāvyamiti cet - na, vyāpakatvāt tayoranyatarasandehe
sattvasyaiva sandehāt | svasaṃvedanasya tu śakti śvetādivadeva dūrīkuru mā tatpratyāśayā
sthāḥ | na ca pramāṇāntaramastīti parasya sandigdhāsiddhimudbhāvayato'pi na svayaṃ sad-
vyavahāraḥ | sādhakabādhakavedhurye [93a] sandehasya nyāyaprāptatvāt | svasaṃvidite ca
sākārasiddhiśāstram
nīlādijñānasvarūparāśau bādhādarśanameva balavad bījamasya | tata eva tarhi bhavatu
svasaṃvido'prāmāṇyam, bādhāyā abhāve tu prāmāṇyamiti cet - naivam, adarśana-
mātreṇābhāvasiddheḥ | bahiḥ samastamabhyastamabādhakasya ca sādhakasaṃbhavānnāparo dṛśyānupa-
lambhaḥ | śāstra eva tu cintito'yamabādhavāda ityāstāṃ tāvat |
vedotpādyakathādīnāmapi caivaṃ pramāṇatā |
utsargasiddhaṃ mānatvamityapi grastamagrimaiḥ ||
svato yatrāpi mānatvaṃ tadabhyāsaphalaṃ viduḥ |
bahiḥ samastamabhyastamasadantastu cintyate ||
nanu grāhakākārabalādalīkasyāpi grāhyākārarāśeravabhāsa ityaśakyāpahnavaḥ
sukhādiriti cet - na,
svaprakāśasvabhāvatvād bhāgayorubhayorapi |
kiṃ grāhyaṃ grāhi vā kiṃ syānna cānyenānyabhāsanam ||
iti bahiradūṣaṇe prā[geva] nirūpaṇāt | na cābhimānamātrād vastusthitiriti | kiṃ
cātra mate duḥkhādivannirākārajñānarūpatayā,
rāgadveṣamohamānādinikhilakleśagaṇa: sahajo yadi |
iṣṭāniṣṭatayā ca vibhāgaḥ kaḥ sākāramate'ṅga virāgaḥ ||
ālokākārayogo hi bhrāntirbhavatām | tadabhāvādavidyādayaḥ svabhāva eva bhava -
bhājāṃ bhaveyuḥ, ālambanadvāreṇālīkatve sukhāderapi prasaṅgāt | tato'niṣṭatayā hāna-
mupādānamanyathā keṣāñciditi sākārapakṣa evākṣarāntareṇoktaḥ | ākāracakraikadeśadṛśya-
spṛśyaparyavasānaṃ tu vaimatyamiti na kiñcidetat | yathā bhrāntitve'pyaniṣṭatayā kasyacit
tyāgaḥ tathālokatve'poṣṭatayā ākāraviśeṣasya sthitirastviti sādhyakṣatiḥ | caittāścaite
sukhādaya iṣyante, cittaṃ viṣayagrāhitayā ākārasvarūpaṃ heyam, caittaṃ cāvasthāyīti
nāyaṃ saṃprayuktadharma ityāgamavirodhaḥ | abhede ca cittavadevālīkatvaṃ teṣāṃ tadvad vā
cittasyāpi satyateti kathamanākārasya sādhyasya siddhiḥ ?
nanu yad yathā bhāvyate tat tathā sphuṭībhavatīti vyomākāramapi cittaṃ bhāvya-
mānaṃ tathā sphuṭībhaviṣyati, prasiddhākāravirahācca nirākāraṃ tadeveti kathaṃ sādhyasiddhi: ?
na, prayojanābhāvāt,430
jñānaśrī mitranibandhāvalau

nanu saṃbhogakāyo'yamiṣṭa evārhatāṃ sutaiḥ |
dharmakāyasya lābhecchurbhajed vyomopamaṃ vapuḥ ||
iti cet ? tattarhi na tāvat sādhyaṃ yathokta evecchāparisamāpteḥ | nāpi sādhanaṃ

payaṃnte svayamapi prakarṣaparyantavartinyeva syāt, kathaṃ tato vicchidyeta, anyato vā

tadvadeveti saṃbandhaḥ |
na so'sti kaścit samayaprakāro

nāparaṃ vastu cāstīha sarvagrāsā hi śūnyatā ||
sākārasiddhiśāstram

śrāvakādimārgo na tadukta: ? atra ca yasyāpi heyatayā nirdeśaḥ tasyāpi nājñatayā

jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalau
iti | tatrākiñcanādiviśeṣaṇaṃ vyomta eva rajonohārādādikṛtasya nimno[94a]nnatasya

karaṇyaṃ bādhaka bahuvacana nirdeśayatnāt | sugate tu bhagavati yathoktākāre evāpavādasamāropa-

bādhyabādhakabhāvasya
api ca, na tāvajjñānamātmānameva bādhate, svarūpasaṃvedanasyaiva balavattvāt |
pareṇāpi tadviṣayeṇa bhinnaviṣayeṇa vā bādhā syāt, samakālenāsamakālena vā ? tatra tadviṣayaṃ
tacca bādhata iti asaṃbaddham | bhinnaviṣayeṇāpi tasya kīdṛśī bādhā ? svaviṣayopasthāpana-
mātrāccet ? tenaivāsya kiṃ na bādhā ? na ca samasamayena | ekakālamanekasya sajātīyasya
vijātīyasya vā pratibhāse kasya kena bādhā ? kālabhede tu sutarāmanavakāśo mahāsaṃmata-
śrīharṣayorapi prasaṅgāt |
athaikasya jñānasya jñānāntareṇa nirviṣayatvapratipādanaṃ bādhārthaḥ sa ca bhinnakāla-
yorna virudhyate | so'rthastatra jñāne yadi pratibhāsate, tadā sanneveti kuto bādhā ?
apratibhāse tu svayamevāsan ki niṣedhāntareṇa ? na vā tadviṣayaṃ bādhanamuktaṃ bhavati |
āropitasya niṣedha iti cet ? āropo'pi vyavahāramātrasiddha iti pratipādanāt,
tadāśrayā bādhāpi na sāṃvṛtamatikrāmati | atha yathaiva pratītyasamutpādabhe [95b]dasamā-
śrayeṇa jñānāntaraprasavamātralakṣaṇo bhramaḥ, tathaivaivametannānyathetyapi jñānākārodaya eva
bādhā bhaviṣyati |
yadyevaṃ tattvatto na bādheti siddhametat | kenacidākāraparigraheṇa jñānamidaṃ jātaṃ
nāma, na tu kiñcidanena bādhitaṃ sādhitaṃ vā, nīlajñānānantaraṃ madhurajñānavat | anyatra
bādhādhyavasāyena viśeṣa iti cet ? adhyavasāyamātrasiddha ityeva sāṃvṛta ucyate |
tasmānnālambanaśūnyatāpratipādanaṃ bādhārthaḥ | ki ca, sālambanetarabhedena dvaite gatiriyaṃ
syādapi | advaite tu svarūpamātraparyaṃva sitavedana sthitīnāṃ matīnāmanyo'nyaṃ bādha iti

siddhidhiyaḥ paradhiyo na yathā tathā na bādhāpi
iti | nanu vijñaptimātratāsiddhirapi parata eva tathā bādhāpi bhaviṣyatīti cet ?
asārametat | saṃvṛtivyavasthito hi nānumānamanāsthāya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ, anyathā na
kacit pravṛttinivṛttyādikamācaret | anumānāśraye ca balādvijñaptimātratāsiddhi-
rāpatati | na tu tattvapariniṣṭhāyāmanumānāvakāśaḥ | tathā yadi saṃvṛtāveva bādhasvīkāraḥ,
tadā punaḥ pratibhāsamānametat bahiravasitamiti bādhastatraiva syāt | yatkiñcidetat
buddhirjaḍaṃ vā tatraiva bādhasiddhiḥ, tadāpi na bāhyarūpātikrameṇa sādhanavṛttiḥ | atha kimatra
vikalpena buddhirūpameva citramālambya dharmīkaraṇamiti na bāhye sādhanavyāpāraḥ |
tadetadaśvārūḍhāśvavismaraṇavṛttāntamanuharati ||
vedanaṃ kiñciduddiśya yad bāhyaṃ bāhyameva tat |
taca jñānaṃ jaḍaṃ vā syāditi cintā nirathikā ||
sarvathā bāhyagrāhyavyavasthānāntarīyako bādhaka iti siddham |
nanvetadeva nīlādibādhāyā viṣayo mataḥ |
tacca jñānaṃ jaḍaṃ vā syāditi cintā nirarthikā ||
na ca tatra dhiyo rūpamiti bhītiḥ prabādhituḥ |
nāpi paścāt tathā jñāne śakterutkīlanaṃ bhavet ||
bāhya grāhyavyavasthāyā vyapekṣāniyamo na ca |
idaṃ hi bādhitaṃ nīlaṃ bahirastu mano'stu vā ||
astu vā tadvayavasthāpi tathāpyetasya bādhanam |
vairabuddhayā na kiṃ bandhoḥ prahāro maraṇapradaḥ ||
iti cet ? punarapi brūmaḥ na vijñaptimātratāsiddhau bādhakāvakāśa iti prakṛtam | tatra
grāhya grāhakavyavasthā nāntarīyake bādhake sidhyati nāniṣṭamāpāditaṃ bhavati, yathā hi
tasyā viplavastathā bādhakasyeti sādhyasiddheḥ | na ca tannāntarīyakatāparihāra: śakyaḥ |
na cāviṣayīkṛtasya bādhaḥ, idamanena bādhyata iti bādhādhyavasāyāt | viṣayīkaraṇaṃ
ca bādhyasya bādhakādanyena, bādhake[netareṇa] svayaṃ svapareṇa veti vikalpāḥ | bādhakād
sākāra siddhiśāstram
anyena viṣayīkaraṇe tāvadabādhyameva | bādhakenāpi viṣayīkaraṇe ka bādhakāvakāśaḥ,
viṣayīkaraṇasya svarūpanirbhāsa [96a] tvāt ? bādhyamānatvenaiva svarūpasya nirbhāsa iti
cet ? vyāhatametat | svarūpanirbhāsa iti svarūpasattvaṃ, bādhyamānatā cāsattvam |
krameṇa dvayamapīti cet ? na tāvat prathamaṃ bādhā, saṃbandhino'pratīteḥ | atha svarūpa -
nirbhāsastadā tāvataiva sattvākṛṣṭe: ka bādhā ? na khalu kālāntare bhavantyapi tasyāḥ
syāt, tadā tasya svayamevābhāvāt | bhāve vā bādhakaśatenāpi na kiñcit | ubhayena
tu viṣayīkaraṇe saṃvādasiddhireva ka bādhāgandhaḥ ? na ca tena
vānyena vānyasya
viṣayīkaraṇaṃ nāmopapattimat, vijñānasiddhau cintāyāḥ prārabdhatvāt | nāpi svayameva
viṣayīkaraṇe bādhāvakāśinī,
svayaṃ nirbhāsamānasya pareṇa viṣayīkṛtau |
bādhakenātmano mūrddhā bādhitavyo balīyasā ||
tataśca nīlamidaṃ bādhitaṃ mayānayā yuktyeti svākāramātra paryavasāyivyāpāro
vikalpastasya vārtāmapi na spṛśati bhede, abhede'pi tamātmānameva bādhata iti sāhasam |
svaparavedane ca pūrvavat saṃvāda eva | aviṣayīkṛtasya tu bādhane'tiprasaṅgaḥ bāhyagrahādhi-
muktau tu tadasparśinyapi jñānodaye tatsiddhabādhavyavahāra iti syāt pratyāśā | sa
cādhimokṣe viplava iti tatkṛtā bādhāpi viplava eva | bāhyagrahavyavasthāparibhave hi
svasaṃvedanamagnamaśeṣamiti kasya kena kiṃ kriyā syāt ? na hi tadāpīdamevamiti śakyaṃ
kartum | tathā sati punadvaitaprāpteḥ | yadāhuḥ,
vijñānamātramevedamityapi hyupalambhataḥ |
sthāpayannagrataḥ kiñcittanmātre nāvatiṣṭhate ||
iti | atha tattvaniścaye'pyasākṣātkaraṇāvasthasya pravṛtyādivad bādhakamapyavakāśeteti
cet ? tathāpi na doṣaḥ | yathā hīdamato vedyaṃ prāpyaṃ veti sahajāvidyayā bahiradhikāre-
jaiva pravṛttyādiḥ, tathā bādho'pi tanmūrdhanyeva nipatet | vinmātracintāyāṃ punaḥ sarva-
vyāpāroparamaḥ | tadayaṃ bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ sāṃvṛta eva, na tattvarūpāmukhīkaraṇakāle
avakāśamāsādayati | tadā ca kāmaṃ sādhanasyāpi nāvatāraḥ, kevalamanavatāro'pyasya
na bādhate, sādhyasya siddhatvāt |jñānaśrīmitranibandhāvalī
tadasiddhāvitarasyānavatāra : paraparitoṣādanyatra kamarthaṃ puṣṇāti ? yadi tarhi
tatsādhakapramāṇavṛttimapekṣya bādhakaprayogaḥ, tadaiṣa doṣaḥ | kaḥ punarevaṃ vilambiṣyate ?
prathamata eva bādhakaprayogo'stu | bhautācamanamātrametat | yadā hi vijñaptimātratā-
pratīto nāsyāvatāra iti siddham tadā tadātmatāvirahamapekṣyeva tatprayoga iti
tannirūpaṇāpekṣāyāṃ prakāśatayaiva vijñānatāsiddhau vidhūto bādhakāvatāraḥ, bhavan vā yadi
nedaṃ vijñānamityanenākāreṇa bhavet | tasmād yāvad bādhastāvad bahirātmanyeva na
vijñānarūpa iti siddham | kaḥ punarevaṃ sādhanadoṣa iti cet na, vijñaptimātratā siddhau
anumānasyaivo[96b]tthānābhāvāt ka sādhanadūṣaṇāvakāśa: ? tathā hi,
bahirbodhe'numānādi mānaṃ na svaikasa vidi |
svaikasaṃvitprasiddha tu tadgrahādeva tadbhavaḥ ||
tathāpi yadi doṣoktyā santoṣaḥ,
asiddheḥ pararūpasya dharmihetusvarūpayoḥ |
na siddhirnāpi ca vyāptiriti kiṃ vā na dūṣaṇam ||
kiṃ ca, ayaṃ vyāpakānupalambho'nyo vā bādhako vicārādināmā nānumānāt
anyaḥ saṃbhāvanāviṣayaḥ | sarvaṃ hi vivādarūḍhasya vacanamāvirbhāvitasādhyasādhanadṛṣṭāntāditayā
nānumānamanākṣipya prakṛtopayogi bhavitumarhati | ataeva saṃvṛtāvavaśyaṃ pramāṇasvīkāra
ityadvaitabindī darśitamasmāmiḥ |
anyathā yathā tathānuvādamātreṇa kasya kīdṛgarthasiddhi : ? na cānumāna-
madhyakṣamadhikṣipya yathārthaṃ bhavitumarhati saṃbandhagrahaṇādī paramparayāpi niyatopayogitayā
tenaiva janyatvāt | tadapyatadapramāṇane pramāṇamiti janayiturakulīnatāyāṃ kulīnatā-
śaṃsanametat | svarūpe caitadākāravedanaṃ dūrīkṛtabhrāntikalpanatayā pratyakṣamiti kuto

sākārasiddhiśāstram
atha vijñaptisādhanakāle kathaṃ svayonipratyakṣaparibhava iti cet - na, sādhya-
siddhau svasyāpi paribhavāt |
dahati drumamāśrayāśano
nijaśākhāṃpugaghṛṣṭijo yathā |
paravittirapītthamātmano
yadi hantrī ka ihāparādhyatu |
na khalu vijñaptisādhanaṃ paravedanamaparaṃ bādhamānamātmanaḥ prāmāṇyamāśaṃsati | paravedana-
sāmānyena tu tathotthāpito vicāraḥ, vahniryathā sarvasyaiva dāhaka iti naikasya kasyacit
aparādha: | vyāpakānupalambhastu prāyakṣaparibhavenaiva prāmāṇyamākāṃkṣatīti na nyāyaḥ |
vijñaptisādhanasya tu paravedanāntaraprāmāṇyāvadhikameva prāmāṇyam | yadā punararthakriyā-
śaktipratītivyavahṛtasattākastasyāvimarśenādarśanānna tathā vyavaharati, na tadā vyāpakā-
nupalabdheraparādhaḥ, svayamabādhanāt, paratastu samānatvāt daṇḍasya | na hi svasaṃvedane
śaktipratibhāsaḥ | yadā tu vyāpakānupalambha eva nāyakastadā pratyakṣāntarasyāpi na
prāmāṇyamupahantuṃ śaktaḥ, prāgeva svasaṃvedanasya jātyaiva dūrīkṛtabhrāntivikalpaśaṅkā-
kalaṅkasya | tasmānna saṃvedanarakṣitasya kṣatiḥ kutaścit |
nanu,
aprāmāṇye yathākṣasya nānumāyā: pramāṇatā |
tathānumānāprāmāṇye nākṣasyetyapi śakyate ||
tadgṛhītāṅgato liṅgājjātānumitidūṣaṇe |
tasyaiva doṣo'doṣe hi kiṃ kṛtaṃ tajjadūṣaṇam ||
tato yadyubhayasyāpi prāmāṇyam, tathāpi

jñānaśrī mitra nibandhāvalī
tadapi naupathikam | vyāpakānupalambhasya hi paravedanaikaniyatasya vyāptyādigrāhiṇā
paravedanenaiva pratyakṣeṇa samakakṣatā bhavatu, yata ekaprāmāṇyasvīkāranāntarīyakamapara-
prāmāṇyam | svasaṃvedanaṃ tu dvayorapyāśrayaḥ savayānāśrayaṃ ceti kastena saha tulārohaḥ ?
viṣayabhedācca parokṣaviṣayatvādanumānasya, pratyakṣe tadanavatārāt ka balābalacintāvakāśaḥ ?
ataeva pratyakṣādibhiranirākṛtaḥ pakṣa ākhyātaḥ |
nanu pratyakṣe'pi svabhāvāntaramavyavahṛtaṃ vyavahārayitumanumānamanumatameva |
na ca pratibhāsina eva kacid vidhiniṣedho vā | pratibhāsamāne hi śṛṅgalāṅgulādi-
sanniveśaviśeṣe gavādiśabda pravartanam kacit kevalabhūtalopalambhe kumbhādiniṣedha-
vyavahāraḥ | jñānagatacandradvayākāre cābahirinduyugalasya | na tu pratibhāsināmeva vidhi-
niṣedhau | tathehāpi niṣedhaprastāve pratibhāsino nīlādyākārasya yāvantaḥ kalpitā dharmā
niṣidhyante, tāvanto niṣidhyantām | yathātmaparagrāhya grāhakajñāpyajñāpaka nityakṣaṇikai-
kānekatvādayo dravyaguṇatriguṇīmayatvādayo vā sparśādilakṣaṇarūpāntarasahacāraparamāṇu-
rūpatārthakriyāśaktiparyantāḥ prapañcaśabdavācyāḥ, sarveṣāṃ kalpitamātratvāt | tasmāt
prakāśamāne dharmiṇi dharmāntarasyāpratibhāsina eva niṣedho vidhirvā vyavahāramāśritya,
śabdādivyavahāravirahe'pi tadyogye'pi tadyogyatāyāḥ parokṣarūpatvāt | na tu pratibhāsinaḥ
kacinniṣedhaḥ | yadāha nyāyaprasūtiḥ,
iti |
tasmin bhāvānupādāne sādhye'syānupalambhanam |
tathā heturna tasyaivābhāvaḥ [ śabdaprayogataḥ ] ||
vyasto he toranāśrayaḥ |

iti ca | yadi tarhi pratibhāsino vidhiniṣedhau vyarthāsamarthau apratibhāsino'pi sa
eva niṣedha ityasamarthavyarthī ka tarhi śabdavyāpāra : ? na kacit tatvataḥ, pratītya-
samutpādāśrayavyavahāramātrametat śabdena kiñcid vidhīyate niṣidhyate veti | yathā
hi vṛkṣo'stīti saṃketavaśāt tadanurūpapravṛttyākṣepaparikalpotpādanameva śabdena vṛkṣasattā-

sākārasiddhiśāstram
vidhiḥ, tathā vṛkṣo nāstīti tarthivyāvṛttyākṣepakavikalpotpādanameva tanniṣedhaḥ, nañastyora-
prayoge tu kevalaṃ vṛkṣaśabdasya pravṛttinivṛttyasamarthaśā[khā] dimadākāravikalpotpādanameva
vidhiniṣedhākaraṇaṃ nāma | tasya cāstipadasannidhau sa eva śākhī sattayopacīyamāna iva
pratibhātīti pūrvāpekṣayā ākāraviśeṣollekhamātram | nañyogepyapacoyamāna iveti vidhyanu-
bhavāpekṣayā kṣīṇākāro[97b]llekha eva | tatastadanurūpapravṛttyādiḥ |
evaṃ liṅge'pi vikalpavivartino vardhūmajaladarśanādau, saṃvādaniyametarābhyāṃ tu
viśeṣaḥ | tathā ca na sphurato buddhyākārasya kacid vidhiniṣedhau | nāpi bāhyasyāsphurataḥ
sato'sato vā tattvataḥ | tathāpi vikalpodayadvāreṇa tu bāhyasyaiva vidhiniṣedhavyavahāraḥ kevalaṃ
kalpitasya, puraḥ parisphurato nañśatairapi niṣedhābhāvāt | kalpanaṃ ca bahirmukhaparāmarśādinyat,
tarumātra vikalpe sadasattānirṇayāvadhānāvasthākṣepāt | ataevākāro bahīrūpatayā ropitaḥ
śabdavācyo'poha iti cocyate, śābde jñāne tasyaiva pratibhāsāt | adhyavasāyāttu vijāti-
vyāvṛttaṃ bahiriti niveditaṃ prāk | tasmāt,
nākārasya na bāhyasya tattvataḥ pratiṣedhanam |
bahireva hi saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛttyāpi tu nākṛteḥ ||
tathā anarthatvāt, prakṛtyā ca bahirmukhatvāllokasya | yadā ca bāhye'pi parisphurati
nāvakāśo niṣedhasya, kutaḥ svātmani ? tasmāt,
na pramāṇapratikṣipte hetubhistrāṇasaṃbhavaḥ |
svasaṃvityā ca yat siddhaṃ tattvataḥ siddhameva tat ||
yadyapi sāṃvṛta eva sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ tathāpi satsaṃvṛtisamāśraya evaṃ kartavyaḥ | prati-
puruṣaṃ hi bhinnabhinnasādhanādivyavasthitau sarvaṃ sarvasya sidhyet | na ca samayāntara-
sthāyino'pi bādhite hetubhistrāṇavārtā | svasaṃvedane yadi paraṃ pareṣāṃ vimatiḥ,
tatra ca,
na svavitti vinākṛtya pramāṇairjīvituṃ kṣamam |
viśveneva pramāpāye śāstre nirṇītameva tat ||
